# EstreGenesis Changelog

Each tier (Master / Lite / Compact) has its own version. Master is the authoritative evolution track; Lite and Compact are derived regularly from Master but may lag by a release.

This file is the **changelog SSoT** вҖ” each seed file keeps only a compact header metadata line with tier, language, current version, counterpart, and a pointer back to this `CHANGELOG.md`, not the target project's README. When you upgrade a project using Migration B, the agent uses the seed header version marker plus this changelog to compute the delta.

**Language**: **English** (below) В· [н•ңкөӯм–ҙ](#н•ңкөӯм–ҙ)

---

<a id="english"></a>

## Changelog (English)

- **v2.5.93** (2026-06-13) вҖ” **Constellation v2.4.23 вҖ” PreCompact hook schema fix** вҖ” the compact-survival pipeline's `pre-compact-snapshot.cjs` (shipped v2.4.14) emitted `hookSpecificOutput:{hookEventName:'PreCompact', additionalContext:вҖҰ}`, which fails the host hook-output schema on every compaction вҖ” the schema reserves `additionalContext` for UserPromptSubmit/PostToolUse/Stop-family events and PreCompact has no such channel, so the environment snapshot silently went stale. Post-compaction re-injection is already owned by the SessionStart(matcher:"compact") hook that re-reads the whole handoff file, so the PreCompact half only needs to write the snapshot: it now writes the file and exits with a schema-valid `{suppressOutput:true}` (confirmation routed to stderr). Both the shipped reference (`constellation/reference/runtime/pre-compact/`) and this workspace's active hook fixed. Caught live when a manual `/compact` surfaced the validation error. **No wire change**. verify-nway 10-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.92** (2026-06-13) вҖ” **Constellation v2.4.22 вҖ” dashboard dead-code prune (setupWsCollab removed)** вҖ” a `/roundnext` round's small-ripe pickup. `setupWsCollab` (50 lines) had been unwired since the v2.4.2 key-issuance unification folded its рҹ”— button into `setupWsKeyMgmt`; the E2b rough-tier verification (146-symbol sweep) confirmed it as genuine dead code (defined, never invoked вҖ” the only "call site" was the removal comment itself). Removed from the reference dashboard with a one-line tombstone comment; the `ws-collab-invite.eux` provenance note updated from "is dead code" to "removed @ v2.4.22". Round companions (no version surface): the tracked done-`id` standardization question closed by verification вҖ” `state-schema.md В§2` already lists `id` as optional for `done` entries, so the worker's original "non-canonical field" caution was over-strict and no schema change is needed; two planned items re-classified to honest blocked form (Ultrasafe evidence is gated on the self-dogfood decision; the multigroup schema expansion is gated on the recorded "enter on limit signals" decision); the two hub-side blockers escalated to В§13.20 tier 2 (explicit reminder + ETA query, findings attached). **No wire change**. verify-nway 10-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.91** (2026-06-13) вҖ” **Hyperbrief v0.7.0 вҖ” post-response tone-estimate Stop hook (deferred candidate #5 landed)** вҖ” track в‘ў, the last of the three user-approved feedback tracks. The v0.6 triage deferred #5 ("hook post-response tone evaluation layer") on "needs a PostResponse hook spec to stabilize"; a blocker drill proved the host's **Stop hook is the PostResponse equivalent** (officially documented lifecycle + block capability + battle-tested in this workspace every turn), and the triage's "hooks are only PreToolUse+Stop" premise was itself stale. Landed as an extension of the existing В§11.4 hook tier вҖ” not a new architectural layer: **(1) `hooks/tone-estimate.cjs`** (Stop, advise mode, exit 0 always) вҖ” armed only while `.hyperbrief/active-profile.json` exists; extracts the last assistant text from the transcript and re-runs the renderer's deterministic 6-heuristic `estimateSurfaceProfile` (now re-exported from mini-engine, additive) against the declared profile; |О”| вүҘ 2 on any axis (renderer-consistent threshold) emits ONE advisory suggesting the В§5.6.7 fallback re-render; repeat advisories suppressed per decision_id + gap signature (В§2.4 alert-fatigue), 24h TTL backstop. **(2) Skill MUST-20** вҖ” at IR-emit time the skill also writes the active-profile file (decision_id + declared tone), arming the hook; deleting it closes the cycle. **(3) Spec**: В§5.6.7-pre gains the post-response tier paragraph; В§11.4 hook contract gains the tone line. End-to-end verified: gap-advise fires (declared L1.1.1 vs technical-register text вҶ’ audience L1вҶ’L5 flagged), repeat run silent, unarmed run silent. Zero cost on every non-brief turn. **No wire change**. verify-nway 10-axis PASS (docs-badge axis also expanded this session to all 5 modules вҖ” caught and fixed 2 more stale hero badges).
- **v2.5.90** (2026-06-13) вҖ” **Greatpractice v0.3.1 вҖ” micro-tier first decomposition (mezzo 9 вҶ’ 20 atoms)** вҖ” the user-approved track в‘Ў cut. Every mezzo entry now carries its executable atoms: two per mezzo (three for `n-way-sync-registry`), each a command-check-decision 3-tuple per the canonical `outbox-append-json-roundtrip` pattern вҖ” e.g. `version-bump-all-surfaces`, `dry-run-file-list-review`, `internal-name-grep-zero`, `tty-publish-check`, `outbox-write-route-gate` (a PreToolUse route gate for the outbox-push discipline). Built by a 10-agent workflow with the anti-padding rule ("if the mezzo yields one good atom, write one") вҖ” three agents correctly returned "no new atom" where the parent mezzo's own enumeration was already satisfied, and the run rode the В§3.2 resume cache through a mid-flight session-budget wall (7 cached + 2 live on re-issue, zero duplicate cost вҖ” the discipline's second live validation). Verification (real YAML parser + `node --check` on 33 extracted JS blocks) caught 2 frontmatter parse failures (unquoted scalars containing `: `) вҖ” fixed across all 10 affected files in one sweep, re-verified 20/20 PASS. INDEX.md gains the micro section in count+discovery form (atom ids live on disk; the вүӨ300-token cap remains a v0.2+ auto-gen target, unchanged-class placeholder). Known follow-ups recorded: `.greatpractice/blocklist` SSoT is adopter-local (atoms self-guard on absence); two Decision blocks carry illustrative cross-invocation state. **No wire change**. verify-nway 10-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.89** (2026-06-12) вҖ” **Constellation v2.4.21 вҖ” .eux rough-tier re-distill (E2b вҖ” the re-distill track complete)** вҖ” spec-only, plugin unchanged. The six `ws-*` dashboard component specs (channel-input В· conn-bar В· tabs В· tool-card В· fab-badge В· collab-invite), 15 commits behind the reference dashboard, re-distilled at their declared rough fidelity ("flexible brew starting points") вҖ” absorbing the v2.4.2вҖ“v2.4.9 surface evolution (unified A2A-intent cards, attachment chips, client-side SelectionPrompt chips, date-line divider, anchor presets + position persistence, key-issuance panel unification + UI5 management modal, connection dots, group tinting, mid-task prompt injection). **Anti-fabrication discipline, learned from the v2.5.88 incident, was enforced as hard rules**: absorb only behaviors greppable in the current implementation (never from doc prose), and cite the implementing symbol for every added behavior. The verification agent then word-boundary-grepped **all ~146 referenced symbols against the implementation: zero fabrications**, plus 10 numeric spot-checks (z-indexes, px offsets, char clamps, timer values) all line-exact, zero В§13.14 leakage. Bonus finding confirmed true: `setupWsCollab` is dead code (defined, never invoked since the v2.4.2 unification) вҖ” pruning candidate noted. With detail tier (v2.4.20) + rough tier (this cut), the user's .eux-SSoT decision is fully enacted: every spec with a live reference counterpart now describes the current implementation. **No wire change**. verify-nway 10-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.88** (2026-06-12) вҖ” **Constellation v2.4.20 вҖ” .eux detail-tier re-distill (the .eux-SSoT decision enacted) + В§6 UI6 misattribution fix** вҖ” doc+spec, plugin unchanged. The user resolved the eux-vs-cjs gate as **re-distill** ("if the code changed first, distilling it back is the point of adopting EstreUX") вҖ” the specs regain SSoT standing instead of being demoted. **Scope (this cut = detail tier)**: git-history drift mapping showed the server family 7 commits behind (v2.5.56вҖ“71: KEY-MGMT, session routing, channel-history deletion, В§13.19.10 detector, В§13.22 observe set, security hardening) and ws-core/watchdog/server-keys 1 each; a 7-agent workflow re-distilled `server-core` (secure-by-default bind + WS_BIND opt-in + startup warnings), `server-relay` (В§13.19.10 opt-in deadlock detector + DeleteChannelHistory routing), `ws-core` (WS_MAX_FRAME single-frame + reassembly cap), `watchdog` (single-instance PID-lock guard), verified `server-keys` already-absorbed (hex-length corrected to 24), and updated the `server.eux` parent manifest. **Adversarial verification earned its keep**: the verify agent caught one fabricated behavior вҖ” `server-relay.eux` had absorbed a server-side UI6 SelectionPrompt store/TTL that does not exist in the reference (zero symbol hits; the cited source anchors pointed at unrelated code). Root cause: **Constellation.md В§6 itself misattributed UI6 SelectionPrompt to server-relay** (it is a dashboard-client surface; the server relays those CUSTOMs plainly) вҖ” the re-distill agent trusted the doc. Both the spec and the В§6 line are corrected. Note: EstreUX `drift-check.mjs` compares provenance sha against brewed `dist/` outputs, which this spec-only repo intentionally does not carry вҖ” implementation-contrast spot-checks (line-exact) are the verification tier here. Rough-tier `ws-*.eux` (15 commits behind, flexible-starting-point class) deferred to a follow-up cut. **No wire change**. verify-nway 10-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.87** (2026-06-12) вҖ” **Constellation v2.4.19 вҖ” /drillnow skill (top-blocker depth drill)** вҖ” plugin 0.3.16. The depth counterpart to `/roundnext`'s breadth: pick the single highest-priority blocked item and spend the turn *actually trying to clear it*. Contract: a drill ends in exactly one of two states вҖ” the blocker is gone and the work has started, or the blocker is **proven** unclearable right now and the queue is re-prioritized around that proof; "still blocked, unchanged" is not a valid exit. Procedure: в‘  target selection (top blocked item; user-decision gates are excluded вҖ” they belong to the decisions panel, not to drilling); в‘Ў blocker decomposition into this-side-doable / other-party / environment / time parts (recorded blockReasons are routinely coarser than reality); в‘ў escalating clearing attempts вҖ” re-verify (already gone?) вҶ’ this-side prerequisite work вҶ’ alternative/partial route вҶ’ tool substitution вҶ’ В§13.20 nudge one tier up with the drill's findings attached, all under В§13.18 gates; в‘Ј exit A: unblock + start now; в‘Ө exit B: state the immovable part + what/when will move it, demote the item, promote the doable work the drill surfaced, and rewrite `blockReason` to the decomposed verified form вҖ” the next drill starts from truth, not a stale coarse reason; в‘Ҙ report the delta. A drill that merely re-describes the blocker has failed its contract. **No wire change**. verify-nway 10-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.86** (2026-06-12) вҖ” **Constellation v2.4.18 вҖ” dashboard UI setup-time localization MUST (В§6)** вҖ” doc-only, plugin unchanged. The reference dashboard ships Korean-original: ~1,900 hardcoded UI string spans (buttons, labels, tooltips, status copy) across `app.js`/`index.html`, with no localization guidance anywhere in the spec вҖ” only locale-sensitive *behaviors* (client-local timestamps В§13.11.3 rule 3, date-line day labels) were normative, and those are language-independent. New В§6 rule: when an adopter sets up the board for a user whose prevailing language is not Korean, the setting-up agent MUST localize the UI strings as part of setup вҖ” the setup agent is an LLM that already knows the user's language from the surrounding conversation, so a faithful one-time pass needs no i18n infrastructure (display strings only; identifiers, wire vocabulary, CSS classes, event names, and В§13.14-redaction-checked content are untouchable). Same discipline family as Hyperbrief В§5.6.7 auto-localize, applied to the board surface вҖ” closing the asymmetry where one module had a normative language rule and the other none. Optional for mixed-language teams: extract to an i18n dictionary (the EG promo site under `docs/` carries a working EN/KO pattern to copy) вҖ” registered as a planned item, not required for the single-language common case. **No wire change**. verify-nway 10-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.85** (2026-06-12) вҖ” **Constellation v2.4.17 вҖ” stop-hook registry-path fallback chain (cwd-independent session routing; cursor-steal regression fix)** вҖ” runtime-only, plugin unchanged. The v2.4.7 register-all session routing resolved its registry at `<cwd>/.agent-sessions.json` вҖ” a trap: when an agent ends a turn while `cd`'d into a nested repo (e.g. an inner public repo inside the workspace), the hook misses the workspace-root registry, reports `registry=none`, and falls through to the legacy no-routing path вҖ” where the main session's hook advances *worker-owned* inbox cursors, the exact cursor-steal v2.4.7 was built to prevent (observed live 2026-06-12; no content was lost because the worker had already consumed the affected lines, but the protection had silently lapsed). Fix: `resolveRegistryPath()` searches a fallback chain вҖ” `AGENT_SESSIONS_PATH` env вҶ’ cwd вҶ’ `CLAUDE_PROJECT_DIR` вҶ’ up to four parent directories of `INBOX_PATH` (the workspace root is embedded in the inbox path regardless of where the agent has wandered). All-absent preserves the legacy single-session behavior. Reproduced the failure condition (inner cwd, no env) вҶ’ now `registry=active В· session-route OWN`. **No wire change**. verify-nway 10-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.84** (2026-06-12) вҖ” **Constellation v2.4.16 вҖ” В§13.22.10 optional server-side PR observe tier (doc-only, plugin unchanged)** вҖ” the first item started by a live `/roundnext` round (ripeness check: registered 2026-06-08, unblocked, due). The base server treats `CUSTOM` as pure relay; the PR system's five types are the one declared place a server MAY opt into slightly more, now specified as a bounded tier: (a) **observe set** вҖ” project the five В§13.22.3 types onto the board as a per-PR lifecycle card tracking the В§13.22.8 five-state machine, read-only over in-flight messages; (b) **merge-authority gate** вҖ” `wsPrMergeReject` rejects `PRMergeRequest` from non-main-for-target-repo roles and logs to the decisions panel вҖ” the server-side half of В§13.22.7, justified as merge is the protocol's only irreversible transition; (c) **strictly optional** вҖ” the protocol is complete agent-side without the tier; (d) **declared exception, no creep** вҖ” content-awareness for exactly these five types, registered as a named exception to the В§13.13 layer split, explicitly not a precedent for general payload inspection; (e) reference implementation adopter-side (hub `_PR_CUSTOM` observe set + `PRStatusUpdate` observation + strict gate, dry-run default). Closes the planned item that had aged since 2026-06-08. **No wire change**. verify-nway 10-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.83** (2026-06-12) вҖ” **Constellation v2.4.15 + Hyperbrief v0.6.2 вҖ” /roundnext skill + decisions-panel fallback button (В§5.6.7 board surface)** вҖ” plugin constellation 0.3.15 / hyperbrief 0.6.2. **(1) New plugin skill `roundnext`** вҖ” mechanizes the composition of В§13.16.6 element 5 (planned-queue scan) + В§13.20 (blocker tracking/nudge) + В§13.18 (autonomous execution) into one invocable round, 5 steps: в‘  ripeness-check unblocked planned items and start what is ready; в‘Ў re-verify blockers *now* (recorded blockReasons go stale silently) вҖ” unblock, start, or re-sort; в‘ў for surviving blockers, derive what would clear them and which part is doable from here вҖ” register as planned or start if small (BlockerNudge cadence armed otherwise); в‘Ј multi-dimensional new-work scan (release surfaces В· doc/spec drift В· verification gaps В· security follow-ups В· dogfood evidence В· cross-module В· undecomposed user intents) with an anti-inflation rule; в‘Ө route human-gated items to the decisions panel as a Hyperbrief briefing, default tone L1.1.1 unless the project pins another level. A round never ends as a silent no-op вҖ” its delta (or why there is none) is the report. **(2) Hyperbrief В§5.6.7 live-board surface (v0.6.2)** вҖ” the decisions panel becomes the third fallback surface alongside HTML/MD: every non-resolved decision card renders a tone-floor fallback button (label from the entry's `fallback.label`, populated from the IR's `audience_profile_fallback.button_label` per the auto-localize discipline; plain default otherwise); clicking POSTs `{kind:"fallback-rerender", id, question}` to the board feedback channel, and the brief-owning agent regenerates the entry's `detail` one floor lower вҖ” the MD trigger-phrase contract, board-mediated. Reference dashboard impl: button + handler + CSS; `detail` rendering also gains newline-to-`<br>` after escaping (decision details are plain text with line structure вҖ” HTML in `detail` was rendering as literal tags since the v2.5.75 escape hardening). Endpoint smoke-tested (POST 200 + feedback row). **(3) docs-badge drift corrections** вҖ” index.html Constellation module-tag was stale at v2.4.13 and hyperbrief.html hero at v0.6.0 (an uncovered surface class); corrected and a new **docs-badge axis** added to the outer verify-nway harness (now 10 axes, negative-tested: injected stale вҶ’ FAIL detected). **No wire change**. verify-nway 10-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.82** (2026-06-11) вҖ” **Constellation v2.4.14 вҖ” pre-compact handoff mechanization (В§13.16.6 element 6 hook pair + before-compact skill)** вҖ” plugin 0.3.14. Compaction fires outside agent control and its summaries reliably drop *procedural* details вҖ” env-var call conventions, routing rules, policy one-liners, resume handles. Observed failure (2026-06-11): a required env-var prefix on one script call lived only in-context, was dropped by a compaction summary, and the post-compact agent reverted to the script's default path вҖ” misrouting five A2A messages to the wrong board until a human noticed downstream. **New reference runtime** `constellation/reference/runtime/pre-compact/`: (a) `pre-compact-snapshot.cjs` вҖ” `PreCompact` hook (matcher `*`): deterministically snapshots environment truth (git HEAD / dirty / latest tag, optional secondary repo + track-doc listing) into a two-zone handoff file and emits `additionalContext` directing the post-compact agent to read it; (b) `reload-handoff.cjs` вҖ” `SessionStart` hook (matcher `"compact"`): prints the handoff file to stdout for harness re-injection into the fresh context. The handoff file pairs a machine-replaced **auto-snapshot block** with a model-maintained **standing card** (the half no script can collect вҖ” what in-context details are load-bearing). **New plugin skill `before-compact`** populates the standing card: procedure conventions / in-flight cycle anchors / unrecorded decisions / active resource IDs + resume handles, with a keep-it-short discipline (the file re-enters context after every compaction вҖ” length is a recurring tax) and a promote-to-durable step. Spec note added under В§13.16.6 element 6 (division of labor: hooks own environment + re-injection, the model owns judgment; this is what makes В§13.21 operative at the procedural layer). **No wire change**. verify-nway 9-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.81** (2026-06-11) вҖ” **Superscalar v0.4.3 вҖ” В§3.2 resume cache (journal-backed re-issue of interrupted fan-outs) + В§11 Entry 07** вҖ” doc cut, plugin v0.1.2 unchanged. **New В§3.2**: CPU mapping = checkpoint / precise-exception recovery. A wide fan-out interrupted mid-flight (token/session budget exhaustion, harness restart) after some lanes retired should not force full re-dispatch: a journal-backed resume cache replays each retired lane's `(prompt, opts) вҶ’ result` from the journal and runs only un-retired lanes live. Harness-neutral discipline, three demands: (1) **determinism precondition** вҖ” referentially stable orchestration scripts (no wall-clock, no randomness, inlined static work-lists) or the cache key drifts; (2) **idempotent lane side-effects** вҖ” a real crash window exists between artifact-written and retirement-journaled, so artifact-writing lanes must tolerate re-execution (journal = retire SSoT, artifact presence = advisory); (3) **cost-benefit composition** вҖ” above the ~30-60k token dispatch horizon, resume capability is a prerequisite-grade harness feature; the manual fallback is per-item completion files + a skip-existing pre-check. Reference impl: Claude Code Workflow resume. **New В§11 Entry 07** (n=1, incidental): a 53-lane read-only translation fan-out hit a session budget wall at 25 retired / 28 harness-failed; one re-issue recovered 25 lanes from journal (zero re-execution), idempotently overwrote 9 lanes caught in the artifact-vs-journal crash window, and ran the rest live вҖ” 53/53 + verification PASS, zero content loss. Validates both В§3.2 preconditions in one incident. **No wire change**. verify-nway 9-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.80** (2026-06-11) вҖ” **Greatpractice v0.3.0 вҖ” retire axis (В§7.7: active / probation / retired state machine)** вҖ” the GP-side implementation of EG's north-star value axis 3 (deprecation as a first-class operation): a standard that cannot shed cruft becomes precisely the burden its cleaner successor inherits, so retiring a practice must be as first-class as promoting one. **New В§7.7**: a minimal 3-state `status:` frontmatter enum вҖ” `active` (default) / `probation` (validity in doubt вҖ” В§7.3 validation failure, В§5.6 miss-counter threshold, or suspected environment change; hooks keep enforcing but tag messages) / `retired` (enforcement stops; body preserved with mandatory `retire_reason` + optional `superseded_by`). Four transitions only (over-design forbidden): activeвҶ’probation and probationвҶ’active are automatable; probationвҶ’retired and activeвҶ’retired (direct, when superseded вҖ” with a В§5.5 redirect stub) require user ratification, symmetric with promotion. Explicitly orthogonal to the existing `lifecycle` habit-formation axis (`lifecycle: probation` = "still young" vs `status: probation` = "under suspicion" вҖ” the combination `lifecycle: automatic` + `status: probation` is valid) and to В§7.6 cold eviction (idle-driven vs validity-driven). **INDEX rule**: retired entries leave the tier sections; a one-line `Retired: N` counter preserves the вүӨ300-token cap. **Surfaces**: Greatpractice.md В§7.7 + В§7 cross-deps + `_schema.md` `status`/`retire_reason` fields + `INDEX.md` Retired stub. Hook-runtime status-scan exclusion lands with the runtime build (per В§11 cut scope). **Module versions**: Greatpractice v0.2.1 вҶ’ **v0.3.0** (plugin.json / marketplace / docs module-tag + hero badge synced). **No wire change**. verify-nway 9-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.79** (2026-06-11) вҖ” **MCP serverInfo drift correction (complement R2, audit U6 follow-up)** вҖ” metadata-only, no functional or wire change, no module version bump. The 2026-06-10 full-audit drift sweep (U6) measured two MCP `initialize`-handshake `serverInfo.version` values stale against their own `package.json`: hyperbrief `0.4.2` vs pkg `0.6.1` (carried since the v0.4.2 era across four version bumps) and constellation `0.2.0` vs pkg `0.2.4`. Both servers now derive serverInfo from `require("./package.json").version` вҖ” the structural fix, not a one-time renumber (a hardcoded correction would re-drift on the next bump; ultrasafe was already safe via its single-source `VERSION` constant). Live-verified: stdio `initialize` returns `0.6.1` / `0.2.4`. Companion (outer maintenance repo): `verify-nway-version.cjs` expanded from 5 to 9 axes вҖ” 3 new MCP-serverInfo axes (accepting the require-dynamic, single-constant, and matching-hardcoded patterns) + 1 seed-module-registry axis (6 seed files Г— 5 modules + plugins/ presence + marketplace listing), so this blind spot is now machine-checked on every cut. verify-nway 9-axis PASS.
- **v2.5.78** (2026-06-11) вҖ” **Repo pruning cut (G5вҖ“G9)** вҖ” doc/asset-only, no module or seed version change, loss-zero discipline throughout (everything removed either moves to an archive surface or is a byte-identical duplicate). **(G5) Constellation.md frontmatter codicil pruned** вҖ” the single-line frontmatter had accreted ~11.3KB of per-cut narrative; now ~1KB carrying only version / date / protocol capabilities + an explicit pointer that per-cut detail lives in CHANGELOG.md (verified: every pruned clause's version token appears in a CHANGELOG entry). **(G6) CHANGELOG archive split** вҖ” v1.0вҖ“v2.4.x entries (39 EN + 39 KO) moved verbatim to new `CHANGELOG-archive.md`; active CHANGELOG.md keeps v2.5.x+ with a delegation pointer per section. Count-verified: 234 entries before = 156 active + 78 archived after. **(G7) Hyperbrief research originals archived** вҖ” `_proposals/006_2026-06-03_hyperbrief/` six-axis research + synthesis originals (4 files, ~370KB) moved to the bundle's `archive/` subfolder; bundle README links updated (8). **(G8) Distilled RRP docs superseded** вҖ” `2026-06-01-a2a-pr-system-rrp.md` (distilled into В§13.22) and `deadlock-resolution-draft.md` (absorbed into В§13.19) get SUPERSEDED banners + move to `constellation/reference/docs/archive/`; 4 spec citations re-pointed. **(G9) Logo dedup** вҖ” 4 files in `logo/` were byte-identical (md5) duplicates of the served copies in `docs/assets/` with zero inbound references; removed (вҲ’855KB). PNG recompression (main 851KB / favicon 179KB) deferred вҖ” no lossless optimizer available in this environment. **No wire change**. verify-nway 5-axis PASS.

- **v2.5.71** (2026-06-10) вҖ” **Constellation v2.4.11 security hardening patch (seed+module+plugin full-audit follow-up)** вҖ” per direct user instruction (2026-06-10: security/remediation/improvement-level items proceed as patch bumps; pruning-class and minor-bump-or-larger items go to separate review), of the reference-runtime security findings identified in the full audit (Workflow `wf_fe661e2b-c4c` вҖ” 10-area parallel survey completed + Phase 2/3 hit the session limit so main synthesized directly + core security code spot-check вң…verified), the 3 **patch-level (code fix / fact correction, no wire change)** items: **(1) secure-by-default bind** вҖ” reference `server.cjs` now binds `127.0.0.1` (loopback) by default (`WS_BIND` env override) + non-loopback startup warning. **Rationale (вң…code-verified)**: the KEY-MGMT gate on board connections (`server.cjs:532` `if (isAgent && wsAgentRole!=='main')`) uses `isAgent &&`, so a board connection that never sent HELLO bypasses the gate entirely вҶ’ unauthenticated KeyIssue/KeyList/KeyRevoke/SetMain (`:769-770` fall-through), while RegisterUpstream/CollabKey (`:527-528`) В· SetMain (`:540`) have no gate at all. board=trusted-operator is intentional, but the previous `server.listen(PORT)` (`:796`, no host argument) = 0.0.0.0 bind meant LAN exposure вҶ’ anyone could issue keys / list keys (KeyList returns collab/upstream in plaintext `:369-379`) / SetMain. Plus HELLO `msg.agentId` is unvalidated (`:705`) with a `'main-agent'` default (`:262`) вҶ’ role spoofing. **The default loopback bind blocks this remote vector (critical + highГ—2) in one stroke** (gate/agentId-role redesign affects the wire вҶ’ separate review). **(2) WS frame cap** вҖ” `ws-core.cjs` `decodeFrame` terminates immediately when the declared length > `WS_MAX_FRAME` (default 16 MiB), and the fragmented-reassembly total (`_fragLen`) gets the same cap вҖ” blocks memory-exhaustion DoS via huge declared lengths / unbounded continuation accumulation (the v2.4.5 2.5GB runaway class). **(3) credential gitignore + server-keys.eux correction** вҖ” `key.json` (keyStore) + legacy `ws-keys.json` + `local-keys/*.key` were not covered by `.gitignore` (`git check-ignore` exit 1 вң…) вҶ’ plaintext key files could land in a tracked directory. - **v2.5.70** (2026-06-08) вҖ” **Constellation v2.4.10 A2A PR System В§13.22 distill + deadlock server automation opt-in** вҖ” two normative reinforcements (direct user directive 2026-06-08: "apply the PR system, and add the server-side deadlock automation as an optional item that Constellation adopters can apply if needed"). **(1) В§13.22 A2A PR System promoted to formal spec** вҖ” distills the previously dangling В§13.22 reference at `Constellation.md` line 740 (reference existed with no section body) from the RRP design document (`constellation/reference/docs/2026-06-01-a2a-pr-system-rrp.md`, 972 lines) into a В§13.19-grade formal normative section: **two-level abstraction** (Level 1 = A2A-only **virtual PR** вҖ” propose/review/merge negotiation over board A2A alone, without a git provider; Level 2 = **Github PR** provider-mediated вҖ” local-bridge creates/merges the actual PR) + **5 wire vocabulary** (`PRRequest` proposal / `PRDraftReady` draft ready / `PRReviewAck` review / `PRMergeRequest`В·`PRMergeAck` merge negotiation / `PRStatusUpdate` status) + `sourceContentRef.kind` enum (inline / attachment-ref / mirror-branch / patch) + **fail-safe reject** of unrecognized kinds + **topology b** (agents have no direct git access вҖ” routed via local-bridge commands) + **approval discipline** (trusted-mirror auto-approve / standard opt-in **default** / emergency override) + **ОІвҖІ mirror-branch-on-target** sourcing (mirror branch on the target repo, not the source repo) + **per-repo authority** (strict: only `role==main` passes the merge gate) + **5-state lifecycle** state machine (requestedвҶ’draftвҶ’reviewвҶ’merge-pendingвҶ’merged/rejected) + composition with В§13.13 (at-least-once relay) / В§13.19 (deadlock) / В§13.20. EG **ships the protocol spec only** вҖ” the PR-bot reference impl is adopter-side (provider tokens/permissions live in the adopter environment). **(2) В§13.19.10 Q3 deadlock server detector opt-in reference impl** вҖ” adds a board-adapter strict 2-cycle detector to `runtime/server.cjs`, `WS_DEADLOCK_DETECT` env-gated (**default OFF**): when enabled, approximates wait-edges via a reply-pairing map (`_a2aPending`) вҶ’ on detecting a strict 2-cycle where both sides exceed the threshold (`WS_DEADLOCK_PROBE_MS`, default 120s), emits a `DeadlockProbe` CUSTOM to the board (duplicate suppression via `_deadlockSeen` Set + auto-clear when the cycle resolves, scan interval = min(probe, 30s) unref). Default OFF so **serverвҶ”application coupling is not forced** вҖ” **canonical detection remains the agent-side turn-start wait-edge DFS (В§13.19.3)**, and quasi-deadlock remains agent-side SLA discipline (В§13.19.4); the server detector is strictly a supplementary safety net (it approximates from observable reply-pairing only, so false negatives are possible вҖ” explicitly non-canonical). **Files modified**: Constellation.md (frontmatter v2.4.9 вҶ’ v2.4.10 + codicil; new В§13.22 section distilled after В§13.21; opt-in reference impl paragraph after В§13.19.10 Q3); plugins/constellation/.claude-plugin/plugin.json (v0.3.9 вҶ’ v0.3.10 + desc); .claude-plugin/marketplace.json (metadata 0.3.15 вҶ’ 0.3.16 + constellation v0.3.9 вҶ’ v0.3.10 + desc); constellation/reference/runtime/server.cjs (WS_DEADLOCK_DETECT detector вҖ” both inner + outer collab-self/server.cjs, node --check PASS); README(badge + Current/нҳ„мһ¬ EN+KO); docs/index.html(hero badge v2.5.69 вҶ’ v2.5.70 + module-tag v2.4.9 вҶ’ v2.4.10); docs/shared/data.js(v2.5.70 + shipCount 85 вҶ’ 86); CHANGELOG. **Module versions**: Constellation v2.4.9 вҶ’ **v2.4.10** (patch вҖ” spec distill + server opt-in detector, **no default-behavior wire change**), plugin v0.3.9 вҶ’ v0.3.10. - **v2.5.68** (2026-06-08) вҖ” **Constellation v2.4.8 dashboard EstreUF-parity 5-gap port** вҖ” ported 5 EstreUF-only behaviors identified via full comparison against the upstream original (EstreUF) dashboard (3-agent parallel, function/CSS/id inventory diff + inline behavior cross-check). EG was mostly equivalent or actually ahead (wsConfirm custom dialog В· key-management kind dropdown/local-worker keys В· anchor-based positioning В· settings modal В· context menu), and only the following 5 were EstreUF-only: **(1) hide decisions badge at zero** вҖ” `renderDecisions` toggles `_decBadge.hidden = (unresolved+adhoc === 0)`. Previously only `.textContent` was updated without toggling `.hidden`, so the `#decisions-badge[hidden]{display:none}` CSS was dead code вҶ’ the tab showed a red "0" pill at all times even with zero decisions. **(2) preserve message send-time** вҖ” `wsMsgEpoch(m)`(m.timestamp epoch вҶ’ m.at ISO Date.parse вҶ’ null) + `wsRowTime(m)` helpers derive `_t`(HH:MM:SS)В·`_ts`(epoch) at the top of onWsEvent вҶ’ unified across all row pushes (status/user/TEXT_MESSAGE_START/TOOL_CALL/Attachment/a2acard/selection). Previously `_msgT` covered only the m.at number case + `row.ts=Date.now()` always + some `nowHM()`, so **after refresh/History replay all date-change lines collapsed to "today" + group-merge ordering followed receive order + per-card times within the same stream were inconsistent** вҶ’ now uniformly pinned to the original send time. **(3) closed-session permanent-delete cross-board sync + persist** вҖ” added a `DeleteChannelHistory` handler to the server (`runtime/server.cjs`) (`wsCloseChannelHist`(remove history file) + `wsToBoards`(broadcast to other boards), mirroring the existing CloseChannel handler pattern) + inbound `DeleteChannelHistory`(synced channel removal) / `HistoryCleared`(full-delete sync) handlers on the client. Previously the server did not handle `DeleteChannelHistory` вҶ’ **рҹ—‘ permanent-delete was not persisted server-side, resurrecting on refresh + unsynced across multi-browser boards** (this fix resolves both the persistence bug + cross-board sync). **(4) routing-independent early handling of `SelectionResolved`** вҖ” handled at the top of onWsEvent (before the agent-outbound agentId guard) so the chip dims even when arriving as a direct server reply without agentId (previously only inside the agent-outbound switch вҶ’ required passing the agentId guard, a defensive-coverage gap). **(5) 4-role color tint on member tab names when a group is selected** вҖ” `wsRenderTabs` adds `grpSel = (active===group)` + assigns the group cls to `.nm` + CSS `.ws-tab .nm.{up,main,local,collab}` 4 roles (previously `.ws-tab.up/.main .nm` 2-role always-on color вҶ’ 4-role tint on group selection). **Files modified**: Constellation.md(frontmatter v2.4.7 вҶ’ v2.4.8 + codicil); plugins/constellation/.claude-plugin/plugin.json(v0.3.7 вҶ’ v0.3.8 + desc); constellation/reference/dashboard/app.js(wsMsgEpoch/wsRowTime + unified _t/_ts + badge hidden + early SelectionResolved + grpSel + DeleteChannelHistory/HistoryCleared handlers) + dashboard/style.css(.nm 4-role); constellation/reference/runtime/server.cjs(DeleteChannelHistory handler); README(badge + Current/нҳ„мһ¬ EN+KO); docs/index.html(hero badge v2.5.67 вҶ’ v2.5.68 + module-tag v2.4.7 вҶ’ v2.4.8); docs/shared/data.js(v2.5.67 вҶ’ v2.5.68 + shipCount 83 вҶ’ 84); .claude-plugin/marketplace.json(metadata 0.3.13 вҶ’ 0.3.14 + constellation v0.3.7 вҶ’ v0.3.8); CHANGELOG. **Module versions**: Constellation v2.4.7 вҶ’ **v2.4.8**(patch вҖ” dashboard parity + server DeleteChannelHistory handler, no wire change: adds server-side handling + board broadcast for an existing clientвҶ’server message, no impact on non-handling adopters), plugin v0.3.7 вҶ’ v0.3.8. - **v2.5.67** (2026-06-07) вҖ” **Constellation v2.4.7 single-workspace multi-agent session-aware routing (register-all + fail-safe) + dashboard issuance bug fix** вҖ” when multiple Claude Code sessions (main + local worker, etc.) are open in the same workspace, they share-execute the same Stop hook (`pre-send-probe --rearm`) вҶ’ contention on the same A2A cursor (a worker turn-end advances main's surfacing cursor first вҶ’ main never sees the inbound; surface theft). Avoids splitting into separate workspaces (duplicate extension loading per IDE window + harness/doc context severance cost) by branching on the **per-session env `CLAUDE_CODE_SESSION_ID`** (injected into the hook process by Claude Code вҖ” `src=env` empirically confirmed, stdin payload `.session_id` fallback). **register-all model**: every session (main included) declares its own inboxes in the `<cwd>/.agent-sessions.json` registry; each hook run processes only SELF-owned inboxes вҖ” (a) unregistered/unidentifiable session вҶ’ SKIP-ALL (fail-safe: no cursor advance, never intrudes on another session's surface вҖ” main protection guaranteed by mechanism, not discipline), (b) inbox owned by another session вҶ’ skip, (c) ownerless inbox вҶ’ skip (register-all requires explicit ownership), (d) self-owned вҶ’ normal processing. When the registry is inactive (absent/empty workers), legacy default (single-session workspace, identical to before) вҖ” back-compat. **New/changed files**: `runtime/stop-hook/register-session.cjs` (NEW вҖ” registers/validates/releases session `{role, ownInboxes}`, keyed by `CLAUDE_CODE_SESSION_ID`) + `runtime/stop-hook/pre-send-probe.cjs` (register-all routing block вҖ” 6/6 case simulation PASS) + `runtime/scripts/join-local.cjs` v2.4.7 (local worker `OUTBOX` drain = the worker session appends to the outbox file вҶ’ join-local sends via a 1.5s drain, new worker emit path + full inbound logging so Delegate value bodies are read) + `runtime/server.cjs` (startup warning when WS_PRIMARY_AGENT is unset вҖ” when unset, the main session is demoted to local; mechanizes `feedback_self_board_restart_env`). **Two-tier wakeup for low-latency A2A inbox reception**: tier 1 = вүӨ5s polling file Monitor (immediate wakeup on event), tier 2 = long ScheduleWakeup fallback heartbeat (1200-1800s) вҖ” relying on ScheduleWakeup cadence (minute-scale) alone delays reception by that much (confirmed by the 2026-06-07 case where board-observer waited for a Delegate until the /loop cadence). **Dashboard issuance bug fix (Cut A bundle)**: blocked the `.ws-collab-*` cursor:move leak (`.ws-pop-head`'s cursor:move was inherited down the issuance panel's child chain вҖ” leak path confirmed via Playwright) + (private self-board) 5-handler drift fix for KEY-MGMT responses (root cause of key issuance stalling at "л°ңкёү мӨ‘вҖҰ" вҖ” the outer dashboard was missing the v2.4.0 canonical KeyIssued/KeyError/KeyListResult/KeyRevokedВ·LabeledВ·RevokePending handlers, confirmed via Playwright WS frame capture). **Live verification**: round-trip with the local worker (board-observer) вҖ” DelegateвҶ’WorkerAck/WorkerReport, **direct proof of main-cursor non-collision** (multiple worker turn-ends SKIP the collab-self inbox вҶ’ main cursor held at 287; the worker's 3 replies remained unsurfaced and main's next hook surfaced them normally) + main auto-reception (вүӨ3s file Monitor, no nudge). **Files modified**: Constellation.md(frontmatter v2.4.6 вҶ’ v2.4.7 + codicil); plugins/constellation/.claude-plugin/plugin.json(v0.3.6 вҶ’ v0.3.7); pre-send-probe.cjs + register-session.cjs(NEW) + scripts/join-local.cjs + server.cjs + dashboard/style.css; README(badge + Current/нҳ„мһ¬ EN+KO); docs/index.html(hero badge v2.5.66 вҶ’ v2.5.67 + module-tag v2.4.6 вҶ’ v2.4.7); docs/shared/data.js(v2.5.66 вҶ’ v2.5.67 + shipCount 82 вҶ’ 83); .claude-plugin/marketplace.json(metadata 0.3.12 вҶ’ 0.3.13 + constellation v0.3.6 вҶ’ v0.3.7); - **v2.5.54** (2026-06-05) вҖ” **Hyperbrief docs L1.1.1.I tone-consistency re-render + two candidate #7 spec corrections (C scope = no retroactive prompt + I low-frequency override).** Continuation of the v2.5.53 cycle. Two spec corrections added to candidate #7 (tone-axis term-pairing) from user input: **(a) structural exclusion of the C (conversation) scope** вҖ” the C scope is unaffected by all three retroactive_apply options prompt/Y/N (rewriting the author's own historical output is difficult + determinism is hard to guarantee + cognitive load + negligible consistency value; the command `L1.I.C` вҶ’ apply immediately without asking; `L1.I.C+D` вҶ’ prompt for the D portion only). **(b) low-frequency override for I (initial) mode** вҖ” when a term is used вүӨ 3 times within the application-scope unit, pair it on every occurrence even in I mode; from 4 uses and up, spell out only the first mention (rationale: author cognitive load + the longer the gap, the harder abbreviation recall + accounting for the distance across Hyperbrief brief's 9 sections Г— multiple items). - **v2.5.44** (2026-06-04) вҖ” **`constellation/reference/runtime/stop-hook/pre-send-probe.cjs` self-emission echo filter вҖ” drop lines where `o.ev === "sent"` during meaningful classification. The bridge logs both outbound (`ev:"sent"`) and inbound (`ev:"inbound"`) to the same inbox.log file, so without this gate the В§13.16.9 name-only allowlist (Report / Delegate / WorkerReport / Request / PRRequest / etc.) classified every outbox push as meaningful inbound on the next probe вҖ” a self-emission echo class that polluted the watch-state cycle.** Watch-state hygiene patch cut. Diagnosis: v2.4.16 (3565b32) removed a `grep '"ev":"in...'` 1st-stage gate because some adopter bridges write inbound without the `ev` marker; the removal correctly unblocked bridge-alive direct inbound, but it implicitly admitted self-emission `ev:"sent"` lines into the classification pipeline. The downstream В§13.16.9 allowlist filters by message name only, so every outbound A2A-intent push (Report, Delegate, PRRequest, etc.) re-appeared as meaningful inbound on the next Stop hook fire вҖ” the agent's `feedback_pre_send_inbound_check.md` discipline then forced a "read meaningful body + classify" round-trip that costs context without supplying any new information, since the body was the agent's own just-sent payload. Real observed incident: after EG outbox push 348 (`m-eg-cycle1-ack-1780528600` Report to main), the next Stop hook surface listed line 23271 as meaningful вҖ” the very same Report content the agent had just composed. **Fix**: `if (o?.ev === 'sent') continue;` injected immediately after the `JSON.parse` step in `probe()` (lines 90-91 area). Per-line `ev:"sent"` SKIP, NOT an `ev:"inbound"` REQUIRE вҖ” adopters whose bridges write inbound without the `ev` marker continue to have their inbound surfaced normally (the v2.4.16 regression risk is preserved). Inline comment block documents the design choice + cross-references v2.4.16 + v2.5.20 doubly-wrapped envelope handling (orthogonal вҖ” `value.name` fallback still applies after the self-emission skip). **No protocol wire change** вҖ” this is a Stop hook reference-impl classification fix, not a В§13.x specification change. No `Constellation.md` body change. No `local-bridge.eux` change. No `Hyperbrief.md` change. No plugin manifest change. No schema change. No renderer change. No seed lib change. **docs/promo catch-up**: `docs/index.html` hero badge `v2.5.43 вҶ’ v2.5.44`; `docs/shared/data.js` meta `'v2.5.43' вҶ’ 'v2.5.44'` + `shipCount: 59 вҶ’ 60`; `README.md` top badge `v2.5.43 вҶ’ v2.5.44` + `Current:` line rewritten (EN + KO) to describe the self-emission echo gap + fix + the v2.5.43/v2.5.42/v2.5.44 patch arc. **Scope discipline**: `constellation/reference/runtime/stop-hook/pre-send-probe.cjs` (~10 lines net change: 1 skip line + comment block) + `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry, EN + KO) + `docs/index.html` hero badge + `docs/shared/data.js` meta + `README.md` top badge + Versioning Current line (EN + KO). - **v2.5.43** (2026-06-04) вҖ” **`constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs` outboxCursor init aligned with `local-bridge.eux` `@state.outboxCursor` spec (init = EOF, pre-existing lines skipped on respawn). Closes a spec-vs-impl mismatch where the implementation initialized `outboxCursor = 0` at module init, causing the entire accumulated outbox.jsonl to be re-shipped on every bridge restart вҖ” В§13.13.2 server-side dedup masked the application-level impact (every duplicate carried the same `msgId` and was rejected with `AckProcessed{dedupHit:true}`), but bandwidth + log noise was significant: a 19h disconnection window followed by respawn replayed 331 `ev:'sent'` entries in a single drain cycle in a real observed incident.** Bridge runtime patch cut. The `local-bridge.eux` `@state.outboxCursor` declaration documents the intended behavior as `byte offset already shipped from outbox (init = EOF so pre-existing lines are skipped)`, and `derive.connected_gate` reiterates `cursor inits at EOF`. The reference C implementation in `local-bridge.cjs` however set `let outboxCursor = 0;` at module init, then byte-offset-tailed from there вҖ” diverging from the spec by treating all pre-existing outbox content as un-shipped on every spawn. Adopters using the reference impl experienced the same backlog-replay behavior on every bridge restart; `feedback_a2a_relay_reliability.md`'s at-most-once relay note further compounds the concern (transport-tier `Ack delivered` does not guarantee recipient inbox has the body, but here the wire was carrying re-sends of already-acknowledged content). **Fix**: replaces `let outboxCursor = 0;` with `function initOutboxCursor() { try { return fs.statSync(OUTBOX).size; } catch { return 0; } } let outboxCursor = initOutboxCursor();` вҖ” module-init reads the current outbox.jsonl file size and treats that as the cursor's starting position. Pre-existing lines are now skipped per the spec. Inline comment block updated to call out the alignment and reference the В§13.13.2 dedup masking that hid the impact previously. **Trade-off discipline**: this matches spec intent but means lines appended to outbox.jsonl while the bridge is dead will be lost on respawn. The spec assumes the agent only appends when the bridge is live; adopters needing queue-during-restart semantics can override (e.g., persist cursor across restarts) as an opt-in extension вҖ” recommended pattern documented in the inline comment. EG's own outer `EstreGenesis-maintenance` workspace runs a separate `collab/collab-client.cjs` with line-count-based cursor persistence as a stricter local choice; that file is not part of the public reference impl. **No protocol wire change** вҖ” this is a reference impl alignment, not a В§13.x specification change. No `Constellation.md` body change. No `local-bridge.eux` change (spec already documented the correct behavior). No `local-bridge-and-watcher-NOTES.md` change (the bug was in `.cjs`, not in the spec NOTES). No plugin manifest change. No schema change. No renderer change. No seed lib change. **docs/promo catch-up**: `docs/index.html` hero badge `v2.5.42 вҶ’ v2.5.43`; `docs/shared/data.js` meta `'v2.5.42' вҶ’ 'v2.5.43'` + `shipCount: 58 вҶ’ 59`; `README.md` top badge `v2.5.42 вҶ’ v2.5.43` + `Current:` line rewritten (EN + KO) to describe the bridge fix + В§13.13.2 dedup masking. **Scope discipline**: `constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs` (~4 lines net change) + `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry, EN + KO) + `docs/index.html` hero badge + `docs/shared/data.js` meta + `README.md` top badge + Versioning Current line (EN + KO). Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” bridge reference-impl bug fix surfaced by an adopter-equivalent incident is a meaningful push, cut as a patch release. Per `feedback_public_repo_redaction.md` вҖ” no chat verbatim, no governance attribution; the trade-off rationale stays technical.

- **v2.5.41** (2026-06-03) вҖ” **Hyperbrief v0.5.5 вҶ’ v0.5.6 вҖ” В§5.6.7 tone-floor fallback auto-localize discipline codified (skill MUST populate `audience_profile_fallback.button_label` AND `audience_profile_fallback.trigger_phrases_md` in the user's prevailing conversation language at IR-emit time; schema/renderer Korean defaults demoted to last-resort fallback for IR-direct-call/test only; reference EN/KO/JA literals + trigger lists named in В§5.6.7 and SKILL.md). MUST-19 rewritten to fold the discipline in normatively. docs/promo Hyperbrief card (`docs/index.html`) + overview (`docs/hyperbrief.html`) general-tier prose updated to show both EN and KO button literals side-by-side with a "follows the user's language" / "мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ м–ём–ҙм—җ л”°лҰ„" parenthetical.** Same-day design correction cut. User flagged that the v2.5.40 promo prose `"(canonical EG default localizes to plain Korean; adopters localize)"` reflected a real design problem вҖ” the schema default `button_label` is hardcoded Korean (`"лӯ” мҶҢлҰ¬м•ј? н•ңкөӯм–ҙлЎң лІҲм—ӯн•ҙмӨҳ (лӮҙк°Җ м•Ңм•„л“Өмқ„ мҲҳ мһҲлҠ” л§җлЎң)"`) and `trigger_phrases_md` default is Korean-only, with the v0.5.0 spec saying "adopters localize for non-Korean reader-bases SHOULD". This conflated *EG-the-project* (Korean) with *Hyperbrief-the-library* (a public module that ships to adopters in any language); the practical reality is that the skill (LLM composing the IR) already knows the user's prevailing conversation language and can populate the IR accordingly, so the schema's Korean default never needs to surface for non-Korean users in normal flow. The fix is skill-side discipline (not schema change вҶ’ deterministic invariant preserved). **В§5.6.7 HTML surface bullet** rewritten as two bullets: the first names the permanent re-render button + the `audience_profile_fallback.button_label` slot; the second is a new **Auto-localization at IR-emit time (v0.5.6 вҖ” load-bearing default)** bullet that mandates skill-side population in the user's prevailing conversation language, names reference literals for EN (`"What? Just say it plainly."`) / KO (`"лӯ” мҶҢлҰ¬м•ј? н•ңкөӯм–ҙлЎң лІҲм—ӯн•ҙмӨҳ (лӮҙк°Җ м•Ңм•„л“Өмқ„ мҲҳ мһҲлҠ” л§җлЎң)"`) / JA (`"дҪ•гҒ“гӮҢпјҹз§ҒгҒҢеҲҶгҒӢгӮӢиЁҖи‘үгҒ§гҖӮ"`), specifies mixed-language session handling (follow most recent prevailing-language signal), and clarifies that schema/renderer defaults are last-resort fallback for IR-direct-call / programmatic / test invocations only вҖ” in normal skill-driven flow this fallback never surfaces. Same auto-localize discipline applies to `trigger_phrases_md` (skill populates the trigger list in the user's prevailing language). Hard override at `.hyperbrief/profile.json` takes precedence for adopters who want a fixed single language. **В§5.6.7 MD surface bullet** updated to reference the auto-localized trigger list from the new discipline. **MUST-19** rewritten to fold the auto-localize discipline in as normative: skill MUST populate both `button_label` and `trigger_phrases_md` in the user's language at IR-emit time; schema defaults are last-resort fallback only; in skill-driven flow the Korean fallback MUST NOT surface for non-Korean users. **`plugins/hyperbrief/skills/hyperbrief/SKILL.md`** вҖ” section 1 table's `audience_profile_fallback` row extended with explicit reference EN/KO/JA literals + trigger lists (EN: `what?`, `huh?`, `say it plainly`, `i don't get it`, `too much jargon`, `try again simpler`, `in plain english`, `eli5`; KO: `лӯ” мҶҢлҰ¬`, `м•Ҳ мқҪнҳҖ`, `л¬ҙмҠЁ л§җ`, `мқҙн•ҙ м•Ҳ`, `лҚ” мүҪкІҢ`, `л„Ҳл¬ҙ м–ҙл ө`, `лӢӨмӢң н’Җм–ҙ`, `мүҪкІҢ лӢӨмӢң`, `н•ңкөӯм–ҙлЎң`, `н•ңкөӯл§җлЎң`; analogous JA) + mixed-language session handling + hard override precedence note. **No schema change** вҖ” the schema `default` for `button_label` and `trigger_phrases_md` stays Korean (load-bearing for IR-direct-call test invocations and for backwards compatibility with v0.5.0-v0.5.5 IRs that omit the fields); the discipline is enforced at the skill layer (LLM composing the IR), which is the natural place since the LLM knows the user's language and the renderer does not. **No renderer change** вҖ” the renderer's fallback to the schema default stays (`mini-engine.cjs:414`); the discipline shifts WHERE the populated value comes from, not WHAT the renderer does. **Determinism invariant preserved** вҖ” same IR + same options вҶ’ same output bytes (the auto-localize happens upstream at IR-compose time; the IR itself still uniquely determines the surface). **docs/promo updates**: `docs/index.html` Hyperbrief card general-tier prose rewritten вҖ” EN: `"...in plain language you can parse with a single click вҖ” the button reads \"What? Bundle 008's downstream adopter, after the v2.5.32 H1 ajv emergency-fix landed and the rest of bundle 008 + bundle 007 was absorbed across v2.5.33-v2.5.37 (вүҲ 1 hour, 12 releases), re-synced their vendored copy to v2.5.37 and immediately surfaced H7 вҖ” a same-class blocker generated by v0.5.2's own H5 fix: the new `stripHeadingEpistemicTag(ir)` was placed BEFORE `validateIr(ir)` in both render entrypoints, but the schema requires `tagged_text` (epistemic prefix mandatory) on `section_6_decision_prompt.essence_one_line`, so once strip ran the IR no longer matched the schema and ajv rejected every FullBrief at the default code path. The adopter caught this by running clean-install ajv 8.x + validation-on, exactly the same regression-vector as H1; this time they chose pure-mirror-plus-`--skip-validate` over vendor-patch (the M3 trade-off learning paid off вҖ” vendor patches against a 1-hour-turnaround upstream become redundant before they ship). **H7 fix** вҖ” both `renderMd` (line ~328) and `renderHtml` (line ~383) reordered: (1) `stampRecommendedArtifacts(ir)` stays first because the stamped fields (line_count + body_hash) are part of the IR contract and travel with archive bundles, schema-valid by construction; (2) `validateIr(ir)` now runs on the canonical IR (tag prefix intact) вҖ” schema passes; (3) `const renderIr = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(ir))` deep-clones for rendering only; (4) `stripHeadingEpistemicTag(renderIr)` mutates the clone (IR original preserved); (5) `substitute(template, renderIr, surface)` uses the cloned IR. In `renderHtml`, the inline `IR_JSON` placeholder is also fed the stripped clone so the embedded debug-IR agrees with the surface вҖ” `archive_config` callers pass the original `ir` separately to maintain audit invariance. Net code change: ~6 lines added per entrypoint + comment block explaining the fix. **Smoke test PASS** вҖ” clean ajv 8.x environment, full FullBrief IR with all sections populated, validation-on default path: MD render PASS (hash `c5e4ef58aa2edf3f`, 2 warnings вҖ” AF-18 audience-profile-estimate gap, expected), HTML render PASS (hash `2afe182dfdf65b15`); IR original `essence_one_line` confirmed to still start with `[verified]` post-render (pre-v0.5.4 would have crashed before the assertion ran). **В§11.3 vendor-patch-vs-pure-mirror trade-off** вҖ” new paragraph at the end of В§11.3 (`Cross-seed adoption`) codifying the M3 / H1-vs-H7 learning: vendor patch is the right call when upstream turnaround is slow; pure-mirror-plus-workaround is the right call when upstream turnaround is fast (like the EG-owner-as-adopter ~1h baseline measured in bundle 008 002). Either way, the choice should be EXPLICIT in the adopter's project notes so future contributors know whether the local diff is intentional drift or a temporary workaround. **В§11.4 host self-config approval gate** вҖ” new paragraph at the end of В§11.4 (`Hook-tier review queue`) covering the adopter-installation reality: registering the hook with the running Claude Code session requires editing `.claude/settings.json` (or equivalent), which the host's auto-mode classifier treats as agent-runtime self-modification and blocks without explicit user approval. - **v2.5.37** (2026-06-03) вҖ” **Hyperbrief v0.5.2 вҶ’ v0.5.3 вҖ” PreToolUse + Stop hooks activated in advise mode (closes the Phase 2 PreToolUse-hook item carried as "deferred" since v0.4.0) + new review-queue routing extending the simple alert into a deferred-review pipeline (Constellation-on вҶ’ DECISION_REQUEST envelope to board; Constellation-off + auto_generate_review_doc=on вҶ’ `.hyperbrief/pending-reviews/<id>.md` placeholder; default 'ask' вҶ’ stderr advise + setup hint; off вҶ’ simple alert). New `Hyperbrief.md В§11.4` codifies the hook-tier discipline as plugin-tier (Claude Code-specific) on top of the host-agnostic SSoT-tier `SKILL.md` model-invoked discipline. dogfood Entry 03 archived.** Hook activation cut. The v0.4.0 status entry had carried "PreToolUse hook + MCP server **deferred to v0.4.1+**"; the MCP server landed at v0.4.2 (cut v2.5.28), but the PreToolUse hook stayed in the `hooks.json` Phase 1 placeholder through v0.5.0 вҶ’ v0.5.1 вҶ’ v0.5.2 as each cycle prioritized schema / cross-module integration / clean-install blocker fixes. v2.5.37 closes the carry with an advise-mode hook design (exit 0, never block) that adds a *silent-skip detection layer* over the existing model-invoked SKILL.md discipline. **Hook architecture** вҖ” three files under `plugins/hyperbrief/hooks/`: (1) `hooks.json` вҖ” Claude Code hook registration (PreToolUse `AskUserQuestion` + `Bash` + Stop `*`); (2) `trigger-advise.cjs` (~190 LoC, deps-0 except Node stdlib) вҖ” the PreToolUse wrapper, runs on every matching tool call with stdin = tool input JSON, applies the danger-list match for Bash (12 patterns: `git push` / `gh release` / `gh pr create|merge` / `npm publish` / `pnpm publish` / `yarn publish` / `kubectl apply|delete|create` / `docker push` / `terraform apply` / `gcloud вҖҰdeploy` / `aws s3 cp|sync|update|deploy` / `curl -X POST|PUT|DELETE`), generates a `decision_id` matching the В§1 pattern, then routes per the 4-way decision tree (Constellation detection + standalone preference); (3) `revisit-scan.cjs` (~85 LoC) вҖ” the Stop wrapper, scans `hyperbrief-ledger.jsonl` for `revisit_date вүӨ today` (excluding rows with `outcome_actual` filled) and `.hyperbrief/pending-reviews/` for unreviewed placeholders, emits a single advisory line on either signal. **Review-queue routing** (the user-requested extension): on PreToolUse hook fire, the script detects whether Constellation is reachable (CONSTELLATION_WS_URL env set + a local outbox path exists at one of `$CONSTELLATION_OUTBOX_PATH`, `assets/collab/outbox.jsonl`, or `.constellation/outbox.jsonl`). If yes вҶ’ append a `DECISION_REQUEST` envelope to the outbox as a *pending-review placeholder* (carries `decision_id`, `origin: "hyperbrief-hook"`, `pending: true`, `detected_tool`, `detected_intent`, `stage: "pending-review"`, `ack_tier_required: "decided"`); the local Constellation bridge relays the envelope to the board and the board's decisions/review-items panel surfaces it; stderr advise mentions the board surface explicitly. If no вҶ’ check `auto_generate_review_doc` (env `HYPERBRIEF_AUTO_GENERATE_REVIEW_DOC=on|off|ask` or `.hyperbrief/config.json {auto_generate_review_doc: "on"|"off"|"ask"}`, default `"ask"`). When `"on"` вҶ’ write a placeholder MD to `.hyperbrief/pending-reviews/<decision_id>.md` carrying detected tool + intent + raw tool input clipped to 4KB + next-step instructions; stderr advise mentions the file path. When `"ask"` (default) вҶ’ stderr advise only + setup-hint pointing at the config knob. When `"off"` вҶ’ simple stderr alert, no file. This 4-way design lets the hook function as a *deferred-review pipeline* вҖ” the user can defer decisions for later inspection rather than being forced into immediate-or-skip dichotomy at the alert moment, which composes cleanly with the В§2.4 alert-fatigue circuit breaker. The pending вҶ’ HyperbriefCard upgrade follows the same envelope-pair pattern Constellation В§13.16.9 already carries (DECISION_REQUEST + paired HyperbriefCard by parentId; ack_tier='decided' on the Constellation MCP `a2a_wait_ack` side per v2.5.28). **`Hyperbrief.md В§11.4` Hook-tier review queue (v0.5.3 вҖ” Claude Code plugin-tier discipline)** new sub-section ~60 lines: hook contract (advise mode invariants); 4-way review-queue routing with stderr message templates; "why advise mode (not hard-block)" rationale grounded in В§2.4 alert-fatigue circuit breaker semantics; falsification triggers (10/day вҶ’ matcher too broad; 0/week with samples accumulating вҶ’ matcher too narrow or stderr propagation broken; 3+ revisits past date вҶ’ notify-on-revisit opt-in candidate); cross-references to Constellation В§13.16.9 / В§13.16.10 + Hyperbrief В§8. - **v2.5.35** (2026-06-03) вҖ” **Seed lib v2.4.1 вҶ’ v2.4.2 вҖ” Migration B dual-track guidance per bundle 007 M1: Step 1 (Identify starting version) + Step 2 (Diff capabilities) now explicitly describe the seed-version vs EG-release-version separation and require cross-checking BOTH markers before declaring a starting state. Cascades across all 6 seed tiers (Master + Lite + Compact Г— EN/KO).** Seed-lib cut. Bundle 007 M1 surfaced a 2-track tracking gap: the seed-version marker (e.g., `v2.4.1`, embedded in `AGENTS.md`) and the EG-release version (e.g., `v2.5.x`, advancing on every meaningful push per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md`) are independent вҖ” a release-only cut (e.g., Constellation `В§13.x` patch, Hyperbrief module ship) does NOT bump the seed version, so a migrating adopter that checks only the seed marker may conclude "no delta" when substantial module/spec changes have landed. The fix is a Migration B Step 1 + Step 2 rewrite (Master tier full, Lite tier condensed, Compact tier 1-liner) that makes the dual-track expectation explicit. **Master tier (Master EN + Master KO)** вҖ” Step 1 expanded from one paragraph to a structured sub-section naming the two tracks ("seed version" vs "EG release version") + a "Check both markers before declaring a starting version" paragraph explaining the failure mode + cross-check sources (AGENTS.md seed marker + adoption manifest EG-release + upstream `CHANGELOG.md` HEAD) + revised user-question wording ("which EG release tag was current at that time?"). Step 2 prefaced with "List X for the starting **seed version** (table below), AND list Y for the starting **release version** (consult upstream `CHANGELOG.md` between the two release tags вҖ” typically a `git log <starting-tag>..HEAD --oneline -- CHANGELOG.md` against the EG repo, or just read the CHANGELOG entries between the two tags)" and the existing seed-delta table is now labeled "Seed-delta table" so readers know it's only one of the two tracks. **Lite tier (Lite EN + Lite KO)** вҖ” condensed equivalent: Step 1 carries the dual-track explanation in 2 sentences + cross-check instruction; Step 2 prefaced with the dual-track diff. **Compact tier (Compact EN + Compact KO)** вҖ” 1-liner extension at the start of Step 1 + 1-liner reframe of Step 2 ("diff capabilities (both tracks)"). **Frontmatter version markers** вҖ” all 6 tier headers bump `version: v2.4.1 вҶ’ v2.4.2` + `date: 2026-05-31 вҶ’ 2026-06-03` + status fragment `v2.4.2 = bundle 007 M1 reflection вҖ” Migration B Step 1/2 dual-track guidance` (Master) / condensed forms (Lite + Compact). **Why a seed bump (rather than just a CHANGELOG note)** вҖ” the change is to the seed body itself (Migration B procedure), not to a referenced module вҖ” adopters bootstrapping new projects from this seed cut get the dual-track guidance built into the Migration B section, not as an out-of-band CHANGELOG cross-reference. The seed-version marker was unchanged since v2.4.1 (2026-05-31) because the prior cuts (v2.5.0 through v2.5.34) were all release-track changes that did not touch the seed body вҖ” this is the first true seed-body change since v2.4.1, validating the 2-track separation that the change itself codifies. **Cross-tier consistency check passes** вҖ” the dual-track guidance is now present in all 6 tiers; the substance is identical (two tracks, cross-check both, ask user which EG release tag was current); the verbosity scales per tier (Master = full prose explanation, Lite = 2 sentences, Compact = 1 line). **Scope discipline**: 6 seed-tier files (Master EN + Master KO + Lite EN + Lite KO + Compact EN + Compact KO) вҖ” each gets Migration B Step 1 and Step 2 prefix updates + frontmatter version bump. - **v2.5.32** (2026-06-03) вҖ” **Hyperbrief v0.5.0 вҶ’ v0.5.1 emergency-fix вҖ” clean-install ajv blocker (bundle 007 H1): `mini-engine.cjs` + `mcp/server.cjs` ajv import switched from default draft-07 entrypoint (`require("ajv")`) to draft-2020-12 dialect entrypoint (`require("ajv/dist/2020")`). Determinism PASS re-verified post-fix.** 2-line emergency-fix release. Bundle 007 (Hyperbrief adoption dogfooding from a downstream adopter) surfaced a blocker: `ajv` 8.x default export is the draft-07 dialect, but `hyperbrief.schema.json` declares `"$schema": "https://json-schema.org/draft/2020-12/schema"` вҖ” so `ajv.compile(schema)` throws `no schema with key or ref draft/2020-12/schema` on every IR, breaking the validation-on default code path entirely. The adopter could render only with `--skip-validate`; shipped packages installed via `npm install` could not validate at all. The v0.4.0 determinism smoke test PASSED because it was run with `--skip-validate` against an already-vendored older ajv resolution; clean-install adopters did not have that escape. **The fix** is the 1-line import change per file (Г—2 files: renderers + mcp), with an inline comment explaining why the default draft-07 entrypoint is wrong for this schema's dialect. **Reproduction**: smoke test re-run with real `ajv ^8.17.0` installed in a clean node_modules confirms (a) compile no longer throws, (b) validation-on render proceeds normally, (c) IR-content schema enforcement now catches per-field violations as designed (the test ran against a sample IR with deliberate epistemic-tag gaps, ajv flagged each at correct path); determinism re-verified PASS (`md run1==run2` byte-identical, `html run1==run2` byte-identical вҖ” hashes match v0.5.0 post-button-label baseline). **Why a separate cut rather than folding into v2.5.33/.34**: H1 is a clean-install blocker for every adopter pulling EG @ v2.5.30; folding it into a larger Constellation/Hyperbrief refinement sweep would delay the fix availability. The bundle 007 + bundle 006 absorption sweeps follow as v2.5.33 + v2.5.34. **Hyperbrief frontmatter** `version: v0.5.0 вҶ’ v0.5.1` + status string rewritten to flag the v0.4.0 smoke harness gap (smoke ran with `--skip-validate`, missed this) and the v0.5.1 emergency-fix cut ahead of bundle 007 absorption. **Plugin manifest + sibling package.json** all bump `0.5.0 вҶ’ 0.5.1` (plugin / renderers / mcp). **Scope discipline**: 2-line code change (renderers/mini-engine.cjs + mcp/server.cjs, each 1 import line + a one-line inline comment) + version bumps (1 frontmatter + 3 package.jsons) + this CHANGELOG entry. No schema change. No SKILL.md change. No template change. No reference runtime change. No Constellation.md change. No Superscalar.md change. No docs/promo change. No seed lib change. No wire format change. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” clean-install blocker fix is an emergency-fix patch cut.

Hyperbrief module `frontmatter` v0.4.0 вҶ’ v0.4.1. **В§11.2 externalization**: SSoT body `В§11.2 Dogfood ledger` is rewritten as a layer-separation rationale + a 2-row recent-entries index + pointer; full Entry-01 / Entry-02 rows + per-entry meta-learnings summaries moved to new file `_proposals/006_2026-06-03_hyperbrief/dogfood-ledger.md` (canonical human-readable; bundle-tracked). Optional machine-readable stream `.agent/_decisions/hyperbrief-ledger.jsonl` documented in the SSoT body as the append-only one-row-per-line counterpart (gitignored per EG workspace-cleanliness; reproduce locally as needed). Rationale: spec body and operational telemetry are different layers; mixing them (a) inflates the SSoT body as Entry-N grows beyond ~3 rows, (b) contaminates `git log Hyperbrief.md` with operational noise so spec-change vs ledger-append commits become indistinguishable, (c) destabilizes the file hash external adopters pin against (every Entry adds a hash delta that has nothing to do with normative spec change). **В§9 archive_config layer-separation note added** вҖ” short paragraph clarifying that per-decision `archive_config` (one decision's 5-element bundle) and module-level dogfood ledger (В§11.2 index over all decisions) are distinct layers; both pointer at external files but live at different granularities. **В§10.2 SHOULD-8 new** вҖ” codifies the externalization rule normatively: "Module-level dogfood ledger SHOULD live in an external file, not inside the SSoT body вҖ” keep В§11.2 to a recent-N-row index + pointer; full ledger at `_proposals/<bundle>/dogfood-ledger.md` (human) and/or `.agent/_decisions/<module>-ledger.jsonl` (machine, append-only)." with reason field. **English-normalize prose**: `Hyperbrief.md В§10.3 Phase 1 transition rules` (5 numbered rules + closing paragraph + v0.4.0 status update paragraph) and `В§11.3 Cross-seed adoption` (4 bullet adapter discipline + EstreUF ledger pointer paragraph) rewritten from Korean prose into English prose вҖ” Constellation.md / Superscalar.md convention parity restored (English single-language SSoT for normative body; adopters cite stable English surface). - **v2.5.24** (2026-06-03) вҖ” **Hyperbrief v0.1.1 вҶ’ v0.4.0 вҖ” Phase 2 deterministic renderer shipped (`plugins/hyperbrief/renderers/`: `mini-engine.cjs` self-engineered placeholder substitution + tone-axis transform + canonical IR hash + ajv schema validation, `types.d.ts` interface contract, `bin/render.cjs` CLI entry point, `package.json` declaring single dep `ajv ^8.17.0`). Determinism smoke test PASS (MD/HTML run1 == run2 byte-identical). dogfood Entry 02 archived. MCP tool exposure (`hyperbrief_render`) deferred to v0.4.1.** Phase 2 ship for Hyperbrief module. This cut closes the renderer-absent interval that the v0.1.1 SSoT specified in `В§10.3 Phase 1 transition rules` вҖ” the LLM no longer free-writes MD/HTML; it emits JSON IR only, and the deterministic Node renderer produces the MD/HTML. **4 renderer files** (`plugins/hyperbrief/renderers/`): (1) **`mini-engine.cjs` (~210 LoC)** вҖ” `canonicalIrHash` (stable JSON serialization with sorted keys at every depth вҶ’ same logical IR вҶ’ same hash) + `getValidator` / `validateIr` (ajv lazy load + graceful fallback when ajv not installed) + `substitute` (PLACEHOLDER_RE `\{\{([^}]+)\}\}` + auto-escape per surface) + 3 tone-axis transforms (`applyAudienceTransform` вҖ” L1-L2 epistemic bracket tags вҶ’ Korean word forms `нҷ•мқёлҗЁ / м¶”лЎ  / к°Җм • / лҜёмғҒ`, L4-L5 вҶ’ superscript shorthand `бөӣ вҒұ бөғ бөҳ`; `applyAbbreviationTransform` вҖ” L3 bullet-first, L4+ telegraphic with `vs` `вҶ’` `вҲө` `вҲҙ` symbolic operators; `applyJargonTransform` вҖ” L1-L2 first-occurrence gloss via `JARGON_GLOSS` dict for RAPID / Cynefin / MCDA / Toulmin / blast radius / idempotent / Hyrum) + both `renderMd` / `renderHtml` surfaces + warnings accumulation + `resolveProfile` (override > IR > DEFAULT_PROFILE `{2,2,2}` with 1-5 clamp). (2) **`types.d.ts` (41 LoC)** вҖ” `AudienceProfile` `{audience, abbreviation, jargon: 1|2|3|4|5}` + `AudienceProfileFallback` + `HyperbriefIR` + `RenderResult` `{output, output_hash, ir_hash, audience_profile_applied, warnings[]}` + `RendererOptions` `{audience_profile_override?, self_contained_assets?, skip_validate?}` + `renderMd` / `renderHtml` / `canonicalIrHash` declared signatures + `McpRenderToolInput` for v0.4.1 MCP exposure. (3) **`bin/render.cjs` (~116 LoC)** вҖ” CLI entry point with `--format md|html` В· `--ir <path>` (or stdin) В· `--audience N` В· `--abbreviation N` В· `--jargon N` В· `--self-contained` В· `--skip-validate` В· `--help`; exit codes 0 OK / 1 IR read failure / 2 schema validation failure / 3 unknown format; stderr emits `[warning] <msg>` for non-fatal renderer warnings. (4) **`package.json`** вҖ” name `@hyperbrief/renderers` В· version `0.4.0` В· private В· main `./mini-engine.cjs` В· types `./types.d.ts` В· bin `hyperbrief-render` вҶ’ `./bin/render.cjs` В· single npm dep `ajv ^8.17.0` В· engines `node >=18` В· Apache-2.0. **Determinism smoke test (load-bearing v0.4.0 invariant per В§7)**: rendering the same IR twice produces byte-identical output for both MD and HTML formats (verified вҖ” run1_hash == run2_hash for both surfaces using `bin/render.cjs --skip-validate` smoke harness). **В§10.3 Phase 1 transition rules retained** (NOT deprecated, agent judgment per user delegation "(мһ„мӢң patch лҢҖмІҙ? лҘј м§ҖкёҲ н• м§ҖлҠ” л„Өк°Җ нҢҗлӢЁ.)"): historical record value + external adopters won't migrate immediately so the fallback discipline retains value + preserving Phase 1 operational experience grounds future schema evolution + the drift-log's meaning naturally evolves into "Phase 1 template-substitute output vs Phase 2 renderer output backwards-compat regression verification". Body kept verbatim + one added **v0.4.0 status (2026-06-03 update)** paragraph stating the renderer ship fact and that new briefs after v0.4.0 SHOULD use mini-engine. **Hyperbrief.md frontmatter** v0.1.1 вҶ’ v0.4.0 + status updated ("design draft v0.4.0 (Phase 2 вҖ” deterministic renderer shipped: plugins/hyperbrief/renderers/ mini-engine.cjs + types.d.ts + bin/render.cjs + package.json {dep: ajv ^8.17.0}; В§10.3 Phase 1 transition rules retained with deprecation note)"). **dogfood ledger Entry 02 recorded** вҖ” decision_id `hb-20260603-r2nd02` В· reversibility `one_way_with_migration_path` рҹҹЎ В· outcome accept (alternative B вҖ” self-built mini-engine + ajv + CLI; MCP tool exposure deferred to v0.4.1) В· revisit 2026-09-01 В· archive `_proposals/006_2026-06-03_hyperbrief/dogfood-entry-02.md`. **Entry 02 learnings (3 schema-gap candidates for future patches)**: (1) Declared vs effective `audience_profile` gap вҖ” the IR `audience_profile` is a *declaration* only, with no automated metric for whether the actual surface matches the declared level; root cause of this entry's R1 (declared L2 / effective L3-L4 with excessive English-jargon ratio) вҶ’ R2 (L1/L1/L1 re-render); v0.5 candidate: add `surface_profile_estimate` (auto-computed jargon ratio / English-noun ratio / average sentence length) alongside `epistemic_distribution` + renderer warning when declared vs estimate gap > 1.0. (2) Culture-bound omission in the `trigger_phrases_md` default вҖ” self-reference-style confusion expressions like "мқҙкІҢ level 2 лқјкі ?" missing from the default; continuous learning over user-utterance pattern diversity needed (candidate for automated learning based on adopter feedback ledger telemetry). (3) Missing sub-schema for when `recommended_artifacts[].body` is structured code вҖ” sub-fields like `language` (hint) + `line_count` (cross-check metric) recommended as v0.5 candidates. **AF-22 self-admission cycle** вҖ” at Entry 02 R1 the user uttered "мқҙкІҢ level 2 лқјкі ? н•ңкөӯм–ҙлЎң л¶ҖнғҒн•ҙ" вҶ’ missing from the trigger_phrases_md default вҶ’ AF-22 self-surfaced вҶ’ trigger list reinforced (6 added: `н•ңкөӯм–ҙлЎң`, `н•ңкөӯл§җлЎң`, `level 2 лқјкі `, `L2 лқјкі `, `мқҙкІҢ level`, `мқҙкІҢ L`) вҶ’ R2 (L1/L1/L1) re-render. **MCP tool exposure deferred to v0.4.1** (agent judgment, scope control): creating a new `plugins/hyperbrief/mcp/` directory + writing an MCP server separate from the Constellation MCP server was judged separate work from this cut's minimal core; Constellation-side integration also carries cross-cutting dependency burden. **Scope discipline**: 4 new renderer files + one Hyperbrief.md В§10.3 deprecation-note paragraph + frontmatter version bump + В§11.2 dogfood ledger Entry 02 addition + dogfood-entry-02.md archive.
