- **v2.5.23** (2026-06-03) вҖ” **Hyperbrief v0.1.0 вҶ’ v0.1.1 вҖ” new optional EG module + plugin scaffold (decision-delegation gating discipline). 6-axis deep research workflow synthesis (AI harness / humanities / psychology / management / philosophy / development; 6 parallel agents вҶ’ barrier synth вҶ’ design вҶ’ proposal authoring вҶ’ scaffold; ~861k subagent tokens), self-applied as dogfood Entry 01 with 5 patches landing in v0.1.1.** New top-level module вҖ” `Hyperbrief.md` SSoT (same EG-root tier as Constellation.md / Superscalar.md, governing the orthogonal "agent вҶ’ user decision delegation" axis) + `plugins/hyperbrief/` (3 skills + IR schema + 2 templates + hooks placeholder) + `_proposals/006_2026-06-03_hyperbrief/` bundle (research bilingual + synthesis-and-design bilingual + dogfood-entry-01 archived). **Core thesis** (synthesis): Hyperbrief is a 5-stage pipeline disciplining "the very act of the AI asking the user for a decision" (trigger rubric вҶ’ epistemic honesty вҶ’ cognitive debiasing вҶ’ reversibility-first governance вҶ’ learning loop closure). **JSON IR + deterministic renderer separation** вҖ” the LLM emits only the IR, blocking MD/HTML drift (load-bearing). **В§0 Decision Header** declares escalation 4-score + reversibility class + RAPID + Cynefin + decision_lineage + deadline + reading_minutes + stake + audience_profile (new in v0.1.1). **В§7 Decision Tree** meta-branch (accept / reject_framing / defer / request_investigation) + 3 standardized root nodes (reversibility / blast_radius / time_pressure) + Cynefin-adaptive domain format. **В§10 Normative rules**: 19 MUST + 7 SHOULD. **В§6 Anti-patterns**: 23 AF (16 from v0.1 + 7 new in v0.1.1). **dogfood Entry 01 (self-application)** вҖ” applied the module to the read-through/approval decision for Hyperbrief.md v0.1 itself; the user decision cycle (sum=8/12 вҶ’ FULL_HYPERBRIEF вҶ’ alternative B accept) + 3 follow-up user prompts converted into 5 patches (P1+P2 user-explicit + P3+P4+P5 user-requested refinements) that landed in the v0.1.1 SSoT. **v0.1.1 patches**: (P1) **В§11.3 cross-seed adoption** вҖ” `hb-uf-` / `hb-eg-` decision_id namespaces for EG-seed fork adapters like EstreUF + ledger separation + A2A intent sharing + schema version pinning discipline. (P2) **В§10.3 Phase 1 transition rules** вҖ” operating rules for template-substitute mode during the renderer-absent v0.1.x ~ v0.4.0 window (IR-first invariant retained + template substitution enforced + drift-log telemetry + tone profile applied + self-throttle stays active). (P3) **В§8 recommended_artifacts[] schema slot** (load-bearing) вҖ” closes the structural gap the user surfaced in the first briefing as "patch ліёл¬ёмқҙ м–ҙл”” мһҲм–ҙ?"; mandates an IR slot for the artifact body attached to a recommendation `{artifact_type: patch|spec|code|design|config|other, target_file, target_anchor, body, rationale_one_line}` + MUST-18 + AF-20. (P4) **В§5.6 audience_profile 3 axes Г— 5 levels + В§5.6.7 tone-floor fallback affordance** вҖ” user fed back that the first briefing "м „нҳҖ лҲҲм—җ м•Ҳ л“Өм–ҙмҷҖ" вҶ’ audience (L1 general / L2 general-dev mid default / L3 dev / L4 dev-expert mid / L5 expert-academic) В· abbreviation (L1 full sentences / L2 light compression default / L3 bullet-heavy / L4 telegraphic / L5 spec-density) В· jargon (L1 no jargon / L2 1-line gloss on first use default / L3 free / L4 framework cited / L5 terse citations) 3 orthogonal axes (collapsing into a single complexity score prohibited). **Tone-floor fallback** = always-visible HTML button ("лӯ” мҶҢлҰ¬м•ј? н•ңкөӯм–ҙлЎң лІҲм—ӯн•ҙмӨҳ") + MD trigger phrases (`лӯ” мҶҢлҰ¬`, `м•Ҳ мқҪнҳҖ`, `л¬ҙмҠЁ л§җ`, `мқҙн•ҙ м•Ҳ`, `лҚ” мүҪкІҢ`, `л„Ҳл¬ҙ м–ҙл ө`, `лӢӨмӢң н’Җм–ҙ`, `мүҪкІҢ лӢӨмӢң`, `н•ңкөӯм–ҙлЎң`, `н•ңкөӯл§җлЎң`, `level 2 лқјкі `, `L2 лқјкі `, `мқҙкІҢ level`, `мқҙкІҢ L`) вҖ” re-render at `{1,1,1}` on auto-detection. (P5) **В§9 archive_config** (optional, default ON) вҖ” archives a 5-element bundle (brief_original.md + decision.json + related_user_prompts.md + recommended_artifacts_applied.md + meta_learnings.md) on decision capture; archive_path defaults to `.agent/_decisions/<id>.archive/` or `_proposals/<bundle>/dogfood-entry-NN.md` (proposals-tracked). **Additional anti-patterns**: AF-17 (audience_profile missing/out-of-range) В· AF-18 (surface vocab mismatch profile) В· AF-19 (3 tone axes collapsed) В· AF-20 (recommendation cites artifact but body missing) В· AF-21 (HTML brief without tone-floor button) В· AF-22 (MD brief: user confusion trigger but no regen) В· AF-23 (decision archived but follow-up prompts not captured). **Additional normative rules**: MUST-16 (audience_profile required + 1-5 range) В· MUST-17 (3 axes orthogonality) В· MUST-18 (recommendation artifact disclosure) В· MUST-19 (tone-floor fallback affordance) В· SHOULD-5/6/7 (tone profile chip + abbreviation-aware prose style + jargon-aware glossing). **Workflow synthesis insight** (original draft's 8 sections вҶ’ v0.1.1's 9 sections + IR + 5-stage pipeline): the 6-axis synthesis identified that the original draft's "force MD/HTML form output" pattern induces representation drift вҶ’ evolved into schema-enforced JSON IR + deterministic renderer separation. Redefined the essential function from "help the user make decisions well" to "structurally block the agent from pulling the user into a sycophantic over-delegation loop". **dogfood ledger Entry 01 recorded** вҖ” decision_id `hb-20260603-a1b2c3` В· reversibility `one_way_with_migration_path` рҹҹЎ В· outcome accept (alternative B + 5 patches) В· revisit 2026-09-01 В· archive `_proposals/006_2026-06-03_hyperbrief/dogfood-entry-01.md`. **Renderer (conversion tool) deferred to v2.5.24 (Phase 2 cut)** вҖ” this cut covers through the v0.1.1 SSoT + schema + skills + templates + dogfood archive; deterministic Node renderer (`renderers/`) + MCP tool exposure ship separately. **Scope discipline**: limited to the new module + plugin + proposal bundle. - **v2.5.22** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **constellation plugin v0.2.2 вҶ’ v0.2.3: README "Infrastructure requirements" section added prominently for community-marketplace submission readiness; plugin manifest + marketplace description rewritten to disclose external-WS-server dependency upfront.** Plugin documentation patch вҖ” `plugins/constellation/README.md` gains a new prominent вҡ  section between the intro paragraph and "What this plugin gives you", spelling out the three runtime requirements (WS server at `CONSTELLATION_WS_URL`; state file at `CONSTELLATION_STATE_PATH`; role-keyed auth via `CONSTELLATION_TOKEN` / `_UPSTREAM_KEY` / `_COLLAB_KEY`), explaining what the plugin does WITHOUT a running server (loads clean, skills are docs-only, hook degrades gracefully, MCP tool calls fail with connection errors), and explaining why the architecture chooses external infra over a bundled default server (Constellation is a peer-coordination layer; the WS server holds shared state across agents, so bundling a single-process default server would defeat the multi-agent purpose). The README also adds a `What's in v0.2.3` and a backfilled `What's in v0.2.2` section (the v0.2.2 README sync from v2.5.20 was bundle-only and did not include a release-notes section in the README itself). Plugin manifest (`plugins/constellation/.claude-plugin/plugin.json`) and marketplace entry (`.claude-plugin/marketplace.json`) bump from v0.2.2 to v0.2.3; the marketplace description is rewritten to lead with "Live multi-agent orchestration *client* for Claude Code. Connects to a separately-running Constellation WebSocket server (user-provisioned; canonical reference impl at constellation/reference/runtime/server.cjs in this repo)" so the external-infra requirement is visible in the marketplace UI before install. **Trigger** вҖ” community-marketplace submission readiness research (this session's (c) workstream). Anthropic does not publish an explicit policy on plugins with external infrastructure dependencies, but the official `claude-plugins-official` marketplace already lists multiple precedents (Airtable, MongoDB, PostgreSQL, GitHub, Stripe вҖ” all of which connect to user-managed accounts / services / databases external to the plugin install), and the Claude Code MCP documentation explicitly endorses remote MCP servers (HTTP / SSE / WebSocket) as a standard supported transport. The conclusion is that infrastructure-dependent plugins are accepted; the submission-readiness work is therefore (a) explicit upfront disclosure in README + marketplace description and (b) clear graceful-degradation messaging вҖ” both of which v0.2.3 delivers. **Scope discipline**: plugin documentation + manifest version bumps only. Plugin source code (`mcp/server.cjs`, `hooks/pre-send-probe.cjs`, skills) unchanged. Constellation.md body unchanged. Reference-runtime unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” community-marketplace submission readiness cut.
- **v2.5.21** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.9.1` AgentHello opt-in broadcast presence + `В§13.9.2` canonical-id alias discipline + `В§13.13` layer-split normative clarification for gateway / adapter (Hermes 2nd handoff bundle review reflection).** Spec-body patch вҖ” `Constellation.md` gains two new sub-sections under В§13.9 + one paragraph extending В§13.13 "Layer split" to gateway / adapter implementations. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.18 вҶ’ v2.3.19` + status string gains three new fragments. Reference-runtime unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged. **Trigger** вҖ” 2026-06-01 Hermes 2nd handoff bundle (3 outer files + 9 inner ZIP files, sha256 anchor `2c370bвҖҰ` byte-exact match, byte-verified in v2.5.18 S5 cycle) included three EG-side SSoT reflection asks from its MD section 5 review: explicit ack-semantic ownership rule extended to adapters / gateways (not just bridges), main-agent alias discipline for adopter identity layering, and AgentHello presence as opt-in broadcast rather than required handshake step. **В§13.13 layer-split clarification** вҖ” the existing "bridge does NOT auto-emit `AckProcessed` / `Pong`" prohibition is extended explicitly to "every layer that sits between the agent's active runtime turn and the WS server вҖ” bridges, gateway adapters (Python `websockets`, Discord / Telegram / Slack platform adapters, IPC sidecars, any other proxy / connector / shim)." Discriminator is the owner of the agent-layer commitment signal, not the implementation language; same failure mode applies regardless of layer. **В§13.9.1 AgentHello opt-in broadcast presence** вҖ” strict required handshake is `SERVER_HELLO` + `HELLO`; `AgentHello` is opt-in broadcast presence that (a) declares display metadata and (b) triggers receiver-bridge `OnboardAck` auto-emit. Adopters MAY skip when broadcast presence is undesirable (headless / stealth / telemetry-only / ephemeral debug); skipping yields a working connection without display metadata or auto-OnboardAck-driven worker standby. Discipline: when sent, MUST follow В§2 step 3 wire shape; for `upstream` / `collab` MUST be broadcast (no specific `targetAgentId`); MUST NOT be used as a directed DM to `main-agent` (that misuse drives the alias-confusion failure mode below). Default for autonomous-peer / upstream-adapter implementations is `announce_agent_hello: false`. Constellation reference `local-bridge.cjs` sends by default because its canonical deployment is the interactive local-IDE worker pattern вҖ” that default is a property of the reference implementation, not of the protocol. **В§13.9.2 Canonical-id + alias discipline** вҖ” canonical agentId (sent in `HELLO.agentId`) is the single source of truth for identity at the wire level; server has no built-in alias resolution. Adopters MAY operate aliases (e.g., treat `main-agent` placeholder as an alias for their actual canonical id) handled at the adapter layer. Adopter discipline: inbound target-alias SHOULD route to canonical; inbound source-alias + target-canonical MUST be treated as self-loop and dropped (recursive-wake prevention); outbound traffic MUST stamp canonical id (not alias) at `agentId` / `source`; dashboards SHOULD render `AgentList` rows by canonical id (alias is implementation detail). Named failure mode prevented: **alias-confusion** вҖ” an adapter treating `main-agent` as a separate peer, sending `AgentHello` as DM to it, receiving auto-`OnboardAck` for an identity that does not exist, with the live-board UI rendering the same agent twice (canonical + alias) and no error surface. **Scope discipline**: spec-body patch only (~3 paragraphs in В§13.13 + two new sub-sections in В§13.9 + frontmatter version bump + status string). Reference-runtime unchanged (existing `local-bridge.cjs` continues to behave as-is; the В§13.9.1 default-send is preserved as the reference's deployment choice). Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” Hermes-feedback-driven SSoT clarification is a minor cut.
- **v2.5.20** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.16.9` A2A-intent allowlist extension + doubly-wrapped envelope inner-name fallback in `pre-send-probe.cjs` (plus constellation plugin v0.2.1 вҶ’ v0.2.2 bundle sync).** Reference-runtime patch вҖ” `constellation/reference/runtime/stop-hook/pre-send-probe.cjs` + bundled copy at `plugins/constellation/hooks/pre-send-probe.cjs`. **ALLOWLIST extension** вҖ” five new A2A-intent names added: `Request` / `Reply` (generic ask/respond envelopes used in cross-agent S4-style coordination), `Attachment` (standalone attachment metadata envelope per the Hermes 2026-06-01 11:09-11:11 UTC pattern), and `ArtifactManifest` / `ArtifactComplete` (chunked-transfer anchors per В§13.11 rule 5; `ArtifactChunk` deliberately excluded as high-volume reassembly state rather than meaningful agent-layer signal). **Inner-name fallback** вҖ” the probe now also checks `value.name` for doubly-wrapped envelopes where the outer `name` field carries the literal string `"CUSTOM"` rather than the MessageName. This was observed in the 2026-06-02 Hermes meta-ack at inbox line 22856 and again at line 22858: Hermes-side envelope construction stamps `type: "CUSTOM"` at the outer name level and the actual MessageName (`Reply` or `Report`) at `value.name`. Without the fallback the cycle-end probe missed these envelopes entirely. The fallback is conservative: it only matches when the outer name is exactly `"CUSTOM"` (or absent) AND the inner name is in the allowlist вҖ” well-formed envelopes are unaffected. **Constellation plugin v0.2.2** absorbs the bundled probe-script update (no other plugin changes). **Scope discipline**: reference-runtime patch only (~10 lines added to `pre-send-probe.cjs` + bundled copy + plugin manifest version bumps in `plugins/constellation/.claude-plugin/plugin.json` and `.claude-plugin/marketplace.json`). Constellation.md body unchanged (В§13.16.9 specifies the 4-group classification at a high level; the script implementation's specific allowlist is operational, extended in lockstep with discovered envelope patterns). Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” user-directed allowlist extension is a minor cut.
- **v2.5.19** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.13.2` v0.5 reference impl bug fixes вҖ” server.cjs `_relayPendingClear` queue-key fix + local-bridge.cjs `delivered-persist` emit gated on `RELAY_REDELIVERY=on`.** Reference-runtime patch вҖ” `constellation/reference/runtime/server.cjs` + `constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs`. Constellation.md body unchanged (v0.5 contract codified in v2.5.17 is correct; this version fixes implementation defects in the v2.5.15 reference). Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged. **Trigger** вҖ” 2026-06-02 dogfood on the hub: main found that its v2.5.15-derived `server.cjs._relayPendingClear` was looking up the wrong queue (key = `tgt` = `AckProcessed.targetAgentId` = original *sender* of the acked message, not the queue key which is the *recipient* = the AckProcessed *sender*). Pre-fix the lookup silently missed every commitment-tier clear, so even normal v0.5 first-receipt envelopes accumulated pending entries that aged into redelivery вҶ’ false `RelayUnreachable{commitment-ack-absent}`. Main fixed the equivalent line on its own server and the dogfood subsequently passed (see v2.5.17 changelog). Main observed the EG reference `server.cjs` has the same line shape and recommended the same fix. Main also flagged a second issue: the EG bridge emitted `AckProcessed{tier:delivered-persist}` unconditionally, even with `RELAY_REDELIVERY=off`, producing board noise when the server's pending queue was dormant; main's own bridge gated the emit by `process.env.RELAY_REDELIVERY === 'on'`. Both fixes are bundled in v2.5.19. **server.cjs fix** (~line 442-445): the AckProcessed inbound branch's pending-clear call changes from `_relayPendingClear(tgt, msg.value.ackFor)` to `_relayPendingClear(conn.meta.agentId, msg.value.ackFor)` вҖ” `conn.meta.agentId` is the AckProcessed *sender* (= the original *recipient* of the acked message = the queue key under which the pending entry was registered). A multi-line code comment now records the bug and the fix rationale at the call site. **local-bridge.cjs fix** (~line 136, the v2.5.18 `delivered-persist` emit branch): the condition `appended && m.msgId && !_BRIDGE_ACK_KINDS.has(m.name)` gains a leading `process.env.RELAY_REDELIVERY === 'on'` gate. With redelivery off, no pending entry needs clearing and the emit is pure board noise; the gate prevents noise without changing v0.5 correctness when the redelivery scheduler is active. **В§13.15 syntax gate**: `node --check` passes on both files. **Scope discipline**: reference-runtime patch only (~12 lines net change in server.cjs + ~3 lines net change in local-bridge.cjs, both inside existing branches). Constellation.md unchanged (v0.5 contract is correct; this is implementation hygiene). Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” main-authorised reference-impl bug-fix cut.
- **v2.5.18** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.13.2` v0.5 reference implementation вҖ” bridge inbox-append commitment hook (EG-side complement to v2.5.17 spec).** Reference-runtime patch вҖ” `constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs` `onInbound` gains a `delivered-persist` emit after successful inbox-append; В§13.13.2 header comment updated to v0.4/v0.5 evolution. Constellation.md body unchanged (v0.5 spec already codified in v2.5.17). Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged (the `tier` field added per v2.5.17 spec is optional and back-compatible). **Trigger**: v2.5.17 spec patch ships the v0.5 contract; this version is the EG-side bridge reference implementation. Main's own bridge (`ws-local-bridge.cjs`) was updated independently and shipped at PID 437484 ahead of EG; this commit is the EG-repo complement so adopters cloning the canonical reference runtime get the v0.5 behaviour. **local-bridge.cjs change** (~20 lines inside `onInbound`, between the existing dedup branch at line 109 and the AgentHello auto-handler): on every CUSTOM inbound that passes dedup AND carries a `msgId` AND is NOT in `_BRIDGE_ACK_KINDS` (`Ack` / `AckProcessed` / `Ping` / `Pong` вҖ” never ack-the-ack), AND whose inbox.jsonl append succeeded, emit `CUSTOM/AckProcessed { ackFor: msgId, tier: "delivered-persist" }` targeted at the original sender (resolved as `m.agentId || m.value.agentId`, identical to the existing dedup-emit path). The emit composes with the v0.4 LRU dedup at line 109: duplicates emit `dedupHit:true` (v0.4 path, no `delivered-persist`); first-receipts emit `delivered-persist` (v0.5 path); the two never collide. **What this does NOT change**: the agent-layer application-tier ack discipline (`Report` / `DONE` / `BLOCKED` per В§13.13) remains agent-emitted on its own dimension; the v0.5 `delivered-persist` ack lives on the *delivery* dimension and is bridge-emitted on its own authority. An agent that ALSO emits a v0.4-style commitment-tier `AckProcessed` is still spec-compliant вҖ” the server observes the pending entry already cleared by `delivered-persist` and treats the commitment ack as informational. **В§13.15 syntax gate**: `node --check constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs` passes. **Scope discipline**: reference-runtime patch only (~20 lines added to local-bridge.cjs + ~9-line comment update on the В§13.13.2 dedup block). Constellation.md unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” main-authorised v0.5 reference impl is a minor cut.
- **v2.5.17** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.13.2` v0.4 вҶ’ v0.5 spec patch вҖ” bridge inbox-append commitment + `delivered-persist` ack subtier (eliminates false-positive `RelayUnreachable{commitment-ack-absent}`).** Spec-body patch вҖ” `Constellation.md` В§13.13.2 sub-section header bumped from `(v0.4 draft)` to `(v0.5)` + three new paragraphs (g) bridge inbox-append commitment + (h) tier-semantics vocabulary table + (i) migration path v0.4 вҶ’ v0.5. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.17 вҶ’ v2.3.18` + status line gains `at-least-once relay reliability v0.5 (В§13.13.2 вҖ” bridge inbox-append commitment)`. Reference implementation ships separately as v2.5.18 EG-side complement. Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged (optional `tier` field added to `AckProcessed.value`, back-compatible). **Trigger** вҖ” 2026-06-02 dogfood: relay RRP В§13.13.2 v0.4 hub adoption immediately after v2.5.15 ship surfaced a false-positive class вҖ” a normal `Ack` from EG вҶ’ main was redelivered 3Г— вҶ’ `RelayUnreachable{commitment-ack-absent}` despite the body having reached main's inbox file on the first attempt, because main's agent layer did not happen to emit a commitment-tier `AckProcessed` for it (agent idle / processing unrelated work). Main paused redelivery to OFF gate (`RELAY_REDELIVERY=off`) + proposed v0.5: bridge emits the commitment ack on its own authority immediately after inbox-append, since the bridge owns the persistence guarantee and the agent layer's commitment is properly an *outcome* signal not a *delivery* signal. EG agreed with all five arguments (false-positive removal В· bridge always alive В· v0.4 LRU dedup composes В· agent layer keeps application-tier ack only В· inbox-append IS the at-least-once anchor); main implemented main bridge v0.5 + restarted (PID 437484) + granted EG autonomous authority to ship spec patch + EG-side reference impl. **В§13.13.2 (g) Bridge inbox-append commitment** вҖ” codifies the v0.5 contract: every successful inbound `CUSTOM` body that the recipient's bridge appends to its inbox file MUST be followed within milliseconds by `AckProcessed { ackFor: msgId, tier: "delivered-persist" }` emitted to the sender. Bridge does NOT wait for agent layer to read or process; the moment the body is durably persisted, the bridge has fulfilled its half of the at-least-once contract. Server treats `tier:"delivered-persist"` as the canonical pending-queue clear trigger, semantically equivalent to v0.4's commitment-tier ack but emitted by the transport layer that actually owns the persistence guarantee. **В§13.13.2 (h) Tier semantics** вҖ” v0.5 distinguishes three named tiers with explicit emitter/trigger/pending-clear columns: `delivered` (server-emitted, wire received, no pending clear) В· `delivered-persist` (bridge-emitted, inbox-append complete, canonical pending clear) В· `commitment` (agent-emitted, body surfaced into working context, redundant after `delivered-persist`). Application-tier outcomes (`Report` / `DONE` / `BLOCKED` per В§13.13) live on a separate outcome dimension; v0.4 `AckProcessed` without `tier` field is interpreted as `commitment` for back-compat (a v0.4 receiver paired with v0.5 server continues to operate at v0.4 semantics, including the false-positive class вҖ” the escape requires the v0.5 *bridge*). **В§13.13.2 (i) Migration path** вҖ” per-component update: server gains "delivered-persist clears pending entry" rule (additive over v0.4 commitment-tier clear) + optional per-target `RELAY_REDELIVERY=off` gate (operators disable redelivery while v0.5 bridges roll out); bridge adds inbox-append hook with immediate `delivered-persist` emit (composes with v0.4 В§13.13.2(c) LRU dedup вҖ” duplicates still emit `AckProcessed{ackFor, dedupHit:true}` without inbox-append, so no `delivered-persist` for duplicates); agent unchanged (mechanism is bridge-layer, invisible to agent code). **Empirical validation** вҖ” 2026-06-02 dogfood with main-EG bidirectional: main's bridge added the hook + restart (PID 437484) + the next EG вҶ’ main envelope cleared pending in <1s without redelivery or `RelayUnreachable`. EG-side reference impl (the v2.5.18 ship) is the EG bridge complement. **Scope discipline**: spec-body patch only (~3 paragraphs added to В§13.13.2 sub-section + header version bump + frontmatter). Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged (optional `tier` field added to `AckProcessed.value` is back-compatible per В§13.13 вҖ” receivers and intermediate proxies that ignore the field continue to function at v0.4 semantics). Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” main-authorised v0.5 spec patch is a minor cut.
- **v2.5.16** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **`docs/promo/` вҖ” EstreGenesis + Superscalar + Constellation public promo site (GitHub Pages publishable; bilingual EN/KO + theme switcher).** (See KO block for details вҖ” this is the same v2.5.16 entry already codified below; full English entry was earlier folded under the v2.5.16 polish cut.)
- **v2.5.15** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.13.2` v0.4 reference implementation вҖ” server pending queue + redelivery scheduler + RelayUnreachable emit + bridge LRU dedup with `dedupHit:true` AckProcessed.** Reference-runtime patch вҖ” `constellation/reference/runtime/server.cjs` + `constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs`. Constellation.md body unchanged (the В§13.13.2 contract codified in v2.5.11 is the spec; this version is its reference implementation per the В§13.13.2 Phase 2 deferred-list). Seed lib unchanged. Triggered by user instruction ("л°”лЎң м§„н–үн•ҳм§Җ?"). **server.cjs additions** (`constellation/reference/runtime/server.cjs` ~lines 155-200 + relay branch): **(a) Pending queue** вҖ” `_relayPending` Map keyed by `targetAgentId`, FIFO per-target with cap `RELAY_PENDING_MAX=256` (env-overridable). Each entry `{ msgId, payload, firstAt, attempts, hasEmbeddedAttachment }`. Entries register on the relay branch whenever `wsIsAckable(msg)` returns true AND the target is connected вҖ” same gate as the transport-tier `Ack delivered` emit; the v0.3 baseline already filtered ack/ping/telemetry out of the pending track. **(b) Commitment-tier clear on AckProcessed** вҖ” when a `CUSTOM/AckProcessed` envelope is relayed with `value.ackFor` matching a pending entry's msgId AND a `targetAgentId` matching the original target, `_relayPendingClear(tgt, ackFor)` removes the entry. This is the key inversion vs v0.3: pending is cleared by commitment-tier ack (agent layer), NOT by transport-tier `Ack delivered` (server layer). **(c) Redelivery scheduler** вҖ” `setInterval(_relayScheduleTick, 10*1000)` scans pending entries every 10s; an entry past `RELAY_THRESHOLD_MS` (default 30s dogfood / 5min prod вҖ” env-overridable) AND recipient AgentList-present AND attempts < max вҶ’ redeliver via `d.send(payload)` + increment attempts + reset firstAt. Recipient-absent вҶ’ defer redelivery until reconnect. Max-attempts hit вҶ’ emit `RelayUnreachable { msgId, targetAgentId, attemptCount, lastError }` to the **sender** (not broadcast вҖ” only the sender needs to know its message did not stick) + clear pending entry. The sender then escalates to human review per В§13.13 application-tier ladder. **(d) В§13.11 rule 5 attachment-aware throttle** вҖ” entries carrying `value.attachments[]` with any `source: "embedded"` (or any `dataUrl` field) attachment use `Math.ceil(max_attempts / 2)` as the effective cap (default 3 вҶ’ 2 for embedded). Duplicate large payload redelivery is bandwidth-expensive + the receiver's msgId dedup catches it on first redelivery anyway; the throttle is the cost-asymmetry response. **(e) Scheduler unref'd** (`.unref()`) вҖ” does not keep the Node event loop alive past server shutdown. **local-bridge.cjs additions** (`constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs` ~lines 75-104): **(f) LRU dedup with TTL** вҖ” `_seenMsgIds` upgraded from unbounded `Set` to `Map(msgId вҶ’ seen-ts)` with `_SEEN_LRU_MAX=1024` entries + `_SEEN_TTL_MS=1h` per В§13.13.2 v0.4 provisional defaults. `_dedupCheck(msgId)` performs TTL evict from oldest (Map insertion-order iteration is JS spec) + LRU evict on cap + insert/refresh. Returns true on duplicate. **(g) `dedupHit: true` AckProcessed emit** вҖ” when `_dedupCheck` returns true, the bridge emits `CUSTOM/AckProcessed { ackFor: <msgId>, dedupHit: true }` targeted at the original sender agent (`m.agentId || m.value.agentId`) + discards the body (no inbox.jsonl append, no agent layer surface). The sender's server-side `_relayPending` entry then clears via path (b) above. Without `dedupHit` emit, redelivery would loop indefinitely until max-attempts (RelayUnreachable false-alarm); with `dedupHit` emit, redelivery is server-side mechanic invisible to the agent layer (correct В§13.13.2 semantic). **Env-overridable knobs**: `RELAY_PENDING_MAX` (default 256) В· `RELAY_THRESHOLD_MS` (default 30000 = 30s; prod adopters set to 300000 = 5min) В· `RELAY_MAX_ATTEMPTS` (default 3). Scheduler scan interval is hardcoded at 10s (sub-threshold; tunable in code). **What v2.5.15 does NOT add** (still В§13.13.2 Phase 3 candidates): durable pending queue (in-memory only; server restart loses pending state вҖ” acceptable for dogfood, prod adopters add persistence) В· cross-server pending state (single-server scope) В· telemetry sink for redelivery/dedup-hit/RelayUnreachable rate calibration (logged via `console.warn` only) В· per-target backpressure (a slow recipient just accumulates pending up to cap then FIFO-evicts oldest). **Composition tested**: PR #4/PR #5 trace would now also clear server pending on the manual fast-path PRMergeAck (which is application-tier, not commitment) вҖ” Phase 3 may add explicit application-tier pending clear OR rely on max-attempts timeout. For now, application-tier outcomes do NOT auto-clear pending (only commitment-tier does); long-running tasks should emit AckProcessed at acceptance time. **Scope discipline**: reference-runtime patch only (~70 lines added to server.cjs + ~25 lines added to local-bridge.cjs). Constellation.md body unchanged (В§13.13.2 spec already codified at v2.5.11). Seed lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged (server-side state keyed by existing `msgId` field per v0.4 contract). Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” user-directed Phase 2 reference impl is a minor cut.
- **v2.5.14** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **A2A PR System RRP v0.3 вҶ’ v0.4 DRAFT: `В§10B Manual fast-path` codified (trusted-mirror short-circuit, PR #4 + PR #5 dogfood validation, dry-run draftRef consistency gate).** RRP-only patch вҖ” `constellation/reference/docs/2026-06-01-a2a-pr-system-rrp.md` body augmentation (new В§10B sub-section between В§10A and В§11; v0.3 вҶ’ v0.4 banner; status preamble updated). Constellation.md body unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Protocol wire unchanged. **Trigger**: 2026-06-01 dogfood вҖ” PR #4 (`a3344d7`, В§13.11 rule 5 + В§13.13.2 RRP mirror, 40 ins) + PR #5 (`1e2c3f9`, В§13.16.12 Pattern 7 mirror, 19 ins) both completed via a **single-envelope manual short-circuit** (PRRequest dry-run вҶ’ PRMergeAck) rather than the В§9/В§10A canonical six-envelope chain (PRRequest + PRDraftReadyГ—2 + PRRequest re-emit + PRReviewAck + PRMergeRequest + PRMergeAck). Main acknowledged the pattern + user authorised codification ("user decision to register d-pr-manual-fastpath + EG autonomous RRP permitted + redaction grep + dry-run draftRef consistency gate as mandatory codification conditions"). **В§10B contract** (six sub-sections): **В§10B.1 e2e diagram** of the short-circuit (PRRequest{dryRun:true} вҶ’ bridge handlePrRequestL1 dry-run вҶ’ PRDraftReady{dryRun:true, draftRef:'dryrun-<msgId>', checksPending:[]} вҶ’ main manual `git append + add <targetPath> + commit + push origin main` вҶ’ PRMergeAck{merged:true, dryRun:false, commit:<sha>, pushSuccess:true, draftRef:<dryrun consistent>, forMsgId:<msgId>}); collapses 8 envelopes (chain) to 2 envelopes (fast-path); operator's manual git step replaces the chain's PRReviewAck+PRMergeRequest+cherry-pick+push steps. **В§10B.2 redundancy cost analysis** вҖ” table mapping each chain step's information contribution; PRReviewAck adds no new information for trusted-mirror (single-file append, redaction grep already in dry-run); the chain's redundancy is intentional for standard PRs (cross-cutting impact catch) but pure cost for trusted-mirror. Fast-path saves 6 envelopes + PR_LIVE state toggle. **В§10B.3 use-criteria** (ALL required): category=trusted-mirror В· kind=inline-section-mirror В· mergeStrategy=append-section В· single target file В· dry-run draftRef present + consistent in PRMergeAck В· redaction grep clean at dry-run В· per-PR operator manual review. **В§10B.4 do-NOT-use** for: standard/branch-ref/inline-files-diff PRs В· multi-file В· non-append-section mergeStrategy В· shared mutable state (state.json/config/schema) В· first-time adopter (loses dogfood signal). **В§10B.5 dry-run draftRef consistency gate** (load-bearing invariant) вҖ” PRMergeAck.draftRef MUST match PRDraftReady.draftRef from the dry-run; without this, fast-path PRMergeAck is indistinguishable from an unauthenticated merge claim (anyone could synthesize merge confirmation). Bridge emits `dryrun-<msgId>` deterministically; main MUST carry verbatim. PR #4 trace: msgId `m-<id>` вҶ’ draftRef `dryrun-constellatio-m-<id>` (dry-run) вҶ’ same draftRef in PRMergeAck (manual merge). Verifiable from inbox.log alone. **В§10B.6 composition** with В§6 approval discipline (trusted-mirror per-PR opt-in still in force) + В§13.14 redaction discipline (dry-run grep load-bearing) + В§13.13.2 dedup (msgId-keyed; fast-path inherits dedup property) + В§13.16.10 pre-send probe (operator's manual append step is preceded by their own probe) + В§13.16.12 board render (PRMergeAck renders as A2A card; manual git ops are out-of-band side channel, acceptable). **В§10B.7 dogfood evidence** вҖ” PR #4 + PR #5 two-case anchor table (both trusted-mirror, single-file append-section, dry-run clean, manual append+push, PRMergeAck draftRef consistent, zero regressions vs chain). **В§10B.8 what fast-path does NOT codify** вҖ” single-axis short-circuit only; does not change wire vocabulary, approval discipline category enum, redaction discipline, dedup mechanic, or operator's manual review responsibility. Fast-path is *easier* not *less rigorous*. **Status preamble** (top of RRP): v0.3 вҶ’ v0.4 + new banner line crediting В§10B addition + PR #4/PR #5 dogfood + load-bearing dry-run draftRef invariant. **Version**: v0.4 DRAFT (2026-06-02). **Scope discipline**: RRP-only patch (~120 lines added). Constellation.md body unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Protocol wire unchanged. Manual fast-path is a *delivery-side discipline*, not a wire-format change. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” user-authorised RRP body augmentation cut.
- **v2.5.13** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.16.12 Pattern 7` вҖ” board render TEXT_MESSAGE fallback to A2A card (defense layer for non-conformant adopters).** Constellation patch вҖ” body-only augmentation (new pattern added to existing В§13.16.12 sub-section under В§13.16), no wire-format change, no seed cascade. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.16 вҶ’ v2.3.17` + status string gains `board render TEXT_MESSAGE fallback (В§13.16.12 Pattern 7)`. **Trigger**: 2026-06-01 dogfood вҖ” Hermes Dev Agent's ws_agent_client.py was diagnosed (main-side, sub-user-instruction inspection of `ws-history/hermes-dev-agent.jsonl`, ~200 lines) to emit ALL outbound A2A as `TEXT_MESSAGE` envelopes carrying serialized JSON in `.text` rather than structured `CUSTOM` envelopes with `value` + `attachments[]`. The Hermes side's R2 pending finding (ws_agent_client.py validation) confirmed at the byte level. Main shipped a render-tier defense layer at commit `5983f57` (app.js `wsExtractA2aReport` helper + TEXT_MESSAGE branch that promotes serialized JSON code blocks into `a2acard` rendering, Playwright-verified). User authorised the formalisation as a В§13.16.12 Pattern 7 candidate; this version codifies it at the protocol tier so other Constellation adopters running similar implementations get the same defense layer. **Pattern 7 contract**: receiver-side dashboard MAY detect TEXT_MESSAGE envelopes whose `text` carries a serialized A2A Report (typically a `[A2A Report]` lead line followed by a fenced JSON code block with `{ type: "Report", ... }`) and **promote** the message into an A2A card render вҖ” extracting the JSON payload, parsing it, and rendering as if it had arrived as a native CUSTOM envelope. Implementation discipline: (1) detection runs as a `TEXT_MESSAGE` branch, after the normal text render is computed but before DOM commit; if extraction succeeds, surface swaps to A2A card; if extraction fails, message renders as normal TEXT_MESSAGE (graceful degradation, never errors loudly). (2) Promoted card MUST carry a `fallback` visual badge (small label or tooltip "promoted from TEXT_MESSAGE") so the operator can distinguish a canonical CUSTOM-rendered card from a Pattern-7-promoted card вҖ” preserves audit-trail integrity and surfaces which adopters remain non-conformant. (3) Promotion MUST NOT alter the outbound ack path (transport-tier Ack continues against the original TEXT_MESSAGE frame; commitment-tier AckProcessed follows В§13.13 normally; promotion is render-layer only). (4) Promotion MUST extract `attachments[]` from the JSON when present + render chips per В§13.11 rule 5 + Pattern 3 graceful-localPath discipline (Pattern 7 supplies the parsed array; Pattern 3 supplies the per-chip render discipline). **Composition**: В§13.11.3 rule 1 (server stamps `type: "CUSTOM"` when absent) handles the *type-omitted* case; Pattern 7 handles the stronger *wrong-envelope-shape* case (sender wrapped the whole envelope into TEXT_MESSAGE). Pattern 6 (source-set-agnostic detection + text relay fallback) handles the *router*-side defect; Pattern 7 handles the *render*-side complement (TEXT_MESSAGE correctly routed but wrongly shaped). With the В§13.16.10 pre-send probe: Pattern 7 promotion does NOT alter cursor advancement; Pattern-7-promoted cards count as meaningful inbound and the watcher / pre-send probe's A2A-intent allowlist SHOULD treat TEXT_MESSAGE-Pattern-7-detected as meaningful for adopters running the fallback. **Lifecycle expectation**: Pattern 7 is a **transitional defense layer**. Adopters view Pattern 7 hits as a backlog signal (each promoted card = an instance of a non-conformant producer needing fix). Discipline target: *zero Pattern 7 hits* over a steady operating window. When all adopters emit structured envelopes per В§13.11, Pattern 7 becomes dormant but is NOT removed вҖ” it protects against regression. **Reference implementation**: upstream commit `5983f57` (app.js `wsExtractA2aReport` helper + TEXT_MESSAGE branch). The dashboard-render-patterns.md reference doc may grow a В§9 "TEXT_MESSAGE-to-A2A-card fallback" section in a future revision to mirror this protocol-tier addition. **Scope discipline**: Constellation.md body augmentation only (one new pattern in existing В§13.16.12 sub-section). Wire format unchanged (Pattern 7 is render-tier behavior вҖ” wire still emits TEXT_MESSAGE from the non-conformant producer; the receiver-side promotion is a render-layer recovery). Seed lib unchanged. `dashboard-render-patterns.md` reference doc unchanged in v2.5.13. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” user-authorised defense-layer protocol body augmentation cut.

- **v2.5.11** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.13.2` at-least-once relay reliability RRP draft (server pending queue + redelivery + idempotent receiver dedup; v0.4 contract).** Constellation patch вҖ” body-only augmentation (new sub-section under В§13.13), no wire-format shape change (server-side state keyed by existing `msgId` field; no envelope additions), no seed cascade. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.15 вҶ’ v2.3.16` + status string gains `at-least-once relay reliability v0.4 draft (В§13.13.2)`. **Trigger**: 2026-06-01 dogfood surfaced **3 relay-drop incidents within one cycle** (a24c5897 Hermes morning drop В· Hermes 2nd handoff localPath drop В· Hermes transport-mode negotiation drop), reaching the escalation threshold codified in `memory/feedback_a2a_relay_reliability.md` (1 cycle / 3 drops = RRP). Main acknowledged the threshold + user authorised the RRP (line 22765, 2026-06-01 15:20 UTC вҖ” "EG мһҗмңЁ м§„н–ү OK + мӢңм җ мЎ°мңЁ"). **The v0.4 contract** (additive, layered on top of v0.3 вҖ” wire envelope unchanged): **(a) Server-side pending queue** вҖ” server retains pending `{ msgId, targetAgentId, payload-hash, first-attempt-ts, attempt-count }` entry per targeted CUSTOM with msgId, FIFO per-target, default cap 256 entries / 30 min. Cleared on commitment-tier `AckProcessed` (NOT transport-tier `Ack delivered` вҖ” key inversion vs v0.3). **(b) Redelivery policy** вҖ” re-emit when first-attempt-ts exceeds threshold (default 5 min production / 30s dogfood вҖ” adopters tune). Bounded by attempt-count (max 3) AND recipient connection state (skip if not AgentList-present; defer until reconnect). After max attempts вҶ’ `RelayUnreachable { msgId, targetAgentId, attemptCount, lastError }` emitted to the SENDER (not broadcast) + pending entry cleared. Sender escalates to human review via board `decisions` panel per В§13.13 application-tier ladder. **(c) Idempotent receiver dedup** вҖ” bridge maintains seen-msgId LRU (default 1024 / 1 hour); duplicate msgId вҶ’ emit `AckProcessed { ackFor, dedupHit: true }` immediately + discard duplicate body. Without dedup, redelivery would surface N copies; with it, redelivery is server-side mechanic invisible to the agent layer (except via the `dedupHit: true` flag for outcome tracking). **(d) Composition with v0.3 ack tiers** вҖ” three tiers preserved verbatim (transport В· commitment В· application); v0.4 changes WHEN server clears pending (commitment, not transport) + adds redelivery-on-absence-of-commitment that v0.3 lacks. Back-compatible: an adopter that has not migrated continues at-most-once; the wire requires no new fields (msgId already exists per v0.3 В§13.13). **(e) Composition with В§13.11 rule 5 attachment transport-mode** вҖ” embedded attachments raise redelivery cost; redelivery SHOULD apply attachment-aware throttle (half the standard max attempts for envelopes with `source: "embedded"` entries, since duplicate large payloads are bandwidth-expensive). Chunked transfer (`ArtifactManifest`/`ArtifactChunk`/`ArtifactComplete`) is independently idempotent at chunk level + does NOT participate in msgId pending queue at chunk granularity. **(f) Composition with broker-forward workaround** вҖ” the workaround codified in `memory/feedback_a2a_relay_reliability.md` (extract from main `ws-history/<sender-agentId>.jsonl` and forward to recipient) remains a valid manual escalation path even after v0.4 ships, for cases where pending queue exceeds cap or recipient stays disconnected past `RelayUnreachable`. Broker-forward emit carries original msgId, so recipient seen-msgId set deduplicates against the original delivery attempt вҖ” workaround does NOT bypass v0.4 dedup. **Phase 1 ship (this version)**: contract codified. **Phase 2 (v2.5.12+)**: reference implementation (server.cjs pending queue + redelivery scheduler + bridge dedup LRU) вҖ” sequenced after Hermes dataUrl reemit catch + Mode B baseline absorption per user-confirmed time scheduling. Provisional defaults (queue cap 256 В· redelivery threshold 5min/30s В· max attempts 3 В· dedup-LRU 1024/1h) expect tuning after 1-2 weeks of v0.4 telemetry. **Scope discipline**: Constellation.md body augmentation only (one new sub-section under В§13.13). Wire shape unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Hub mirror via A2A PR #4 (per main's "PRRequest мӢң н—ҲлёҢ WS-PROTOCOL.md mirror" cadence) is a separate follow-up. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” meaningful protocol body augmentation + user-authorised RRP cut.
- **v2.5.10** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.11 rule 5` attachment transport-mode discipline (`source` enum `local_path | embedded | url | chunked` + standard attachment-object fields + ack-tier semantics + Hermes-EG convergent ship).** Constellation patch вҖ” body-only augmentation, no wire-format shape change (attachment-object fields are additive), no seed cascade. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.14 вҶ’ v2.3.15` + status string gains `attachment transport-mode v0.4 (В§13.11 rule 5)`. New В§13.11 rule 5 closes the cross-environment byte-transport gap surfaced by the Hermes 2nd handoff bundle (inbox lines 22702-22709, 2026-06-01 11:09-11:11 UTC) where `source: "local_path"` attachments did NOT transport bytes across the A2A gateway boundary (provenance metadata only вҖ” receivers cannot fetch the sender's local filesystem), producing a ~10-hour awareness delay + bodyPreview-only consolidation in v2.5.6. **Rule 5 specifies the `source` enum** (`local_path` = sender-filesystem provenance only В· `embedded` = dataUrl base64-encoded bytes вүӨ24 MB practical inline payload, canonical default for cross-environment handoffs В· `url` = external-hosted with signed/token-gated fetch for >24 MB or TTL-controlled artifacts В· `chunked` = multi-message ArtifactManifest + ArtifactChunk + ArtifactComplete sequence for very large or retry-required transfers) + **standard attachment-object fields** (`name` В· `mime` В· `size` В· `sha256` В· `source` В· `path` for sender-local provenance В· `dataUrl`/`url`/`chunks[]` per source-type) + **hybrid embedded form** (canonical default: BOTH `path` (sender-local provenance/debug) AND `dataUrl` (authoritative transported bytes), receiver treats `dataUrl` as bytes source and `path` as metadata-only). Server MAX_BODY = 32 MB; base64 overhead ~33% means practical inline payload вүӨ24 MB. **Convergent ship coordination**: Hermes Dev Agent + EG converged on rule 5 independently during the 2026-06-01 dogfood cycle. EG outbox 295 (14:35 UTC) proposed four transport-mode options with `(d) hybrid` as the recommendation; Hermes line 199 (~15:00 UTC, forwarded by main-broker since the at-most-once relay dropped the substantive Report вҖ” recurrence of the relay-drop class observed earlier in the day, surfaced as a separate В§13.x agenda item for at-least-once relay semantics) accepted `(d) hybrid localPath + dataUrl, source=embedded` as default for future handoffs and explicitly agreed to the В§13.11 rule 5 codification ship at v2.5.10. **Ack-tier semantics for embedded attachments**: В§13.13 transport-tier `Ack` = "envelope delivered to recipient's WS connection" (does NOT separately confirm decode or sha256-verify); commitment-tier `AckProcessed` SHOULD mean "received + decoded + sha256-verified + persisted" per receiver policy; application-tier (`Report` / `DONE`) carries the outcome of using the attachment (archive update, byte-verification pass/fail, regeneration request). Composes with В§13.13 3-tier mapping without introducing a new tier. **Cross-link to В§13.16.12 Pattern 3**: dashboard render-tier already specifies graceful localPath display (chip with "local file, not transported" indicator vs error/broken-link); rule 5 is the protocol-tier counterpart that Pattern 3's visualisation reflects. The two compose: В§13.11 rule 5 = wire contract, В§13.16.12 Pattern 3 = render contract. **Hermes reemit in-progress**: Hermes is verifying `/tmp/hermes` artifact presence and will either reemit the 2nd handoff bundle in the embedded form (md 9384B + diff patch 1811B + tar.gz 262KB as three `source: "embedded"` attachments with dataUrl + sha256) or surface artifact-missing fallback to operator/regeneration. EG-side will byte-decode + sha256-verify against HANDOFF-MANIFEST.json on receipt and update `constellation/reference/docs/2026-06-01_hermes/_2nd-handoff/` archive with verified bytes. **Composition with В§8 MCP integration**: the MCP server skeleton (`plugins/constellation/mcp/server.cjs`, v2.5.9 Phase 1) handles the read interface today; chunked attachment transport via MCP is on В§8.6 Phase 2 deferred-list. **Scope discipline**: Constellation.md body augmentation (one new rule in existing В§13.11.3 sub-section). Wire shape unchanged (attachment-object fields are additive; `source` enum extends вҖ” `local_path` was already the de facto value). Seed lib unchanged. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` alignment вҖ” convergent-evolution protocol body augmentation cut.

- **v2.5.8** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **`pre-send-probe.cjs` hardening + env-var override form + promotion to `constellation/reference/runtime/stop-hook/` (cross-environment shared single file, downstream-usable canonical reference).** Stop hook helper script hardening + canonical promotion patch вҖ” `constellation/reference/runtime/stop-hook/pre-send-probe.cjs` + `constellation/reference/runtime/stop-hook/README.md` (formerly `assets/scripts/pre-send-probe.cjs` + `assets/scripts/STOP-HOOK-CONFIG.md`, which were gitignored under `/assets/`; the hardened version is now a public canonical reference utility that downstream Constellation adopters can use directly). Constellation.md body unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Protocol wire unchanged. Driven by the main-upstream Stop hook adoption report (2026-06-01 14:37 UTC, inbox line 22753) which (a) forked the EG script to the main environment's paths (`examples/ws-inbox.jsonl` + `examples/.ws-inbox-cursor`) and (b) identified two hardening gaps that this patch closes back at the EG canonical script. **Hardening 1 вҖ” alive gate (spawn-leak prevention)**: the original `spawnWatcher` spawned a fresh background watcher every turn-close without checking whether one was already running, stacking a new process per turn. The hardened version probes the system for a watcher process matching the watcher-script basename via `pgrep -f` (POSIX) with `tasklist /V /FO CSV` fallback (Windows); if alive вҶ’ skip spawn (no leak); if neither tool is available (bare Windows without git-bash) вҶ’ skip spawn with the "agent-side rearm is canonical" log line (cost-asymmetry argument inverted вҖ” a false-positive skip costs nothing because the agent's turn-end rearm runs anyway, while a false-positive spawn-leak costs a background process per turn). **Hardening 2 вҖ” cursor advance on meaningful in REARM mode (infinite-loop prevention)**: the original `--rearm` mode exited 2 when meaningful inbound was found but did NOT advance the cursor, so the next turn-close re-detected the same meaningful and exit-2'd again, repeating indefinitely. The hardened version ADVANCES the cursor before exit 2 вҖ” the meaningful is logged once (stderr вҶ’ agent's next-turn input surface), subsequent probes start clean. The agent's В§13.16.6 element 1 turn-start probe is the canonical inspection point; the Stop hook's role is LOG + advance, not perpetual block. (Pre-send mode unchanged вҖ” its exit 2 is meant to abort the in-flight emit, and the caller still surfaces + decides + advances cursor after the emit decision.) **env-var override form**: four env vars (`INBOX_PATH` / `CURSOR_FILE_PATH` / `WATCHER_SCRIPT` / pre-existing `LAST_SURFACED_CURSOR`) allow one script to serve EG, main-upstream, Hermes, and any downstream adopter without forking. Defaults preserve EG's existing paths (`<repo>/assets/collab/inbox.log` etc.); adopters set env vars in their Stop hook command (e.g., `INBOX_PATH=./examples/ws-inbox.jsonl CURSOR_FILE_PATH=./examples/.ws-inbox-cursor node "<eg-path>/pre-send-probe.cjs" --rearm`). The main-upstream adoption (14:37 UTC) explicitly named env-var form as the preferred consolidation path; this patch realizes it. STOP-HOOK-CONFIG.md gains a new section documenting the env-var table + the two hardening lessons + the cross-environment cookbook example. **Scope discipline**: helper-script + config-doc augmentation only (both files gitignored under `/assets/`). Constellation.md body unchanged. Seed lib unchanged. Protocol wire unchanged. No agent behavior change for environments that don't set the env vars (defaults preserve v2.5.2 path semantics). Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” convergent-evolution hardening + cross-environment consolidation cut.
- **v2.5.7** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **Superscalar.md v0.3 вҶ’ v0.4 вҖ” В§1 discipline-vs-parallelism meta-note + В§3 nested-repo worktree limitation + В§11 Entry 05 (n=7 вҶ’ n=8) + В§11 Entry 06 (controlled A/B measurement, parallelism held constant).** Minor release on the Superscalar module вҖ” `Superscalar.md` body augmentation, no seed cascade (the master/lite/compact seeds reference `Superscalar.md` by anchor only; v0.4 additions are inside `Superscalar.md` body). Frontmatter `version: v0.3.0 вҶ’ v0.4.0`; status string updated to `В§11 Entry 01-06` + `nested-repo worktree limitation documented (v0.4 В§3)` + `discipline-vs-parallelism meta-note (v0.4 В§1)`. **В§1 meta-note added** (new sub-section after the Concept-mapping table): codifies the discipline-vs-parallelism distinction the policy surface had been implicit about вҖ” *parallelism alone does not produce cross-lane consistency*; three structural gaps no individual lane can close (duplicate findings not deduplicated В· inter-lane contradictions not reconciled В· completeness gaps not surveyed) explain why the В§3 retire stage is a *coordination* mechanism, not a *scheduling* mechanism; the load-bearing anchor is Entry 06's hash-algorithm-contradiction case where both arms surfaced both halves of the contradiction but only Arm B's consistency gate reconciled them. **В§3 nested-repo worktree limitation documented**: new bullet under the worktree-isolation rule вҖ” `git worktree` worktrees the *parent* repo, but when the write target lives inside a **nested *independent* git repo** the parent does not track (a common monorepo-adjacent shape), the per-lane parent worktree does not contain the nested repo, lanes fall back to working in the *shared* nested repo on separate branches вҶ’ **branch isolation, not worktree isolation**. The ROB's architectural-state isolation contract is *not* met; same-file concurrent writes on the nested repo would produce a real WAW hazard despite the `isolation: worktree` request being honored at the parent level. Three mitigations documented: (a) re-worktree the nested repo per lane (harness must detect nested-repo write targets and re-worktree); (b) guarantee file-disjointness + accept branch isolation as effective boundary; (c) harness emits warning when nested-repo write targets are detected so operator picks (a) or (b). Operator is the safety net until harness implements detection. **В§11 Entry 05 updated (n=7 вҶ’ n=8)**: sample size advances to n=8 with case 8 = first worktree write-lane dispatch (2 parallel UI write tasks `isolation: worktree` + 1 read-only research lane). Adds sub-finding В§2b (nested-repo worktree limitation вҖ” see В§3 above) + R3 reflected at В§3 + secondary lesson **presence verification вү  behavioral verification** (MAST FM-2.6 adjacent вҖ” a write lane's structural self-verify passed but a behavioral bug caught only by user testing; the lesson is to instruct lane self-verification to exercise the action вҶ’ state-change path, not just confirm control rendering; `В§7`'s announce-vs-action audit could fold this in as the verify-side dual: announce-vs-action catches the dispatch-side lie, presence-vs-behavioral catches the verify-side lie). All В§5 adoption thresholds remain green at n=8 (case 8's 2 write lanes merged clean). **В§11 Entry 06 added** вҖ” first cleanly-measured *discipline-vs-no-discipline* A/B with parallelism held constant. Source: a downstream backend-audit dogfood (9-dimension payment-backend deep-dive). Both arms parallelised (workflows multi-parallel); the single experimental variable was the orchestration discipline (Arm A naГҜve max-parallel В· Arm B design-freeze вҶ’ consume вҶ’ cross-cut вҶ’ in-order retire + consistency gate + completeness critic). Quantitative readouts: components covered вүҲ (145 vs 144) В· endpoints enumerated +54% (B) В· crossRefs (grounding) +118% (B) В· assumptions (speculation surface) вҲ’40% (B) В· critical/high severity classes equivalent В· dedup B-only (47 cross-dim duplicates merged into 62 unique risk groups) В· consistency gate B-only (one real algorithm-contradiction case resolved вҖ” both arms surfaced both halves, only B's retire stage reconciled them; the load-bearing anchor for the В§1 meta-note) В· completeness critic B-only (11-gap union map) В· S1вҖҰS16 + X1вҖҰX4 cross-reference B-only. Cost: wall-clock 2.65Г— (A faster) В· tokens +8% (B). **Reading**: Arm A is the appropriate choice for fast first-pass reconnaissance; Arm B is the appropriate choice for handover-grade audits + cross-dimension consistency work. The 2.65Г— wall-clock is the cost of *phase serialisation* (freeze вҶ’ consume вҶ’ cross-cut вҶ’ retire), NOT parallel inefficiency вҖ” in-phase parallelism is identical in both arms. Closes the Entry 04 measurement caveat (Entry 04's +127% wall-clock was sequential single-dashboard arm-execution that confounded in-lane sub-split overhead with parallel-latency-hiding benefit; Entry 06 holds parallelism constant and the discipline-vs-no-discipline axis is the clean signal). Entry 04 (in-lane depth at fixed width below cap) + Entry 06 (cross-lane discipline at full width) form the two-axis empirical anchor for В§5 adoption-threshold tuning. **Redaction discipline**: Entry 06 body uses generic identifiers (payment-backend, Java/Spring/MyBatis, "an authentication-hash class contradiction") вҖ” the unredacted measurement bundle remains in the gitignored `assets/reports/` directory; no service names, hosts, repos, or specific identifiers cited in the Superscalar.md body. **Scope**: minor вҖ” Superscalar.md body augmentation only (frontmatter version bump + В§1 meta-note sub-section + В§3 nested-repo bullet + В§11 Entry 05 update + Entry 06 add). - **v2.5.5** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.16.12` new sub-section вҖ” Dashboard render patterns (6 protocol-tier abstractions from cycle_b track-2 raw cp #1).** Constellation patch вҖ” body-only augmentation, no wire-format change, no seed cascade. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.12 вҶ’ v2.3.13`. New В§13.16.12 inserted between В§13.16.11 (KEY-MGMT kind-enum SSoT) and В§13.17 (main-chat structured-choice ban), codifying six dashboard-render patterns as tier-1 SSoT discipline distilled from the cycle_b track-2 reference consolidation (six newer patterns surfaced through a single hub multi-fix commit on 2026-06-01, in addition to the five prior patterns already captured in `constellation/reference/docs/dashboard-render-patterns.md` v2.5.1). **Why a new sub-section, not just an update to `dashboard-render-patterns.md`**: the reference doc is the *render-tier companion* (renderer implementer's manual вҖ” file paths, function names, CSS selectors), while В§13.16.12 is the *protocol-tier abstraction* (the *invariant* a renderer must satisfy regardless of stack). An adopter building a non-vanilla dashboard (React, Vue, Svelte, native) reads В§13.16.12 for the contract and the reference doc for the vanilla-DOM concrete implementation. **The six patterns**: (1) **Collapse indicator: glyph unification + CSS rotation discipline** вҖ” single glyph rotated via `transform: rotate()` (canonical: `textContent="в—Җ"` constant + `.expanded { transform: rotate(-90deg); transition .15s }`), NOT a `в–ҫ / в—Җ` glyph swap pair (which produces 1-2 px visual jitter on every toggle from per-glyph metric mismatch вҖ” observable as "the row twitches"); orthogonal to the `[hidden]` CSS pitfall already captured in `dashboard-render-patterns.md В§3`. (2) **Date-line divider: client-tz day-boundary insertion + sticky positioning** вҖ” day computed from `row.timestamp` (epoch ms, client-side `new Date(epoch)`) NEVER from wire-format ISO string (the wire string carries sender's tz; the divider must reflect the *viewer's* local-day boundary); `position: sticky; top: 0` with sticky-top offset accounting for chat-panel header height (not page header); locale-dependent visual canonical (`мҳӨлҠҳ / м–ҙм ң / YYYY-MM-DD` Korean, `Today / Yesterday / YYYY-MM-DD` English) with `~ ~` decorators via `::before` / `::after` pseudo-elements (NOT literal DOM characters вҖ” keeps the divider text programmatically accessible). Composes with В§13.11.3 rule 3 (server stamps `msg.timestamp = Date.now()` if absent; dashboard uses that epoch). (3) **A2A attachment chip: mime detection + preview + graceful localPath** вҖ” attachment metadata renders as inline chip inside message card body (NOT separate row beneath); mime-icon glyph + filename + size + (preview | download) triggers; preview/download MUST handle both wire shapes: `dataUrl`/`url` present вҶ’ inline modal renders, OR only `localPath` present вҶ’ chip renders gracefully with localPath as informational metadata + "local file, not transported" indicator (NEVER an error or broken-link icon вҖ” targetless / metadata-only attachments are a common emit pattern where the sender means "here's a file I have, name and check it" rather than "here's a file I'm transmitting"). Composes with В§13.13: an `AckProcessed` on an attachment message means the recipient has *surfaced* the metadata, NOT that the recipient has downloaded the localPath resource. (4) **Closed-session connection indicator: present-set based color dot** вҖ” each agent row's connection indicator dot color reflects present membership in live `AgentList` (green `в—Ҹ` present, gray `в—Ҹ` absent вҖ” history-only); updates on every `AgentList` push (В§13.9 handshake group); tooltip surfaces precise connection state with local-tz timestamp (composes with Pattern 2's client-local rendering); composes with В§13.13 вҖ” a `delivered` ack to a gray-dot agent is wire suspect (recipient currently offline), dashboard MAY surface inline warning rather than escalating silently to commitment-tier wait. (5) **Upstream tab re-exposure: present-set sweep, not just delta** вҖ” auto-re-expose logic MUST trigger on every `AgentList` push where the agent is `present`, not only on `absent вҶ’ present` delta. Rationale: long-lived upstream peers stay continuously connected and never produce an `absent вҶ’ present` delta after initial join; if the operator collapses the tab mid-conversation, the tab stays collapsed forever even though the agent is actively producing messages. Discipline: on every `AgentList`, for each present agent, if the tab is currently `hidden`, un-hide it. The sweep is idempotent (re-exposing an already-visible tab is a no-op). Composes with В§13.16.9 v2.5.2 вҖ” `AgentList` is in the handshake group so the watcher correctly does NOT wake on each push, but the dashboard MUST still re-evaluate tab visibility regardless of watcher-wake intent. (6) **Upstream A2A classification (receiver-side): source-set-agnostic detection + text relay fallback** вҖ” receiver-side A2A-intent detection MUST use the negation form of В§13.11.3 rule 2: `source !== "user" && source !== "board" && targetAgentId && targetAgentId !== self`. CRITICALLY, MUST NOT use the positive-set form `source === "agent"` because upstream peer agents emit `source = <their-agentId>` (nonstandard but conformant); the positive-set check silently false-negatives ALL upstream A2A traffic. The negation form is portable across all emitter variants. **Text relay fallback** (second half of pattern): the server's outbound routing (В§13.16.9 routing decision tree) MUST relay target-unspecified TEXT_MESSAGE envelopes to `wsPrimary` (main A2A path) when target-unspecified TEXT_MESSAGE is A2A-intent вҖ” the fail-safe-default-A2A-intent branch (fourth branch of the tree) MUST cover TEXT_MESSAGE name too, not just CUSTOM (otherwise upstream agents emitting raw text without CUSTOM wrap silently drop on server-side normalization). Composes with В§13.11.3 rule 1 (channel `type` normalization handles producer-side defect; this pattern handles router-side defect independently). **Composition with `dashboard-render-patterns.md`**: the reference doc carries concrete render-tier patterns (function names, CSS selectors, file paths in vanilla-DOM master copy); В§13.16.12 carries the protocol-tier discipline. The reference doc's eight sections correspond to В§13.16.12's six patterns plus two prior-cycle patterns (В§2 row interaction + В§4 board render card form, already absorbed at protocol tier through В§13.16.9 + В§13.11.3 in v2.5.1). **Scope discipline**: Constellation.md body augmentation only (one new sub-section ~110 lines). Wire format unchanged (Patterns 1-5 are render-tier behavior; Pattern 6 codifies receiver-side detection rule + routing tree branch that v2.5.1 В§13.16.9 already documented). `dashboard-render-patterns.md` unchanged in v2.5.5 вҖ” continues as renderer's concrete manual. Seed lib unchanged. Hub mirror via A2A PR #3 is a separate follow-up. Per `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` вҖ” meaningful protocol body augmentation cut, not catch-up.

AgentHello.value.role is a hint"` + per-role `onboard_ack` semantics; (8) **operation discipline** not declared вҶ’ `operation_discipline.upstream_peer` 5 rules + `wait_state` 3 rules (BlockerManifest before idle / BlockerNudge by cadence / board decisions panel for human escalation); (10) **termination signals** not declared вҶ’ `termination_signals: [DONE, BLOCKED, NEEDS_HUMAN]`; (11) **deadlock vocabulary** not declared вҶ’ `deadlock_vocabulary: [DeadlockProbe, PreemptRequest, PreemptForce, MediationProposal, MediationAck, EscalationRequest]`;
