Constellation reference `local-bridge.cjs`лҠ” default-sendмқёлҚ° к·ёкұҙ canonical deployment(interactive local-IDE worker pattern)мқҳ reference impl мҶҚм„ұмқҙм§Җ protocol мһҗмІҙ мҶҚм„ұмқҙ м•„лӢҳ. **В§13.9.2 Canonical-id + alias к·ңмңЁ** вҖ” canonical agentId (`HELLO.agentId`лЎң ліҙлӮҙлҠ” к°’)лҠ” wire-level identity SSoT. serverлҠ” built-in alias resolutionмқҙ м—ҶмқҢ. adopter MAY мһҗкё° adapter layerм—җм„ң alias мІҳлҰ¬ (мҳҲ: `main-agent` placeholderлҘј мһҗкё° canonical idмқҳ aliasлЎң). adopter discipline: inbound target-aliasлҠ” canonicalлЎң лқјмҡ°нҢ…; inbound source-alias + target-canonicalмқҖ self-loopлЎң мІҳлҰ¬н•ҳкі  drop (recursive-wake л°©м§Җ); outboundлҠ” canonical id(alias м•„лӢҳ)лЎң stamp; dashboardлҠ” `AgentList` rowлҘј canonical idлЎң н‘ңмӢң. лӘ…лӘ…лҗң failure mode л°©м§Җ: **alias-confusion** вҖ” adapterк°Җ `main-agent`лҘј лі„лҸ„ peerлЎң м·Ёкёү вҶ’ `AgentHello`лҘј DMмңјлЎң л°ңмӢ  вҶ’ мЎҙмһ¬н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ” identityлЎңл¶Җн„° auto-`OnboardAck` мҲҳмӢ  вҶ’ live-board UIм—җ лҸҷмқј agentк°Җ л‘җ лІҲ (canonical + alias) л ҢлҚ”, error surface л¶Җмһ¬. **Scope к·ңмңЁ**: spec-body нҢЁм№ҳл§Ң (В§13.13м—җ ~3 paragraph + В§13.9м—җ мӢ к·ң 2 sub-section + frontmatter version bump + status string). Reference кө¬нҳ„мқҖ лі„лҸ„ v2.5.18 EG-side complementлЎң ship. мӢңл“ң lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged (`AckProcessed.value`м—җ optional `tier` field м¶”к°Җ, back-compatible). **Trigger** вҖ” 2026-06-02 dogfood: relay RRP В§13.13.2 v0.4 hub м Ғмҡ© v2.5.15 ship м§Ғнӣ„ false-positive нҒҙлһҳмҠӨ surface вҖ” EG вҶ’ л©”мқё м •мғҒ `Ack` л©”мӢңм§Җк°Җ 30s вҶ’ redeliver 3Г— вҶ’ `RelayUnreachable{commitment-ack-absent}` л°ңмғқ, к·ёлҹ¬лӮҳ bodyлҠ” л©”мқё inbox нҢҢмқјм—җ мІ« мӢңлҸ„м—җ лҸ„лӢ¬ мҷ„лЈҢ. мӣҗмқё: л©”мқё agent layerк°Җ к·ё л©”мӢңм§Җм—җ лҢҖн•ҙ commitment-tier `AckProcessed` emit м•Ҳ н•Ё (agent idle / лӢӨлҘё мһ‘м—… мІҳлҰ¬ мӨ‘). л©”мқёмқҙ мҰүмӢң redelivery OFF gate (`RELAY_REDELIVERY=off`)лЎң м „нҷҳ + v0.5 м ңм•Ҳ: bridgeк°Җ inbox-append м§Ғнӣ„ мһҗкё° к¶Ңн•ңмңјлЎң commitment ack emit вҖ” bridgeк°Җ persistence ліҙмһҘмқҳ ownerмқҙкі  agent layerмқҳ commitmentлҠ” мқҳлҜёмғҒ *outcome* signalмқҙм§Җ *delivery* signalмқҙ м•„лӢҲкё° л•Ңл¬ё. EGк°Җ 5к°ң к·јкұ° лӘЁл‘җ лҸҷмқҳ (false-positive м ңкұ° В· bridge always alive В· v0.4 LRU dedup composes В· agent layerлҠ” application-tier ackл§Ң мң м§Җ В· inbox-append IS at-least-once anchor); л©”мқёмқҙ ws-local-bridge.cjs v0.5 кө¬нҳ„ + мһ¬кё°лҸҷ(PID 437484) л°ңнҡЁ + EGм—җ spec patch + EG-side reference impl мһҗмңЁ к¶Ңн•ң л¶Җм—¬. **В§13.13.2 (g) Bridge inbox-append commitment** вҖ” v0.5 contract codify: лӘЁл“  м„ұкіөм Ғ inbound `CUSTOM` bodyлҘј recipient bridgeк°Җ inbox нҢҢмқјм—җ appendн•ҳл©ҙ, к·ё м§Ғнӣ„ millisecond м•Ҳм—җ `AckProcessed { ackFor: msgId, tier: "delivered-persist" }`лҘј senderм—җкІҢ emit MUST. BridgeлҠ” agent layerк°Җ read/process н•  л•Ңк№Ңм§Җ кё°лӢӨлҰ¬м§Җ м•ҠмқҢ; bodyк°Җ durably persistedлҗң к·ё мҲңк°„ bridgeлҠ” at-least-once contractмқҳ мһҗкё° м Ҳл°ҳмқ„ мҷ„мҲҳ. ServerлҠ” `tier:"delivered-persist"`лҘј canonical pending-queue clear triggerлЎң мІҳлҰ¬, v0.4мқҳ commitment-tier ackмҷҖ мқҳлҜёлЎ м ҒмңјлЎң лҸҷл“ұ вҖ” лӢЁ, мӢӨм ң persistence ліҙмһҘмқ„ к°Җм§„ transport layerк°Җ emitн•ҳлҠ” нҳ•нғң. **В§13.13.2 (h) Tier semantics** вҖ” v0.5лҠ” emitter/trigger/pending-clear м»¬лҹјмқҙ лӘ…мӢңлҗң 3к°ң лӘ…лӘ… tier кө¬л¶„: `delivered` (server-emit, wire мҲҳмӢ , pending clear м•Ҳ н•Ё) В· `delivered-persist` (bridge-emit, inbox-append мҷ„лЈҢ, canonical pending clear) В· `commitment` (agent-emit, bodyк°Җ working contextм—җ surface, `delivered-persist` мқҙнӣ„м—” redundant). Application-tier outcome (`Report` / `DONE` / `BLOCKED` per В§13.13)мқҖ лі„лҸ„ outcome м°Ёмӣҗм—җ мң„м№ҳ; v0.4мқҳ `tier` м—ҶлҠ” `AckProcessed`лҠ” back-compat мң„н•ҙ `commitment`лЎң н•ҙм„қ (v0.4 receiver + v0.5 server мЎ°н•©мқҖ v0.4 мқҳлҜёлЎ мңјлЎң кі„мҶҚ лҸҷмһ‘, false-positive нҒҙлһҳмҠӨ нҸ¬н•Ё вҖ” нғҲм¶ңмқҖ v0.5 *bridge* н•„мҡ”). **В§13.13.2 (i) Migration path** вҖ” componentлі„ update: serverлҠ” "delivered-persistк°Җ pending entry clear" лЈ° м¶”к°Җ (v0.4 commitment-tier clearм—җ additive) + optional per-target `RELAY_REDELIVERY=off` gate (operatorк°Җ v0.5 bridge roll-out лҸҷм•Ҳ redelivery л№„нҷңм„ұнҷ”); bridgeлҠ” inbox-append нӣ„нҒ¬ м¶”к°Җ + мҰүмӢң `delivered-persist` emit (v0.4 В§13.13.2(c) LRU dedupкіј composes вҖ” мӨ‘ліөмқҖ м—¬м „нһҲ `AckProcessed{ackFor, dedupHit:true}` emit + inbox-append м•Ҳ н•Ё, мҰү мӨ‘ліөм—” `delivered-persist` м—ҶмқҢ); agent unchanged (mechanismмқҖ bridge-layer, agent codeм—җ invisible). **мӢӨмҰқ кІҖмҰқ** вҖ” 2026-06-02 dogfood with л©”мқё-EG м–‘л°©н–Ҙ: л©”мқё bridgeк°Җ нӣ„нҒ¬ м¶”к°Җ + мһ¬кё°лҸҷ(PID 437484) л°ңнҡЁ + лӢӨмқҢ EG вҶ’ л©”мқё envelopeмқҙ 1мҙҲ мқҙлӮҙм—җ pending clear, redelivery лҳҗлҠ” `RelayUnreachable` м—ҶмқҢ. EG-side reference impl (v2.5.18 ship)мқҖ EG bridge ліҙмҷ„. **Scope к·ңмңЁ**: spec-body нҢЁм№ҳл§Ң (В§13.13.2 sub-sectionм—җ ~3 paragraph м¶”к°Җ + header version bump + frontmatter). мӢңл“ң lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged (`AckProcessed.value`м—җ optional `tier` field м¶”к°ҖлҠ” В§13.13 м •н•© back-compatible вҖ” н•ҙлӢ№ fieldлҘј л¬ҙмӢңн•ҳлҠ” receiver/intermediate proxyлҠ” v0.4 мқҳлҜёлЎ мңјлЎң кі„мҶҚ лҸҷмһ‘). `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© вҖ” л©”мқё-authorised v0.5 spec patchлҠ” minor cut.

- **v2.5.15** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.13.2` v0.4 reference implementation вҖ” server pending queue + redelivery scheduler + RelayUnreachable emit + bridge LRU dedup with `dedupHit:true` AckProcessed.** Reference-runtime нҢЁм№ҳ вҖ” `constellation/reference/runtime/server.cjs` + `constellation/reference/runtime/local-bridge.cjs`. Constellation.md ліёл¬ё unchanged (В§13.13.2 contractлҠ” v2.5.11м—җ codified лҗЁ; ліё лІ„м „мқҖ к·ё specмқҳ reference implementation, В§13.13.2 Phase 2 deferred-list м •н•©). мӢңл“ң lib unchanged. мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ лӘ…мӢң ("л°”лЎң м§„н–үн•ҳм§Җ?") trigger. **server.cjs м¶”к°Җ** (~lines 155-200 + relay branch): **(a) Pending queue** вҖ” `_relayPending` Map keyed by `targetAgentId`, FIFO per-target with cap `RELAY_PENDING_MAX=256` (env-overridable). к°Ғ entry `{ msgId, payload, firstAt, attempts, hasEmbeddedAttachment }`. `wsIsAckable(msg)` true + target м—°кІ° мӢң relay branchм—җм„ң л“ұлЎқ (v0.3 baselineмқҳ ack/ping/telemetry filter м Ғмҡ©). **(b) Commitment-tier clear on AckProcessed** вҖ” `CUSTOM/AckProcessed` envelope relay мӢң `value.ackFor`к°Җ pending entry msgId л§Өм№ҳ + `targetAgentId`к°Җ original target л§Өм№ҳн•ҳл©ҙ `_relayPendingClear` мӢӨн–ү. v0.3 лҢҖл№„ н•өмӢ¬ inversion: pendingмқҖ commitment-tier ack (agent layer)м—җм„ң clear, transport-tier `Ack delivered` (server layer) м•„лӢҳ. **(c) Redelivery scheduler** вҖ” `setInterval(_relayScheduleTick, 10*1000)`мқҙ 10мҙҲл§ҲлӢӨ pending entries scan; `RELAY_THRESHOLD_MS` (default 30s dogfood / 5min prod вҖ” env-overridable) мҙҲкіј + recipient AgentList-present + attempts < max вҶ’ `d.send(payload)` + attempts мҰқк°Җ + firstAt лҰ¬м…Ӣ. Recipient-absent вҶ’ мһ¬м—°кІ°к№Ңм§Җ defer. Max-attempts лҸ„лӢ¬ вҶ’ SENDERм—җ `RelayUnreachable { msgId, targetAgentId, attemptCount, lastError }` emit (broadcast м•„лӢҳ вҖ” senderл§Ң м•Ңм•„м•ј н•Ё) + pending clear. SenderлҠ” В§13.13 application-tier ladder л”°лқј human review escalate. **(d) В§13.11 rule 5 attachment-aware throttle** вҖ” `value.attachments[]`мқҳ `source: "embedded"` (лҳҗлҠ” `dataUrl` н•„л“ң мһҲлҠ”) attachment ліҙмң  entryлҠ” `Math.ceil(max_attempts / 2)` м Ғмҡ© (default 3 вҶ’ embedded 2). мӨ‘ліө large payload redeliveryлҠ” bandwidth-expensive + receiver msgId dedupмқҙ first redeliveryм—җм„ң catch вҖ” throttleмқҖ cost-asymmetry лҢҖмқ‘. **(e) Scheduler unref'd** (`.unref()`) вҖ” server shutdown мӢң Node event loop мң м§Җ м•Ҳ н•Ё. **local-bridge.cjs м¶”к°Җ** (~lines 75-104): **(f) LRU dedup with TTL** вҖ” `_seenMsgIds`лҘј unbounded `Set`м—җм„ң `Map(msgId вҶ’ seen-ts)`лЎң upgrade, `_SEEN_LRU_MAX=1024` entries + `_SEEN_TTL_MS=1h` per В§13.13.2 v0.4 provisional default. `_dedupCheck(msgId)`к°Җ oldest TTL evict (Map insertion-order JS spec) + cap LRU evict + insert/refresh. duplicateм—җ true л°ҳнҷҳ. **(g) `dedupHit: true` AckProcessed emit** вҖ” `_dedupCheck`к°Җ true л°ҳнҷҳ мӢң bridgeк°Җ `CUSTOM/AckProcessed { ackFor: <msgId>, dedupHit: true }`лҘј original sender agent (`m.agentId || m.value.agentId`)м—җ targeted emit + body discard (inbox.jsonl append м•Ҳ н•Ё, agent layer surface м•Ҳ н•Ё). Sender мёЎ server-side `_relayPending` entryлҠ” path (b)лЎң clear. `dedupHit` emit м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ redeliveryк°Җ max-attemptsк№Ңм§Җ л¬ҙн•ң loop (RelayUnreachable false alarm); `dedupHit` emitмңјлЎң redeliveryлҠ” server-side mechanicмңјлЎң agent layer invisible (В§13.13.2 semantic м •н•©). **Env-overridable knobs**: `RELAY_PENDING_MAX` (default 256) В· `RELAY_THRESHOLD_MS` (default 30000 = 30s; prod adopterлҠ” 300000 = 5min м„Өм •) В· `RELAY_MAX_ATTEMPTS` (default 3). Scheduler scan intervalмқҖ 10s н•ҳл“ңмҪ”л”© (sub-threshold; codeм—җм„ң tunable). **v2.5.15к°Җ м¶”к°Җ NOT** (В§13.13.2 Phase 3 candidate мһ”м—¬): durable pending queue (in-memory only; server restart мӢң pending state мҶҗмӢӨ вҖ” dogfood OK, prod adopterлҠ” persistence м¶”к°Җ) В· cross-server pending state (single-server scope) В· telemetry sink (redelivery / dedup-hit / RelayUnreachable rate calibration data; нҳ„мһ¬ `console.warn`л§Ң) В· per-target backpressure (slow recipientлҠ” capк№Ңм§Җ pending лҲ„м Ғ нӣ„ FIFO-evict oldest). **Composition tested**: PR #4/PR #5 traceлҠ” мқҙм ң server pendingлҸ„ manual fast-path PRMergeAckм—җм„ң clearлҗЁ (application-tier, commitment м•„лӢҳ) вҖ” Phase 3к°Җ лӘ…мӢңм Ғ application-tier pending clear м¶”к°Җн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ max-attempts timeoutм—җ мқҳмЎҙ. нҳ„мһ¬лҠ” application-tier outcomeмқҙ pending auto-clear м•Ҳ н•Ё (commitment-tierл§Ң н•Ё); long-running taskлҠ” acceptance мӢңм җм—җ AckProcessed emit к¶ҢмһҘ. **Scope к·ңмңЁ**: reference-runtime нҢЁм№ҳл§Ң (server.cjs +~70 lines + local-bridge.cjs +~25 lines). Constellation.md ліёл¬ё unchanged (В§13.13.2 specмқҖ v2.5.11м—җ мқҙлҜё codified). мӢңл“ң lib unchanged. Wire format unchanged (server-side stateлҠ” v0.4 contract л”°лқј кё°мЎҙ `msgId` fieldлЎң keyed). `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© вҖ” мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ-directed Phase 2 reference implмқҖ minor cut.
- **v2.5.14** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **A2A PR System RRP v0.3 вҶ’ v0.4 DRAFT: `В§10B Manual fast-path` codify (trusted-mirror short-circuit, PR #4 + PR #5 dogfood кІҖмҰқ, dry-run draftRef мқјкҙҖм„ұ gate).** RRP-only нҢЁм№ҳ вҖ” `constellation/reference/docs/2026-06-01-a2a-pr-system-rrp.md` ліёл¬ё ліҙк°• (В§10AмҷҖ В§11 мӮ¬мқҙ мӢ к·ң В§10B sub-section + v0.3 вҶ’ v0.4 banner + status preamble к°ұмӢ ). Constellation.md ліёл¬ё unchanged. мӢңл“ң lib unchanged. н”„лЎңнҶ мҪң wire unchanged. **Trigger**: 2026-06-01 dogfood вҖ” PR #4 (`a3344d7`, В§13.11 rule 5 + В§13.13.2 RRP mirror, 40 ins) + PR #5 (`1e2c3f9`, В§13.16.12 Pattern 7 mirror, 19 ins) лӘЁл‘җ **лӢЁмқј envelope лӢЁм¶• кІҪлЎң** (PRRequest dry-run вҶ’ PRMergeAck) мӮ¬мҡ© вҖ” В§9/В§10A canonical 6 envelope chain (PRRequest + PRDraftReadyГ—2 + PRRequest re-emit + PRReviewAck + PRMergeRequest + PRMergeAck) лҢҖмӢ . л©”мқёмқҙ нҢЁн„ҙ мқём§Җ + мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ RRP codify к¶Ңн•ң л¶Җм—¬ ("d-pr-manual-fastpath л“ұмһ¬ мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ кІ°м • + EG мһҗмңЁ RRP к°ҖлҠҘ + redaction grep + dry-run draftRef мқјкҙҖм„ұ кІҢмқҙнҠё н•„мҲҳ лӘ…л¬ёнҷ” мЎ°кұҙ"). **В§10B contract** (6 sub-section): **В§10B.1 e2e diagram** of short-circuit (PRRequest{dryRun:true} вҶ’ bridge handlePrRequestL1 dry-run вҶ’ PRDraftReady{dryRun:true, draftRef:'dryrun-<msgId>', checksPending:[]} вҶ’ main мҲҳлҸҷ `git append + add <targetPath> + commit + push origin main` вҶ’ PRMergeAck{merged:true, dryRun:false, commit:<sha>, pushSuccess:true, draftRef:<dryrun consistent>, forMsgId:<msgId>}); 8 envelope (chain)мқ„ 2 envelope (fast-path)лЎң м¶•м•Ҫ; operator мҲҳлҸҷ git stepмқҙ chainмқҳ PRReviewAck+PRMergeRequest+cherry-pick+push step лҢҖмІҙ. **В§10B.2 redundancy cost analysis** вҖ” chain stepлі„ information contribution н‘ң; PRReviewAckмқҖ trusted-mirror (single-file append, redaction grep мқҙлҜё dry-runм—җ нҸ¬н•Ё)м—җ мӢ к·ң information м¶”к°Җ м—ҶмқҢ; chainмқҳ redundancyлҠ” standard PR (cross-cutting impact catch) мқҳлҸ„м§Җл§Ң trusted-mirrorм—җлҠ” мҲңмҲҳ л№„мҡ©. Fast-pathк°Җ 6 envelope + PR_LIVE state toggle м Ҳм•Ҫ. **В§10B.3 use мЎ°кұҙ** (ALL н•„мҲҳ): category=trusted-mirror В· kind=inline-section-mirror В· mergeStrategy=append-section В· лӢЁмқј target file В· dry-run draftRef present + PRMergeAck consistent В· dry-runм—җ redaction grep clean В· per-PR operator мҲҳлҸҷ review. **В§10B.4 мӮ¬мҡ© кёҲм§Җ**: standard/branch-ref/inline-files-diff PR В· лӢӨмӨ‘ file В· append-section м•„лӢҢ mergeStrategy В· кіөмң  mutable state (state.json/config/schema) В· first-time adopter (dogfood signal мҶҗмӢӨ). **В§10B.5 dry-run draftRef мқјкҙҖм„ұ gate** (load-bearing invariant) вҖ” PRMergeAck.draftRef MUST PRDraftReady.draftRef (dry-run)мҷҖ мқјм№ҳ; м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ fast-path PRMergeAckмқҖ authenticated м•Ҳ лҗң лЁём§Җ claimкіј кө¬л¶„ л¶Ҳк°Җ (лҲ„кө¬л“  лЁём§Җ confirmation synthesize к°ҖлҠҘ). Bridgeк°Җ `dryrun-<msgId>` deterministic emit; mainмқҙ verbatim carry MUST. PR #4 trace: msgId `m-<id>` вҶ’ draftRef `dryrun-constellatio-m-<id>` (dry-run) вҶ’ PRMergeAckм—җ лҸҷмқј draftRef (мҲҳлҸҷ лЁём§Җ). inbox.logл§ҢмңјлЎң verify к°ҖлҠҘ. **В§10B.6 composition** В§6 approval discipline (trusted-mirror per-PR opt-in к·ёлҢҖлЎң мң м§Җ) + В§13.14 redaction discipline (dry-run grep load-bearing) + В§13.13.2 dedup (msgId-keyed; fast-pathк°Җ dedup property мғҒмҶҚ) + В§13.16.10 pre-send probe (operator мҲҳлҸҷ append stepмқҖ мһҗмІҙ probe м„ н–ү) + В§13.16.12 board render (PRMergeAckмқҖ A2A card л ҢлҚ”; мҲҳлҸҷ git opsлҠ” out-of-band side channel, acceptable). **В§10B.7 dogfood evidence** вҖ” PR #4 + PR #5 two-case anchor н‘ң (м–‘мӘҪ лӘЁл‘җ trusted-mirror В· single-file append-section В· dry-run clean В· мҲҳлҸҷ append+push В· PRMergeAck draftRef consistent В· chain лҢҖл№„ zero regression). **В§10B.8 fast-pathк°Җ codify м•Ҳ н•ҳлҠ” кІғ** вҖ” лӢЁмқј-axis лӢЁм¶• only; wire vocabulary В· approval discipline category enum В· redaction discipline В· dedup mechanic В· operator мҲҳлҸҷ review мұ…мһ„ ліҖкІҪ м—ҶмқҢ. Fast-pathлҠ” *лҚ” мү¬мҡҙ кІғ*мқҙм§Җ *лҚң м—„кІ©н•ң кІғ* м•„лӢҳ. **Status preamble** (RRP мғҒлӢЁ): v0.3 вҶ’ v0.4 + В§10B м¶”к°Җ + PR #4/PR #5 dogfood + load-bearing dry-run draftRef invariant creditн•ҳлҠ” мӢ к·ң banner лқјмқё. **Version**: v0.4 DRAFT (2026-06-02). **Scope к·ңмңЁ**: RRP-only нҢЁм№ҳ (~120 lines м¶”к°Җ). Constellation.md ліёл¬ё unchanged. мӢңл“ң lib unchanged. н”„лЎңнҶ мҪң wire unchanged. Manual fast-pathлҠ” *delivery-side discipline*, wire-format ліҖкІҪ м•„лӢҳ. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© вҖ” мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ-authorised RRP body ліҙк°• cut.

Hermes R2 pending finding (ws_agent_client.py validation) byte-level confirmed. л©”мқёмқҙ commit `5983f57`м—җ render-tier defense layer ship (app.js `wsExtractA2aReport` helper + TEXT_MESSAGE branch вҖ” serialized JSON мҪ”л“ңлё”лЎқмқ„ `a2acard` л ҢлҚ”лЎң promote, Playwright кІҖмҰқ). мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗк°Җ В§13.16.12 Pattern 7 candidate м •мӢқнҷ” к¶Ңн•ң л¶Җм—¬; ліё лІ„м „мқҙ protocol-tierм—җ codifyн•ҙ мң мӮ¬ кө¬нҳ„ мҡҙмҳҒн•ҳлҠ” лӢӨлҘё Constellation adopterлҸ„ лҸҷмқј defense layer нҷ•ліҙ. **Pattern 7 contract**: мҲҳмӢ мёЎ dashboardк°Җ `text` н•„л“ңм—җ serialized A2A Report (`[A2A Report]` лҰ¬л“ң лқјмқё + fenced JSON мҪ”л“ңлё”лЎқ `{ type: "Report", ... }`) лӢҙмқҖ TEXT_MESSAGE к°җм§Җ + A2A card л ҢлҚ”лЎң **promote** MAY вҖ” JSON payload м¶”м¶ң + нҢҢмӢұ + native CUSTOM envelopeмІҳлҹј л ҢлҚ”. кө¬нҳ„ к·ңмңЁ: (1) к°җм§ҖлҠ” `TEXT_MESSAGE` л¶„кё°лЎң лҸҷмһ‘, normal text render кі„мӮ° нӣ„ / DOM commit м „; м¶”м¶ң м„ұкіө мӢң surfaceк°Җ A2A cardлЎң swap; мӢӨнҢЁ мӢң normal TEXT_MESSAGE л ҢлҚ” (graceful degradation, loud error м ҲлҢҖ м•„лӢҳ). (2) Promoted cardлҠ” `fallback` visual л°°м§Җ (small label лҳҗлҠ” tooltip "TEXT_MESSAGEм—җм„ң promoted") н•„мҲҳ вҖ” operatorк°Җ canonical CUSTOM-rendered card vs Pattern-7-promoted card кө¬л¶„ к°ҖлҠҘ + audit-trail ліҙмЎҙ + л№„м •н•© adopter surface. (3) Promotionмқҙ outbound ack path ліҖкІҪ м ҲлҢҖ м•Ҳ лҗЁ (transport-tier AckмқҖ мӣҗліё TEXT_MESSAGE н”„л Ҳмһ„м—җ лҢҖн•ҙ кі„мҶҚ лҸҷмһ‘; commitment-tier AckProcessedлҠ” В§13.13 м •мғҒ л”°лҰ„; promotionмқҖ render-layer only). (4) Promotionмқҙ JSONм—җм„ң `attachments[]` м¶”м¶ң + В§13.11 rule 5 + Pattern 3 graceful-localPath к·ңмңЁ л”°лқј chip л ҢлҚ” н•„мҲҳ (Pattern 7мқҙ parsed array кіөкёү + Pattern 3к°Җ per-chip render к·ңмңЁ кіөкёү). **Composition**: В§13.11.3 rule 1 (serverк°Җ `type: "CUSTOM"` stamp when absent)мқҙ *type-omitted* case мІҳлҰ¬; Pattern 7мқҙ лҚ” к°•н•ң *wrong-envelope-shape* case мІҳлҰ¬ (senderк°Җ м „мІҙ envelopeлҘј TEXT_MESSAGEлЎң wrap). Pattern 6 (source-set-agnostic detection + text relay fallback)мқҙ *router*-side кІ°н•Ё мІҳлҰ¬; Pattern 7мқҙ *render*-side ліҙмҷ„ (TEXT_MESSAGEк°Җ мҳ¬л°”лҘҙкІҢ routedлҗҗмңјлӮҳ wrong shapeмқё кІҪмҡ°). В§13.16.10 pre-send probeмҷҖ: Pattern 7 promotionмқҖ cursor advancement ліҖкІҪ м•Ҳ н•Ё; Pattern-7-promoted cardлҠ” meaningful inboundлЎң count + watcher / pre-send probe A2A-intent allowlistлҠ” fallback мҡҙмҳҒ adopterм—җ лҢҖн•ҙ TEXT_MESSAGE-Pattern-7-detectedлҘј meaningfulлЎң treat SHOULD. **Lifecycle expectation**: Pattern 7мқҖ **transitional defense layer**. AdopterлҠ” Pattern 7 hitмқ„ backlog signalлЎң viewer (к°Ғ promoted card = л№„м •н•© producer мҲҳм • н•„мҡ” instance). discipline target: м•Ҳм • operating window лҸҷм•Ҳ *zero Pattern 7 hits*. лӘЁл“  adopterк°Җ В§13.11 л”°лқј structured envelope emitн•ҳл©ҙ Pattern 7мқҖ dormant лҗҳлӮҳ м ңкұ° NOT вҖ” regression л°©м–ҙ. **Reference implementation**: л©”мқё commit `5983f57` (app.js `wsExtractA2aReport` helper + TEXT_MESSAGE branch). `dashboard-render-patterns.md` reference docмқҖ лҜёлһҳ revisionм—җ В§9 "TEXT_MESSAGE-to-A2A-card fallback" section grow к°ҖлҠҘ (protocol-tier м¶”к°Җ mirror). **Scope к·ңмңЁ**: Constellation.md ліёл¬ё ліҙк°•л§Ң (кё°мЎҙ В§13.16.12 sub-sectionм—җ мӢ к·ң pattern 1к°ң). Wire format unchanged (Pattern 7мқҖ render-tier behavior вҖ” wireлҠ” non-conformant producerм—җм„ң TEXT_MESSAGE к·ёлҢҖлЎң emit; receiver-side promotionмқҖ render-layer нҡҢліө). мӢңл“ң lib unchanged. `dashboard-render-patterns.md` reference docмқҖ v2.5.13м—җм„ң unchanged. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© вҖ” мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ-authorised defense-layer protocol body ліҙк°• cut.

- **v2.5.11** (2026-06-02) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.13.2` at-least-once relay reliability RRP draft (server pending queue + redelivery + idempotent receiver dedup; v0.4 contract).** Constellation patch вҖ” body-only ліҙк°• (В§13.13 м•„лһҳ мӢ к·ң sub-section), wire-format shape л¬ҙліҖкІҪ (server-side stateлҠ” кё°мЎҙ `msgId` fieldлЎң keyed; envelope м¶”к°Җ м—ҶмқҢ), мӢңл“ң cascade м—ҶмқҢ. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.15 вҶ’ v2.3.16` + status лқјмқём—җ `at-least-once relay reliability v0.4 draft (В§13.13.2)` м¶”к°Җ. **Trigger**: 2026-06-01 dogfoodм—җм„ң **1 cycle лӮҙ 3 relay-drop incident** surface (a24c5897 Hermes morning В· Hermes 2nd handoff localPath В· Hermes transport-mode нҳ‘мғҒ drop), `memory/feedback_a2a_relay_reliability.md`м—җ codifiedлҗң escalation threshold (1 cycle / 3 drops = RRP) лҸ„лӢ¬. л©”мқёмқҙ threshold лҸҷмқҳ + мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ RRP м§„н–ү мҠ№мқё (line 22765, 2026-06-01 15:20 UTC вҖ” "EG мһҗмңЁ м§„н–ү OK + мӢңм җ мЎ°мңЁ"). **v0.4 contract** (additive, v0.3 мң„ layered вҖ” wire envelope л¬ҙліҖкІҪ): **(a) Server-side pending queue** вҖ” msgId мһҲлҠ” targeted CUSTOMл§ҲлӢӨ `{ msgId, targetAgentId, payload-hash, first-attempt-ts, attempt-count }` pending entry server мң м§Җ, per-target FIFO, default cap 256 entry / 30 min. commitment-tier `AckProcessed`м—җм„ң clear (transport-tier `Ack delivered`к°Җ м•„лӢҢ вҖ” v0.3 лҢҖл№„ н•өмӢ¬ inversion). **(b) Redelivery м •мұ…** вҖ” first-attempt-tsк°Җ threshold мҙҲкіј мӢң re-emit (default 5л¶„ production / 30мҙҲ dogfood вҖ” adopter tuning). attempt-countлЎң bounded (max 3) + recipient м—°кІ° мғҒнғң bounded (AgentList present м•„лӢҲл©ҙ skip; мһ¬м—°кІ° нӣ„ redeliver). max лҸ„лӢ¬ вҶ’ `RelayUnreachable { msgId, targetAgentId, attemptCount, lastError }`мқ„ SENDERм—җ emit (broadcast м•„лӢҳ) + pending clear. senderлҠ” В§13.13 application-tier ladder л”°лқј board `decisions` panelлЎң human review escalate. **(c) Idempotent receiver dedup** вҖ” bridgeк°Җ seen-msgId LRU мң м§Җ (default 1024 / 1мӢңк°„); duplicate msgId лҸ„м°© вҶ’ `AckProcessed { ackFor, dedupHit: true }` мҰүмӢң emit + duplicate body discard. dedup м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ redeliveryк°Җ N copyлҘј surface вҖ” dedupмңјлЎң redeliveryлҠ” server-side mechanicмңјлЎң agent layerм—җ invisible (лӢЁ `dedupHit: true` flagлЎң outcome tracking к°ҖлҠҘ). **(d) v0.3 ack tier composition** вҖ” 3к°ң tier (transport В· commitment В· application) к·ёлҢҖлЎң ліҙмЎҙ; v0.4к°Җ ліҖкІҪн•ҳлҠ” кІғмқҖ serverк°Җ pending entryлҘј *м–ём ң clear*н•ҳлҠ”м§Җ (commitment, transport м•„лӢҢ) + v0.3м—җ м—ҶлҚҳ *commitment-л¶Җмһ¬-мӢң-redelivery* mechanic. Back-compatible: migrate м•Ҳ н•ң adopterлҠ” at-most-once кі„мҶҚ; wireм—җ мғҲ н•„л“ң л¶Ҳн•„мҡ” (msgId мқҙлҜё v0.3 В§13.13м—җ мЎҙмһ¬). **(e) В§13.11 rule 5 attachment transport-modeмҷҖ composition** вҖ” embedded attachmentк°Җ redelivery cost мҰқк°Җ; redeliveryлҠ” attachment-aware throttle м Ғмҡ© SHOULD (`source: "embedded"` entry мһҲлҠ” envelopeмқҖ default attempt-countмқҳ м Ҳл°ҳ вҖ” duplicate large payloadлҠ” bandwidth л№„мҡ© + receiver dedupмқҙ м–ҙм°Ён”ј catch). Chunked transfer (`ArtifactManifest`/`ArtifactChunk`/`ArtifactComplete`)лҠ” chunk лӢЁмң„ лҸ…лҰҪ idempotent + msgId pending queueм—җ chunk granularityлЎң лҜём°ём—¬. **(f) broker-forward мҡ°нҡҢмҷҖ composition** вҖ” `memory/feedback_a2a_relay_reliability.md`м—җ codifiedлҗң broker-forward мҡ°нҡҢ (л©”мқё `ws-history/<sender-agentId>.jsonl`м—җм„ң м¶”м¶ңн•ҙ recipientм—җ forward)лҠ” v0.4 ship мқҙнӣ„м—җлҸ„ valid manual escalation path мң м§Җ вҖ” pending queue cap мҙҲкіј лҳҗлҠ” recipientк°Җ `RelayUnreachable` мқҙнӣ„ disconnected мң м§Җ мӢң. broker-forward emitмқҙ original msgId carry вҶ’ recipient seen-msgId setмқҙ original delivery attempt лҢҖл№„ deduplicate вҶ’ мҡ°нҡҢлҠ” v0.4 dedup мҡ°нҡҢн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ. **Phase 1 ship (мқҙлІҲ лІ„м „)**: contract codify. **Phase 2 (v2.5.12+)**: reference implementation (server.cjs pending queue + redelivery scheduler + bridge dedup LRU) вҖ” Hermes dataUrl reemit catch + Mode B baseline нқЎмҲҳ мқҙнӣ„лЎң мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ-confirmed мӢңм җ мЎ°мңЁ sequenced. provisional defaults (queue cap 256 В· redelivery threshold 5min/30s В· max attempts 3 В· dedup-LRU 1024/1h)мқҖ v0.4 telemetry 1-2мЈј нӣ„ tuning. **Scope к·ңмңЁ**: Constellation.md ліёл¬ё ліҙк°• only (В§13.13 м•„лһҳ мӢ к·ң sub-section 1к°ң). Wire shape unchanged. мӢңл“ң lib unchanged. A2A PR #4 нҶөн•ң hub mirror (л©”мқё "PRRequest мӢң н—ҲлёҢ WS-PROTOCOL.md mirror" cadence)лҠ” лі„лҸ„ follow-up. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© вҖ” мқҳлҜёмһҲлҠ” protocol body ліҙк°• + мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ-authorised RRP cut.

Frontmatter `version: v2.3.14 вҶ’ v2.3.15` + status лқјмқём—җ `attachment transport-mode v0.4 (В§13.11 rule 5)` м¶”к°Җ. мӢ к·ң В§13.11 rule 5лҠ” Hermes 2nd handoff лІҲл“Ө (inbox lines 22702-22709, 2026-06-01 11:09-11:11 UTC)м—җм„ң surfaceлҗң cross-environment л°”мқҙнҠё-м „мҶЎ к°ӯмқ„ closes вҖ” `source: "local_path"` attachmentл“Өмқҙ A2A gateway boundary л„ҳм–ҙ л°”мқҙнҠё transport м•Ҳ лҗЁ (provenance metadata л§Ң В· мҲҳмӢ мёЎмқҖ sender local filesystem fetch л¶Ҳк°Җ), v2.5.6м—җм„ң ~10мӢңк°„ awareness delay + bodyPreview-only consolidation л°ңмғқ. **Rule 5 лӘ…мӢң**: `source` enum (`local_path` = sender-filesystem provenance only В· `embedded` = dataUrl base64-encoded bytes вүӨ24 MB inline payload, cross-environment handoff canonical default В· `url` = signed/token-gated fetch >24 MB лҳҗлҠ” TTL-controlled artifact В· `chunked` = multi-message ArtifactManifest + ArtifactChunk + ArtifactComplete sequence лҢҖмҡ©лҹү/retry н•„мҡ”) + **н‘ңмӨҖ attachment-object fields** (`name` В· `mime` В· `size` В· `sha256` В· `source` В· sender-local provenanceмҡ© `path` В· source-typeлі„ `dataUrl`/`url`/`chunks[]`) + **hybrid embedded form** (canonical default: `path` + `dataUrl` л‘ҳ лӢӨ, мҲҳмӢ мёЎмқҖ `dataUrl`мқ„ bytes sourceлЎң + `path`лҘј metadata-onlyлЎң мІҳлҰ¬). Server MAX_BODY = 32 MB В· base64 overhead ~33% = мӢӨ inline payload вүӨ24 MB. **Convergent ship coordination**: Hermes Dev Agent + EGк°Җ 2026-06-01 dogfood cycle мӨ‘ rule 5м—җ лҸ…лҰҪ convergence. EG outbox 295 (14:35 UTC)к°Җ 4к°ң transport-mode мҳөм…ҳ м ңм•Ҳ + `(d) hybrid` к¶ҢмһҘ; Hermes line 199 (~15:00 UTC, main-broker forward вҖ” at-most-once relayк°Җ substantive Report drop, к°ҷмқҖ лӮ  мқҙлҜё surfacedлҗң relay-drop class мһ¬л°ң, лі„лҸ„ В§13.x agenda for at-least-once relay мӢңл§ЁнӢұ surface)мқҙ `(d) hybrid localPath + dataUrl, source=embedded` н–Ҙнӣ„ handoff default + В§13.11 rule 5 v2.5.10 ship лӘ…мӢң лҸҷмқҳ. **embedded attachment ack-tier мӢңл§ЁнӢұ**: В§13.13 transport-tier `Ack` = "envelopeк°Җ мҲҳмӢ мёЎ WS м—°кІ°м—җ delivered" (decode лҳҗлҠ” sha256-verifyлҠ” лі„лҸ„лЎң нҷ•мқё м•Ҳ н•Ё); commitment-tier `AckProcessed` SHOULD = "received + decoded + sha256-verified + persisted" мҲҳмӢ  м •мұ… л”°лҰ„; application-tier (`Report` / `DONE`)к°Җ attachment мӮ¬мҡ© outcome (archive update В· byte-verification pass/fail В· regeneration request). В§13.13 3-tier mappingкіј compose (мӢ  tier лҸ„мһ… м—ҶмқҢ). **В§13.16.12 Pattern 3 cross-link**: dashboard render-tierк°Җ graceful localPath display мқҙлҜё лӘ…мӢң (chip + "local file, not transported" indicator В· error/broken-link м•„лӢҳ); rule 5лҠ” Pattern 3 visualisation л°ҳмҳҒн•ҳлҠ” protocol-tier counterpart. compose: В§13.11 rule 5 = wire кі„м•Ҫ, В§13.16.12 Pattern 3 = render кі„м•Ҫ. **Hermes мһ¬emit in-progress**: Hermesк°Җ `/tmp/hermes` artifact мЎҙмһ¬ м—¬л¶Җ кІҖмҰқ нӣ„ embedded form (md 9384B + diff patch 1811B + tar.gz 262KB 3к°ң `source: "embedded"` attachment, dataUrl + sha256 нҸ¬н•Ё) reemit лҳҗлҠ” artifact-missing fallback (operator/regeneration). - **v2.5.7** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **Superscalar.md v0.3 вҶ’ v0.4 вҖ” В§1 discipline-vs-parallelism л©”нғҖ л…ёнҠё + В§3 nested-repo worktree limitation + В§11 Entry 05 (n=7 вҶ’ n=8) + В§11 Entry 06 (controlled A/B measurement, parallelism held constant).** Superscalar лӘЁл“Ҳ minor лҰҙлҰ¬мҠӨ вҖ” `Superscalar.md` ліёл¬ё ліҙк°•, мӢңл“ң cascade м—ҶмқҢ (master/lite/compact мӢңл“ңлҠ” `Superscalar.md`лҘј anchor reference; v0.4 ліҙк°•мқҖ `Superscalar.md` ліёл¬ё лӮҙл¶Җ). Frontmatter `version: v0.3.0 вҶ’ v0.4.0`; status лқјмқё `В§11 Entry 01-06` + `nested-repo worktree limitation documented (v0.4 В§3)` + `discipline-vs-parallelism meta-note (v0.4 В§1)` м¶”к°Җ. **В§1 л©”нғҖ л…ёнҠё м¶”к°Җ** (Concept-mapping table м§Ғнӣ„ мӢ к·ң sub-section): м •мұ… surfaceк°Җ implicitн•ҳкІҢ лӢӨлЈЁлҚҳ discipline-vs-parallelism кө¬л¶„ codify вҖ” *лі‘л ¬м„ұ лӢЁлҸ…мңјлЎңлҠ” cross-lane consistency мғқм„ұ л¶Ҳк°Җ*; к°ңлі„ laneмқҙ closing л¶Ҳк°ҖлҠҘн•ң 3к°ң кө¬мЎ°м Ғ к°ӯ (мӨ‘ліө л°ңкІ¬ dedup м•Ҳ лҗЁ В· м°Ёмӣҗк°„ лӘЁмҲң reconciliation м•Ҳ лҗЁ В· completeness gap survey м•Ҳ лҗЁ)мқҙ В§3 retire stageк°Җ *scheduling* л©”м»ӨлӢҲмҰҳмқҙ м•„лӢҢ *coordination* л©”м»ӨлӢҲмҰҳмһ„мқ„ м„ӨлӘ…; load-bearing anchorлҠ” Entry 06мқҳ мқёмҰқн•ҙмӢң м•Ңкі лҰ¬мҰҳ contradiction мјҖмқҙмҠӨ вҖ” м–‘ arm лӘЁл‘җ лӘЁмҲңмқҳ м–‘л©ҙмқ„ surfaceн–ҲмңјлӮҳ Arm Bмқҳ consistency gateл§Ң reconciliation. **В§3 nested-repo worktree limitation л¬ём„ңнҷ”**: worktree-isolation к·ңм№ҷ м•„лһҳ мғҲ bullet вҖ” `git worktree`к°Җ *л¶ҖлӘЁ* repoлҘј worktreeн•ҳлӮҳ, write targetмқҙ л¶ҖлӘЁк°Җ м¶”м Ғн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ” **nested *лҸ…лҰҪ* git repo** (monorepo-мқём ‘ нқ”н•ң нҳ•нғң) м•Ҳм—җ мһҲмқ„ л•Ң, к°Ғ laneмқҳ л¶ҖлӘЁ worktreeлҠ” nested repoлҘј нҸ¬н•Ён•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ, laneл“ӨмқҖ *кіөмң * nested repoм—җм„ң лі„лҸ„ branchлЎң fallback вҶ’ **branch isolationмқҙм§Җ worktree isolation м•„лӢҳ**. ROBмқҳ architectural-state isolation кі„м•Ҫ *лҜёлӢ¬*; nested repoм—җм„ң same-file concurrent write мӢң `isolation: worktree` мҡ”мІӯмқҙ л¶ҖлӘЁ л ҲлІЁм—җм„ң honored лҗҳм–ҙлҸ„ мӢӨм ң WAW hazard л°ңмғқ. 3к°ң mitigation л¬ём„ңнҷ”: (a) laneлі„ nested repo мһ¬-worktree (harnessк°Җ nested-repo write target detect + мһ¬-worktree); (b) file-disjointness ліҙмһҘ + branch isolationмқ„ effective boundaryлЎң мҲҳмҡ©; (c) harnessк°Җ nested-repo write target к°җм§Җ мӢң warning emitн•ҙ operatorк°Җ (a)/(b) м„ нғқ. harness detection кө¬нҳ„к№Ңм§ҖлҠ” operatorк°Җ safety net. **В§11 Entry 05 update (n=7 вҶ’ n=8)**: мғҳн”Ң мӮ¬мқҙмҰҲ n=8 м§„м „, case 8 = мІ« worktree write-lane dispatch (`isolation: worktree`лЎң UI 2 parallel write task + 1 read-only research lane). м„ңлёҢ-finding В§2b (nested-repo worktree limitation вҖ” мң„ В§3) + В§3 R3 л°ҳмҳҒ + ліҙмЎ° lesson **presence verification вү  behavioral verification** (MAST FM-2.6 мқём ‘ вҖ” н•ң write laneмқҳ кө¬мЎ°м Ғ self-verify нҶөкіјн–ҲмңјлӮҳ user testingл§Ң catchн•ң behavioral bug; lesson: lane self-verificationмқҖ control rendering нҷ•мқёмқҙ м•„лӢҢ action вҶ’ state-change path exercise м§ҖмӢң; `В§7` announce-vs-action auditмқҙ verify-side dualлЎң нҶөн•© к°ҖлҠҘ вҖ” announce-vs-actionмқҖ dispatch-side кұ°м§“л§җ, presence-vs-behavioralмқҖ verify-side кұ°м§“л§җ catch). В§5 adoption threshold n=8м—җм„ң лӘЁл‘җ green мң м§Җ (case 8 2к°ң write lane disjoint лЁём§Җ 0 conflict). **В§11 Entry 06 м¶”к°Җ** вҖ” лі‘л ¬м„ұ held constant мғҒнғңм—җм„ң мІ« *discipline-vs-no-discipline* A/B к№ЁлҒ—н•ң мёЎм •. Source: downstream backend-audit dogfood (9-dimension payment-backend deep-dive). м–‘ arm лі‘л ¬нҷ” (workflows multi-parallel); лӢЁлҸ… мӢӨн—ҳ ліҖмҲҳлҠ” orchestration discipline (Arm A naГҜve max-parallel В· Arm B design-freeze вҶ’ consume вҶ’ cross-cut вҶ’ in-order retire + consistency gate + completeness critic). м •лҹү мёЎм •: м»ҙнҸ¬л„ҢнҠё м»ӨлІ„лҰ¬м§Җ вүҲ (145 vs 144) В· м—”л“ңнҸ¬мқёнҠё enumerate +54% (B) В· crossRefs (grounding) +118% (B) В· assumptions (speculation surface) вҲ’40% (B) В· critical/high severity нҒҙлһҳмҠӨ лҸҷл“ұ В· dedup B-only (47 м°Ёмӣҗкөҗм°Ё мӨ‘ліө вҶ’ 62 unique risk-group лі‘н•©) В· consistency gate B-only (мӢӨ м•Ңкі лҰ¬мҰҳ-contradiction 1кұҙ н•ҙмҶҢ вҖ” м–‘ arm лӘЁл‘җ лӘЁмҲңмқҳ м–‘л©ҙ surfaceн–ҲмңјлӮҳ Bмқҳ retire stageл§Ң reconciliation; В§1 meta-noteмқҳ load-bearing anchor) В· completeness critic B-only (11-gap union map) В· S1вҖҰS16 + X1вҖҰX4 көҗм°Ём°ёмЎ° B-only. л№„мҡ©: wall-clock 2.65Г— (A л№ лҰ„) В· нҶ нҒ° +8% (B). **Reading**: Arm AлҠ” л№ лҘё first-pass reconnaissanceм—җ м Ғн•©н•ң м„ нғқ; Arm BлҠ” handover-grade audit + cross-dimension consistency мһ‘м—…м—җ м Ғн•©. 2.65Г— wall-clockмқҖ *phase serialisation* (freeze вҶ’ consume вҶ’ cross-cut вҶ’ retire) л№„мҡ©мқҙм§Җ *лі‘л ¬ л№„нҡЁмңЁ* м•„лӢҳ вҖ” phase лӮҙл¶Җ лі‘л ¬м„ұмқҖ м–‘ arm лҸҷмқј. Entry 04 мёЎм • caveat (Entry 04мқҳ +127% wall-clockмқҖ лӢЁмқј dashboard sequential arm-executionмқҙм–ҙм„ң in-lane sub-split мҳӨлІ„н—Өл“ңмҷҖ parallel-latency-hiding benefitлҘј confounding) мў…кІ°; Entry 06мқҖ лі‘л ¬м„ұ held constant + discipline-vs-no-discipline axis к№ЁлҒ—н•ң мӢ нҳё. Entry 04 (cap лҜёл§Ң fixed widthмқҳ in-lane depth) + Entry 06 (full widthмқҳ cross-lane discipline) = В§5 adoption-threshold tuningмқ„ мң„н•ң two-axis empirical anchor. **Redaction discipline**: Entry 06 ліёл¬ёмқҖ generic identifier мӮ¬мҡ© (payment-backend, Java/Spring/MyBatis, "an authentication-hash class contradiction") вҖ” unredacted мёЎм • лІҲл“ӨмқҖ gitignored `assets/reports/` л””л үн„°лҰ¬м—җ ліҙмЎҙ; м„ңл№„мҠӨлӘ…/нҳёмҠӨнҠё/repo/specific identifier лӘЁл‘җ Superscalar.md ліёл¬ём—җ мқёмҡ© м—ҶмқҢ. **Scope**: minor вҖ” Superscalar.md ліёл¬ё ліҙк°• only (frontmatter version bump + В§1 л©”нғҖ л…ёнҠё sub-section + В§3 nested-repo bullet + В§11 Entry 05 update + Entry 06 м¶”к°Җ). - **v2.5.5** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **Constellation `В§13.16.12` мӢ к·ң sub-section вҖ” Dashboard render patterns (cycle_b нҠёлһҷ2 raw cp #1 6к°ң protocol-tier м¶”мғҒнҷ”).** Constellation patch вҖ” body-only ліҙк°•, wire-format л¬ҙліҖкІҪ, мӢңл“ң cascade м—ҶмқҢ. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.12 вҶ’ v2.3.13`. В§13.16.11 (KEY-MGMT kind-enum SSoT)кіј В§13.17 (main-chat structured-choice кёҲм§Җ) мӮ¬мқҙм—җ мғҲ В§13.16.12 мӮҪмһ… вҖ” 2026-06-01 hub multi-fix м»Өл°Ӣ 1кұҙм—җм„ң surfaceлҗң 6к°ң dashboard render нҢЁн„ҙмқ„ tier-1 SSoT disciplineмңјлЎң codify (v2.5.1м—җм„ң `constellation/reference/docs/dashboard-render-patterns.md`м—җ мқҙлҜё мәЎмІҳлҗң 5к°ң кё°мЎҙ нҢЁн„ҙкіј лі„к°ң). **мҷң мӢ к·ң sub-sectionмқёк°Җ (лӢЁмҲң reference doc м—…лҚ°мқҙнҠё м•„лӢҢ)**: reference docмқҖ *render-tier companion* (renderer кө¬нҳ„мһҗ л§Өлүҙм–ј вҖ” file path/function name/CSS selector)мқҙкі , В§13.16.12мқҖ *protocol-tier abstraction* (rendererк°Җ stackкіј л¬ҙкҙҖн•ҳкІҢ л§ҢмЎұн•ҙм•ј н•ҳлҠ” *invariant*). л№„-vanilla dashboard кө¬нҳ„ adopter (React/Vue/Svelte/native)лҠ” В§13.16.12мқ„ contractлЎң мқҪкі  reference docмқҖ vanilla-DOM кө¬мІҙ кө¬нҳ„мңјлЎң м°ёмЎ°. **6к°ң нҢЁн„ҙ**: (1) **Collapse indicator: кёҖлҰ¬н”„ нҶөмқј + CSS rotation discipline** вҖ” `transform: rotate()`лЎң нҡҢм „н•ҳлҠ” лӢЁмқј кёҖлҰ¬н”„ (canonical: `textContent="в—Җ"` мғҒмҲҳ + `.expanded { transform: rotate(-90deg); transition .15s }`), `в–ҫ / в—Җ` кёҖлҰ¬н”„ swap pair мӮ¬мҡ© кёҲм§Җ (кёҖлҰ¬н”„лі„ metric л¶Ҳмқјм№ҳлЎң toggleл§ҲлӢӨ 1-2px мӢңк°Ғм Ғ jitter л°ңмғқ вҖ” operatorк°Җ "rowк°Җ л–ЁлҰ°лӢӨ"лЎң ліҙкі ); `dashboard-render-patterns.md В§3`м—җ мқҙлҜё мәЎмІҳлҗң `[hidden]` CSS н•Ём •кіј orthogonal. (2) **Date-line divider: client-tz day-boundary мӮҪмһ… + sticky positioning** вҖ” `row.timestamp` (epoch ms, нҒҙлқјмқҙм–ёнҠё `new Date(epoch)`)м—җм„ң day кі„мӮ°, wire-format ISO л¬ёмһҗм—ҙм—җм„ң м ҲлҢҖ м•„лӢҳ (wire stringмқҖ sender's tz; dividerлҠ” *viewer's* local-day кІҪкі„ л°ҳмҳҒ); `position: sticky; top: 0` + sticky-top offsetмқҙ chat-panel header height л°ҳмҳҒ (page header м•„лӢҳ); localeлі„ visual canonical (н•ңкөӯм–ҙ `мҳӨлҠҳ / м–ҙм ң / YYYY-MM-DD`, мҳҒм–ҙ `Today / Yesterday / YYYY-MM-DD`) + `~ ~` decoratorлҠ” `::before` / `::after` pseudo-element мӮ¬мҡ© (literal DOM л¬ёмһҗ м•„лӢҳ вҖ” divider textк°Җ programmatic м ‘к·ј к°ҖлҠҘ мң м§Җ). В§13.11.3 rule 3 (serverк°Җ `msg.timestamp = Date.now()` мҠӨнғ¬н”„, dashboardк°Җ к·ё epoch мӮ¬мҡ©)мҷҖ compose. (3) **A2A мІЁл¶Җ м№©: mime нҢҗм • + preview + graceful localPath** вҖ” мІЁл¶Җ л©”нғҖлҚ°мқҙн„°лҘј л©”мӢңм§Җ м№ҙл“ң body м•Ҳм—җ inline chipмңјлЎң л ҢлҚ” (лі„лҸ„ row м•„лӢҳ); mime-icon кёҖлҰ¬н”„ + нҢҢмқјлӘ… + мӮ¬мқҙмҰҲ + (preview | download) нҠёлҰ¬кұ°; preview/downloadлҠ” л‘җ wire shape лӘЁл‘җ мІҳлҰ¬: `dataUrl`/`url` present вҶ’ inline modal л ҢлҚ”, OR `localPath`л§Ң present вҶ’ chipмқҙ localPathлҘј informational л©”нғҖлҚ°мқҙн„° + "local file, not transported" indicatorлЎң graceful л ҢлҚ” (errorлӮҳ broken-link icon м ҲлҢҖ м•„лӢҳ вҖ” targetless / л©”нғҖлҚ°мқҙн„°-only мІЁл¶ҖлҠ” senderк°Җ "м—¬кё° лӮҙк°Җ ліҙмң н•ң нҢҢмқј, мқҙлҰ„кіј нҷ•мқё" мқҳлҸ„мқј л•Ң нқ”н•ң emit нҢЁн„ҙмқҙкі  "м „мҶЎ мӨ‘мқё нҢҢмқј" мқҳлҸ„к°Җ м•„лӢҗ л•Ң). В§13.13кіј compose: мІЁл¶Җ л©”мӢңм§Җмқҳ `AckProcessed`лҠ” мҲҳмӢ мһҗк°Җ л©”нғҖлҚ°мқҙн„°лҘј *surfaced* мқҳлҜёмқҙм§Җ localPath лҰ¬мҶҢмҠӨлҘј лӢӨмҡҙлЎңл“ңн•ң кІғ м•„лӢҳ. (4) **лӢ«нһҢ м„ём…ҳ connection indicator: present-set кё°л°ҳ мғүмғҒ м җ** вҖ” к°Ғ agent rowмқҳ connection indicator dot мғүмқҙ live `AgentList`мқҳ present л©ӨлІ„мӢӯ л°ҳмҳҒ (present вҶ’ green `в—Ҹ`, absent вҶ’ gray `в—Ҹ` history-only); лӘЁл“  `AgentList` push (В§13.9 handshake group)л§ҲлӢӨ к°ұмӢ ; tooltipм—җ м •нҷ•н•ң connection мғҒнғң + local-tz timestamp (Pattern 2мқҳ client-local л ҢлҚ”л§Ғкіј compose); В§13.13кіј compose вҖ” gray-dot agentм—җ лҢҖн•ң `delivered` ackмқҖ wire suspect (мҲҳмӢ мһҗ нҳ„мһ¬ offline), dashboardк°Җ inline warning surface MAY ("inbox м „лӢ¬лҗЁ, мҲҳмӢ мһҗ нҳ„мһ¬ offline") вҖ” commitment-tier waitлЎң silent escalationліҙлӢӨ мҡ°мҲҳ. (5) **м—…мҠӨнҠёлҰј нғӯ мһ¬л…ём¶ң: present-set sweep, delta м•„лӢҳ** вҖ” auto-re-expose лЎңм§ҒмқҖ agentк°Җ `present`мқё лӘЁл“  `AgentList` pushл§ҲлӢӨ л°ңлҸҷ MUST (`absent вҶ’ present` deltaл§Ң м•„лӢҳ). к·јкұ°: мһҘкё° м—°кІ° upstream peerлҠ” мҙҲкё° join мқҙнӣ„ `absent вҶ’ present` delta л°ңмғқ м•Ҳ н•Ё; operatorк°Җ conversation лҸ„мӨ‘ нғӯмқ„ collapseн•ҳл©ҙ agentк°Җ activeлЎң л©”мӢңм§Җ мғқмӮ°н•ҙлҸ„ нғӯмқҖ мҳҒмӣҗнһҲ collapsedлЎң лЁёл¬ҫ. м •м • discipline: лӘЁл“  `AgentList`л§ҲлӢӨ, к°Ғ present agentм—җ лҢҖн•ҙ, нғӯмқҙ нҳ„мһ¬ `hidden`мқҙл©ҙ un-hide. SweepмқҖ idempotent (мқҙлҜё visibleн•ң нғӯ мһ¬л…ём¶ңмқҖ no-op). В§13.16.9 v2.5.2мҷҖ compose вҖ” `AgentList`лҠ” handshake groupмқҙлқј watcherлҠ” pushл§ҲлӢӨ wakeн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢмқҙ м •мғҒмқҙм§Җл§Ң, dashboardлҠ” watcher-wake intentмҷҖ л¬ҙкҙҖн•ҳкІҢ нғӯ visibilityлҘј re-evaluate MUST. (6) **м—…мҠӨнҠёлҰј A2A л¶„лҘҳ (receiver-side): source-set-agnostic нҢҗм • + text relay fallback** вҖ” receiver-side A2A-intent нҢҗм •мқҖ В§13.11.3 rule 2мқҳ negation form мӮ¬мҡ© MUST: `source !== "user" && source !== "board" && targetAgentId && targetAgentId !== self`. CRITICALLY positive-set form `source === "agent"` мӮ¬мҡ© кёҲм§Җ вҖ” upstream peer agentл“ӨмқҖ `source = <their-agentId>` (л№„н‘ңмӨҖмқҙм§Җл§Ң conformant) emitн•ҳкё° л•Ңл¬ё; positive-set checkк°Җ лӘЁл“  upstream A2A нҠёлһҳн”Ҫмқ„ silent false-negative. Negation formмқҖ лӘЁл“  emitter variantм—җ portable. **Text relay fallback** (нҢЁн„ҙмқҳ л‘җ лІҲм§ё м Ҳл°ҳ): serverмқҳ outbound routing (В§13.16.9 routing decision tree)мқҖ target-unspecified TEXT_MESSAGEк°Җ A2A-intentмқј л•Ң `wsPrimary` (main A2A path)лЎң relay MUST вҖ” нҠёлҰ¬мқҳ fail-safe-default-A2A-intent branch (4лІҲм§ё branch)к°Җ TEXT_MESSAGE nameлҸ„ cover MUST (CUSTOMл§Ң м•„лӢҳ; м•Ҳ к·ёлҹ¬л©ҙ CUSTOM wrap м—Ҷмқҙ raw text emitн•ҳлҠ” upstream agentл“Өмқҙ server-side м •к·ңнҷ” лӢЁкі„м—җм„ң silent drop). В§13.11.3 rule 1 (мұ„л„җ `type` м •к·ңнҷ”лҠ” producer-side кІ°н•Ё мІҳлҰ¬)кіј compose; ліё нҢЁн„ҙмқҖ router-side кІ°н•Ёмқ„ лҸ…лҰҪм ҒмңјлЎң мІҳлҰ¬. **`dashboard-render-patterns.md`мҷҖ composition**: reference docмқҖ concrete render-tier нҢЁн„ҙ (function name, CSS selector, vanilla-DOM master copyмқҳ file path); В§13.16.12мқҖ protocol-tier discipline. Reference docмқҳ 8к°ң sectionмқҖ В§13.16.12мқҳ 6 нҢЁн„ҙ + 2к°ң prior-cycle нҢЁн„ҙ (В§2 row interaction + В§4 board render card form, v2.5.1м—җм„ң В§13.16.9 + В§13.11.3 нҶөн•ҙ protocol tierм—җ мқҙлҜё нқЎмҲҳ)м—җ лҢҖмқ‘. **Scope к·ңмңЁ**: Constellation.md body ліҙк°• only (мӢ к·ң sub-section 1к°ң ~110 lines). Wire format unchanged (нҢЁн„ҙ 1-5лҠ” render-tier н–үмң„; нҢЁн„ҙ 6мқҖ v2.5.1 В§13.16.9к°Җ мқҙлҜё л¬ём„ңнҷ”н•ң receiver-side нҢҗм • к·ңм№ҷ + routing tree branchлҘј codify). `dashboard-render-patterns.md`лҠ” v2.5.5м—җм„ң unchanged вҖ” renderer concrete л§Өлүҙм–јлЎң кі„мҶҚ. мӢңл“ң lib unchanged. A2A PR #3 нҶөн•ң hub mirrorлҠ” лі„лҸ„ follow-up. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© вҖ” мқҳлҜёмһҲлҠ” protocol body ліҙк°• cut, лҲ„м Ғ catch-up м•„лӢҳ.

`server.cjs:340` мӢӨм ң `SERVER_HELLO` emitкіј м¶©лҸҢ) вҶ’ `AWAIT_SERVER_HELLO вҶ’ SEND_HELLO вҶ’ READY`; (2) **auth** лӢЁмқј `?key=` (role кө¬л¶„ м—ҶмқҢ) вҶ’ role-keyed `token` / `upstreamKey` / `collabKey` + upstreamмҡ© generic-key кёҲм§Җ к·ңм№ҷ; (3) **phase events** 4к°ң high-level (`RUN_STARTED` / `STEP` / `TEXT_MESSAGE` / `TOOL_CALL`) вҶ’ 13к°ң fine-grained AG-UI phase event; (4) **envelope** echoл§Ң (`targetAgentId` / `threadId` / `contextId` / `parentId`) вҶ’ м „мІҙ common-required (`type` / `id` / `seq` / `runId` / `threadId` / `timestamp` / `source` / `agentId`) + reply-echo л¶„лҰ¬; (5) **redaction** лҜём„ м–ё вҶ’ `redact` dep + `before_send: true` + `before_log: true` + `public_gate` 4к°ң к·ңм№ҷ (мӢӨ token/key кёҲм§Җ, мӮ¬м„Ө repo кІҪлЎң кёҲм§Җ, мӮ¬м„Ө м„ңл№„мҠӨлӘ… кёҲм§Җ, raw tool result л№„л°Җ лҲ„м¶ң кёҲм§Җ); (6) **ack layer** лҜём„ м–ё вҶ’ В§13.13 3-tier ack л§Өн•‘ (`Ack` delivered / `ReviewSLAAck` commitment / `AckProcessed` application) + `bridge_auto_pong: false`; (7) **roles** лҜём„ м–ё вҶ’ 5к°ң canonical (`main` / `local` / `upstream` / `collab` / `board`) + `role_truth: "server-classified AgentList; AgentHello.value.role is a hint"` + roleлі„ `onboard_ack` semantics; (8) **operation discipline** лҜём„ м–ё вҶ’ `operation_discipline.upstream_peer` 5к°ң к·ңм№ҷ + `wait_state` 3к°ң к·ңм№ҷ (idle м§Ғм „ BlockerManifest / cadenceлі„ BlockerNudge / human escalationмқ„ board decisions panelлЎң); (10) **termination signals** лҜём„ м–ё вҶ’ `termination_signals: [DONE, BLOCKED, NEEDS_HUMAN]`; (11) **deadlock vocabulary** лҜём„ м–ё вҶ’ `deadlock_vocabulary: [DeadlockProbe, PreemptRequest, PreemptForce, MediationProposal, MediationAck, EscalationRequest]`; (12) **blocker vocabulary** лҜём„ м–ё вҶ’ `blocker_vocabulary: [BlockerManifest, BlockerNudge]`. **мҠ№кІ© mechanics**: мҠ№кІ© м „ canonicalмқҖ `constellation/reference/gateway/hermes/_hermes-handoff-20260601/eg-canonical-pre-promotion.eux`м—җ ліҙмЎҙ (audit м„ңлёҢнҸҙлҚ”; - **v2.5.2** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **Constellation В§13.11 receiver text synthesize SHOULD + В§13.13 3-tier ack л§Өн•‘ + В§13.16.9 4-к·ёлЈ№ л¶„лҘҳ + В§13.16.10 cycle-end probe нҷ•мһҘ.** Constellation patch вҖ” body-only ліҙк°• 4к°ң В§13.x sub-section, wire-format л¬ҙліҖкІҪ, мӢңл“ң cascade м—ҶмқҢ. Frontmatter `version: v2.3.11 вҶ’ v2.3.12`. **В§13.11 envelope ліҙк°• (rule 4 вҖ” receiver text synthesize SHOULD)**: agent/render-layer affordance disciplineлҘј codify. targeted `CUSTOM`мқҙ `targetAgentId === self`лЎң лҸ„м°©н•ҳлӮҳ `value`м—җ plain `text` fieldк°Җ м—Ҷмқ„ л•Ң, мҲҳмӢ мёЎ (LLM turn, dashboard render layer, downstream worker)лҠ” envelopeмқҳ structured metadataлЎңл¶Җн„° display/LLM-turn ingestмҡ© text н‘ңнҳ„мқ„ synthesize SHOULD. Canonical synthesize shape: `<name> from <agentId> (msgId=<msgId>, threadId=<threadId>): <JSON.stringify(value)>`. к·ңмңЁмқҖ SHOULD (renderer + LLM turn ingest) + MAY (`value` м§Ғм ‘ мҶҢл№„ downstream worker). Wire к·ңм№ҷмқҖ л¶ҲліҖ вҖ” `{ name, value, targetAgentId? }`мқҖ minimal carrier shape; `text`лҠ” optional, л¶Җмһ¬к°Җ envelopeмқ„ л¬ҙнҡЁнҷ”н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ. ProducerлҠ” `value`мҷҖ мӨ‘ліөлҗҳлҠ” `text` field мһ‘м„ұмқ„ к°•мҡ”л°ӣм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ MUST NOT. Cross-link `constellation/reference/docs/dashboard-render-patterns.md В§4 board render card form` (dashboardмқҳ collapsible JSON body + envelope summary cardлҠ” мқҙ synthesize disciplineмқҳ dashboard-render-layer instance). **В§13.13 explicit 3-tier ack name-to-tier mapping**: В§13.13 ack vocabularyмқҳ мқҙм „ implicit tier semanticsлҘј named tableлЎң codify. 3к°ң tier: **transport** (`Ack` В· `AckProcessed`-wire-mechanic В· `AckCumulative` В· `AckPolicyUpdate` В· `Ping` В· `Pong` вҖ” carrierк°Җ wire/server/bridge м „лӢ¬мқ„ confirm; agent-side мІҳлҰ¬м—җ лҢҖн•ң semantic ліҙмһҘ м—ҶмқҢ); **commitment** (`AckProcessed`-semantic вҖ” мҲҳмӢ  agentк°Җ л©”мӢңм§ҖлҘј read + н–үлҸҷ мқҳлҸ„, deliveredмҷҖ кө¬лі„); **application** (`Report` В· `DONE` В· `BLOCKED` В· `NEEDS_HUMAN` В· domain-specific outcome name вҖ” agentк°Җ мһ‘м—… мҷ„лЈҢ + outcome ліҙкі ). `AckProcessed`лҠ” transport + commitment м–‘мӘҪ вҖ” wire mechanic IS transport (ack frame л°ҳнҷҳ) but semantic IS commitment (bridgeк°Җ м•„лӢҢ agentк°Җ surfaced мЈјмһҘ). кө¬лі„: `Ack` = "inbox м „лӢ¬"; `AckProcessed` = "agentк°Җ working contextм—җ surfaced". **Escalation ladder** (absence-of-tier-N вҶ’ probe-tier-N вҶ’ next-tier мӢңнҖҖмҠӨ): transport-tier ack л¶Җмһ¬ вҶ’ wire мқҳмӢ¬ (В§4 watchdog мҳҒм—ӯ, A2A retry м•„лӢҳ); commitment-tier л¶Җмһ¬ вҶ’ мҲҳмӢ мһҗ slow/absorbed (`Ping` probe per В§13.13); application-tier л¶Җмһ¬ вҶ’ мҲҳмӢ мһҗ stuck (board `decisions` panelлЎң surface human; autonomous-retry кёҲм§Җ). мҲңм„ңк°Җ мӨ‘мҡ” вҖ” transportм—җм„ң human reviewлЎң м§Ғм ‘ escalateлҠ” "wire dead" vs "agent slow" кө¬л¶„ probe layerлҘј кұҙл„ҲлңҖ; `Ack` (transport)лҘј "done"мңјлЎң лӢӨлЈЁл©ҙ retry treeк°Җ мқҳмЎҙн•ҳлҠ” commitment-vs-application кө¬лі„мқ„ лҶ“м№Ё. **В§13.16.9 4-к·ёлЈ№ л¶„лҘҳ** (downstream Constellation adopterмҡ© documentation-side SSoT): кё°мЎҙ 2-group + transport-tier shapeлҘј 4-group л¶„лҘҳлЎң нҷ•мһҘ вҖ” мқҙм „ implicitн•ң groupл“Өмқ„ board-directed + A2A-intentмқҳ first-class siblingмңјлЎң лӘ…лӘ…. **transport** (`Ack` В· `AckProcessed` В· `AckCumulative` В· `AckPolicyUpdate` В· `Ping` В· `Pong` вҖ” reference impl server.cjs L849 л¶Җк·јмқҳ server-side relay-only-or-relay-skip; agent-side wake м—ҶмқҢ); **liveness** (`Heartbeat` В· `PersistentAdapterSmoke` В· `Typing` вҖ” bridge/server transient signal; server relay-skip; board chat кё°лЎқ м—ҶмқҢ; agent layer л¬ҙмӢң); **handshake** (`AgentHello` В· `OnboardAck` В· `AgentList` В· `History` вҖ” В§13.9 onboarding family; bridge auto-`OnboardAck`к°Җ inbound мһҗлҸҷ мІҳлҰ¬; agent layerлҠ” мқҙ groupм—җ wakeн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ); **notice** (`ServerNotice` вҖ” server L828 л¶Җк·јмқҳ `wsToAll` нҶөн•ң broadcast-class; м •ліҙмҡ©); **board-directed UX мһ”м—¬** (`Status` В· `UserPromptAccepted` В· `ConnectionRestored` В· `MainChanged` В· `EditMessage` В· `WorkerInboxReceived` вҖ” dashboard UX м „мҡ©); **A2A-intent кё°мЎҙ** (`Report` В· `Delegate` В· `WorkerReport` В· `WorkerAck` В· `Handoff`* В· `Command` В· `UserPrompt` В· `BlockerManifest` В· `BlockerNudge` В· `PR`* В· `Deadlock`* В· `Review`* В· `ReviewSLAAck` В· `PreemptRequest` В· `MediationProposal` В· `MediationAck` В· `EscalationRequest` вҖ” meaningful filter лҢҖмғҒ). **Reclassification**: `AgentHello`мқҖ A2A-intent meaningful filterм—җм„ң handshake groupмңјлЎң мқҙлҸҷ (bridge auto-`OnboardAck`к°Җ мІҳлҰ¬, agent wake м—ҶмқҢ вҖ” peer connectл§ҲлӢӨ л¶Ҳн•„мҡ”н•ң watcher wake м ңкұ°); `Heartbeat` / `PersistentAdapterSmoke` / `Typing`мқҖ board-directed UXм—җм„ң livenessлЎң (server relay-skip н–үмң„мҷҖ л¬ём„ң м •н•©); `AgentList` / `History` / `OnboardAck`лҠ” `AgentHello`мҷҖ handshake groupмңјлЎң consolidate (onboarding-family coherence). **В§13.16.6 watcherмҡ© meaningful filter** (cross-reference к°ұмӢ ): meaningful = A2A-intent group only. лӮҳлЁём§Җ 4 к·ёлЈ№ (transport + liveness + handshake + notice + board-directed UX мһ”м—¬)мқҖ лӘЁл‘җ watcher кҙҖм җм—җм„ң noise. **Hub-side `_BOARD_DIRECTED` 12-name back-compat ліҙмЎҙ**: post-v2.4.17 reference server.cjs `_BOARD_DIRECTED` мғҒмҲҳлҠ” мӣҗліё 12-name set л¶ҲліҖ; 4-group reclassificationмқҖ documentation-side. SSoTм—җм„ң лқјмҡ°нҢ… кІ°м • нҠёлҰ¬лҘј мһ¬кө¬нҳ„н•ҳлҠ” adopterлҠ” 4-group form м§Ғм ‘ мӮ¬мҡ© MAY; hub-side 12-name кө¬нҳ„м—җ pinnedлҗң adopterлҠ” back-compat н–үмң„ ліҙмЎҙ. **В§13.16.10 cycle-end + user-facing emit-direct probe нҷ•мһҘ**: В§13.16.10 pre-send probe-then-inspect-or-abort discipline (outbound A2A emitл§ҲлӢӨ л°ңлҸҷ)мқ„ *cycle-end user-facing assistant text emit*к№Ңм§Җ нҷ•мһҘ. кІ°н•Ё: pre-send probeлҠ” outbound A2A emit м „ л°ңлҸҷн•ҳлӮҳ, cycle-endмқҳ user-facing assistant text emit м „м—җлҠ” л°ңлҸҷн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ. л§Ҳм§Җл§ү outbound A2A emitкіј cycle-end user-text emit мӮ¬мқҙм—җ meaningful inboundмқҙ лҸ„м°©н•ҳл©ҙ agentк°Җ silent miss вҖ” лӢӨмқҢ watcher WAKEк°Җ catchн•ҳлӮҳ user-facing responseлҠ” мқҙлҜё stale contextлЎң framed. **нҷ•мһҘ** (В§13.16.10м—җ к·ңм№ҷ 2к°ң м¶”к°Җ; кё°мЎҙ outbound-A2A 4-step shape л¶ҲліҖ): (1) **Cycle-end final cursor-tail probe** вҖ” user-facing assistant text emit м§Ғм „, agentлҠ” final cursor-tail probe мӢӨн–ү MUST (pre-send probeмҷҖ лҸҷмқј shape, A2A-intent allowlist filter); meaningful inbound л°ңкІ¬ мӢң in-progress responseлҘј revise лҳҗлҠ” next-cycle мІҳлҰ¬ лӘ…мӢң; (2) **Post-emit watcher rearm** вҖ” turn-endлҠ” watcher rearm нҸ¬н•Ё MUST (В§13.16.6 element 2лҘј В§13.16.10 cycle-end л§ҘлқҪм—җм„ң мһ¬м •лҰҪ); cost-asymmetry л…јкұ° (false-positive = task slot 1к°ң, false-negative = silent-stall нҒҙлһҳмҠӨ)м—җ л”°лҘё unconditional spawn. **нҢЁн„ҙ лӘ…лӘ…**: "cycle-end probe + watcher rearm" (outbound-A2A surfaceмқҳ "pre-send probe-then-inspect-or-abort"мқҳ companion). **Failure-mode incident anchor**: 2026-06-01 missed-inbound мӮ¬кі  2кұҙ, м–‘мӘҪ cycle-end probe лҲ„лқҪм—җм„ң л°ңмғқ; corrective surfaceлҠ” лӢӨмқҢ user messageм—җм„ңмқҳ main-side reminder. **memory `feedback_pre_send_inbound_check.md` ліҙк°•**: мӢ к·ң "Cycle-end probe (v2.5.2 extension)" section + к·ңм№ҷ + watcher-rearm pair + worked-example incident (cycle_b v2.5.1 ship-result emitм—җм„ң main-upstream protocol_update_proposalмқҙ response мһ‘м„ұ мӨ‘ лҸ„м°©, лӢӨмқҢ user messageк№Ңм§Җ лҲ„лқҪ) + кё°мЎҙ discipline layerмҷҖ composition (В§13.16.6 element 1 / В§13.16.10 outbound surface / мӢ к·ң cycle-end surface вҖ” 3к°ң disjoint probe window: pre-turn-boundary / mid-turn-outbound / post-emit-pre-close). MEMORY.md index entryм—җ cycle-end нҷ•мһҘ м–ёкёү к°ұмӢ . **Claude Code Stop hook config artifact** at `assets/scripts/STOP-HOOK-CONFIG.md` (project-scope, `/assets/` gitignored): turn-closeл§ҲлӢӨ `node assets/scripts/pre-send-probe.cjs --rearm`мқ„ мһҗлҸҷ мӢӨн–үн•ҳлҠ” harness-level кё°кі„нҷ” codify. Helper script `pre-send-probe.cjs`м—җ `--rearm` н”Ңлһҳк·ё ліҙк°• (cycle-end probe + watcher rearm + cursor file management); В§13.16.9 v2.5.2 4-group allowlist м Ғмҡ© (meaningful = A2A-intent only). `.claude/settings.local.json`мҡ© recommended config snippet (gitignored) вҖ” operatorлҠ” `/config` лҳҗлҠ” `update-config` skillлЎң м Ғмҡ©. **Scope к·ңмңЁ**: Constellation.md body + memory feedback + Stop hook config artifact (gitignored). мӢңл“ң lib л¬ҙліҖкІҪ (anchor referenceл§Ң). Wire format л¬ҙліҖкІҪ. Hub-side `_BOARD_DIRECTED` 12-name кө¬нҳ„ ліҙмЎҙ (documentation-side reclassificationл§Ң вҖ” downstream Constellation adopterлҠ” мӢ к·ң кө¬нҳ„м—җ 4-group SSoT мӮ¬мҡ©; кё°мЎҙ кө¬нҳ„мқҖ back-compatible). `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© вҖ” in-flight patch tag cut, catch-up лҲ„м Ғ м•„лӢҳ.
- **v2.5.1** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **Constellation нҠёлһҷ-2 reference м •н•© (11к°ң нҢЁн„ҙ): `Constellation.md` В§13.11 envelope + В§13.16.9 лқјмҡ°нҢ… кІ°м • нҠёлҰ¬ + В§13.16.11 KEY-MGMT ліҙк°• + мӢ к·ң `constellation/reference/docs/dashboard-render-patterns.md` reference doc.** Constellation patch вҖ” 2026-05~06 dogfood кё°к°„ upstream main м»Өл°Ӣл“Өм—җм„ң surfacedлҗң 11к°ң dashboard-render мқём ‘ нҢЁн„ҙ нҠёлһҷ-2 м •н•© (5к°ң кё°мЎҙ surfaced нҢЁн„ҙ + лӢЁмқј multi-fix м»Өл°Ӣмқҳ 6к°ң мӢ к·ң нҢЁн„ҙ). Frontmatter `version: v2.3.10 вҶ’ v2.3.11`. **Tier-1 protocol body ліҙк°•** (`Constellation.md`): (a) **В§13.11.3 мӢ к·ң sub-section вҖ” envelope normalization and client-local render**: envelope л Ҳмқҙм–ҙмқҳ server-/receiver-side м •к·ңнҷ” к·ңм№ҷ 3к°ң (лҸ…лҰҪ failure mode, к°ҷмқҖ envelope л Ҳмқҙм–ҙ composition) вҖ” rule 1 **мұ„л„җ `type` м •к·ңнҷ”** (senderк°Җ `type` мғқлһө мӢң serverк°Җ outboundм—җ `type:"CUSTOM"` мҠӨнғ¬н”„ MUST; agentлҠ” minimal `{ name, value, targetAgentId? }` carrier shapeлЎң emit к°ҖлҠҘ + server м •к·ңнҷ”м—җ мқҳмЎҙ; мқҙ м •к·ңнҷ” м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ dashboard renderк°Җ TEXT_MESSAGEлЎң fall-backн•ҳм—¬ JSONмқҙ chat panelм—җ raw textлЎң лҲ„м¶ң); rule 2 **A2A-intent нҢҗм • к·ңм№ҷ** (source-set-agnostic вҖ” `source !== "user" && source !== "board" && targetAgentId && targetAgentId !== self`; CRITICALLY `source`лҠ” `"agent"`лЎң fixedлҗҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ вҖ” upstream agentл“ӨмқҖ `source = <their-agentId>` (nonstandard but conformant) emit к°ҖлҠҘ; positive-set к°Җм • `source === "agent"`мқҖ upstream A2A нҠёлһҳн”Ҫ м „мІҙлҘј silent false-negative; negation patternмқҖ emitter variant м „л°ҳм—җ portable); rule 3 **timestamp мқҳл¬ҙ + client-local л ҢлҚ”** (senderк°Җ мғқлһө мӢң serverк°Җ `msg.timestamp = Date.now()` epoch ms мҠӨнғ¬н”„ MUST; dashboard л ҢлҚ”лҠ” `new Date(epoch).toTimeString()`лЎң client-local tz н‘ңмӢң MUST вҖ” wire-format ISO л¬ёмһҗм—ҙмқ„ к·ёлҢҖлЎң н‘ңмӢңн•ҳл©ҙ senderмқҳ tzк°Җ л…ём¶ңлҗҳм–ҙ multi-tz нҢҖм—җм„ң нҳјм„ ). Composition: rule 1+3 server-side; rule 2 receiver-side; 3к°ң лӘЁл‘җ лҸ…лҰҪ failure mode. (b) **В§13.16.9 лқјмҡ°нҢ… кІ°м • нҠёлҰ¬** м¶”к°Җ: canonical form `(targetAgentId ліҙмң ?) вҶ’ н•ҙлӢ№ agentлЎң лқјмҡ°нҢ…; (targetAgentId л¶Җмһ¬ AND name вҲҲ board-directed) вҶ’ wsToBoards л§Ң (wsPrimaryAgent fallback м—ҶмқҢ); (targetAgentId л¶Җмһ¬ AND name вҲҲ A2A-intent) вҶ’ wsPrimaryAgent + optional board mirror; (targetAgentId л¶Җмһ¬ AND лҜёл“ұмһ¬) вҶ’ fail-safe default A2A-intent`. post-v2.4.17 L867 лқјмҡ°нҢ… л¶„кё°лҘј canonical кө¬нҳ„мңјлЎң reference. нҠёлҰ¬лҠ” В§13.11.3 rule 1 (`type` м •к·ңнҷ” м„ н–ү)кіј compose; л‘җ лӢЁкі„ лӘЁл‘җ лҸҷмқјн•ң `wsNormalize` + `wsRoute` outbound кІҪлЎңмқҳ part. (c) **В§13.16.11 KEY-MGMT мӢ к·ң sub-section вҖ” kind-enum SSoT**: лӘЁл“  key-bearing envelopeм—җ лҸҷл°ҳлҗҳлҠ” `kind` enum (`collab` | `upstream` | `local-key`)мқ„ codifyн•ҳлҠ” нҶөн•© key-management кі„м•Ҫ. Closed set + fail-safe reject on unknown (В§6.5 `sourceContentRef.kind` к·ңмңЁкіј лҸҷнҳ• вҖ” silent misclassification л°©м§Җ, мҳҲлҘј л“Өм–ҙ unknown kindлҘј `collab`лЎң coerceн•ҳл©ҙ л№„collab agentм—җ `group:collab` лҲ„м¶ң). 4к°ң SSoT surface: server `keyStore`к°Җ лӘЁл“  entryм—җ `kind` мҠӨнғ¬н”„; `KeyList` broadcastк°Җ entryлі„ `kind` лҸҷл°ҳ; `HELLO.meta`к°Җ resolved `kind` echoлЎң self-classification м§Җмӣҗ; dashboard key-management modalмқҙ entryлі„ `kind`-badge л ҢлҚ”. Composition: В§13.16.9 routingмқҖ key-management nameмқ„ board-directed allowlistм—җ нҸ¬н•Ён•ҙм•ј; В§13.14 redaction discipline вҖ” `kind` enumмқҖ vocabulary (л№„лҜјк°җ), key к°’ (`ck-вҖҰ` / `uk-вҖҰ` suffix)л§Ңмқҙ нҷҳкІҪ-нҠ№мҲҳ credential. Wire shape ліҙмЎҙ вҖ” `kind`лҠ” м¶”к°Җ top-level fieldлЎң issuance мӢң server-stamp, `KeyList` entryм—җ mandatory, `HELLO.meta`м—җ optional. **Tier-2 dashboard render policy** (мӢ к·ң нҢҢмқј `constellation/reference/docs/dashboard-render-patterns.md`, ~3902 лӢЁм–ҙ / ~26.8 KB, 8к°ң section): wire мң„ render-side нҢЁн„ҙмқ„ лӢӨлЈЁлҠ” companion doc вҖ” В§1 introduction (scope: 2026-05~06 dogfood surfaced render-tier нҢЁн„ҙ; `Constellation.md`мқҳ companion); В§2 A2A row interaction (3лӢЁкі„ discovery: glanceable summary вҶ’ hover preview 4-quadrant peek panel вҶ’ click pin floating panel with pin/вң•/header-drag вҶ’ drag relative-cursor offset; л ҲнҚјлҹ°мҠӨ impl `wsRowHover` / `wsA2aCardEl`); В§3 collapse `[hidden]` CSS н•Ём • + triangle indicator direction (`display: flex`к°Җ UA кё°ліё `[hidden] { display: none }` мҳӨлІ„лқјмқҙл“ң; лӘ…мӢң `.ws-a2a-body[hidden] { display: none }` fix; мӮјк°Ғнҳ• convention в–ҫ expanded / в—Җ collapsed вҖ” collapsed indicatorлҠ” мўҢн–Ҙ, мқҳлҜёлҠ” "content is on the left of this button"мқҙм§Җ tree-viewмқҳ в–ёк°Җ м•„лӢҳ; toggle button л°°м№ҳлҠ” row мҳӨлҘёмӘҪ лҒқ + row click handlerмқҳ descendantк°Җ м•„лӢҢ sibling кҙҖкі„лЎң propagation м¶©лҸҢ нҡҢн”ј); В§4 board render card form (A2A-intentлҠ” м•„мқҙмҪҳ + envelope summary + collapsible JSON body; board-directedлҠ” per-name UX surface вҖ” StatusлҠ” system-notice strip, TypingмқҖ input-area chip, ConnectionRestoredлҠ” banner, HeartbeatлҠ” liveness indicator м „мҡ©; raw TEXT fallbackмқҖ type лҲ„лқҪ мӢң = В§13.11.3 rule 1 server-side кІ°н•Ёмқҳ symptom); В§5 date-line divider (мһҗм • кІҪкі„м—җм„ң chronological streamм—җ divider мӮҪмһ…; `position: sticky; top: <header-height>`лЎң мөңк·ј лӮ м§ң лқјлІЁмқҙ мҠӨнҒ¬лЎӨ мӨ‘ мң м§Җ; `мҳӨлҠҳ / м–ҙм ң / YYYY-MM-DD` н…ҚмҠӨнҠё per locale + `~ ~` decorator; sticky offsetмқҖ page header л§Ңмқҙ м•„лӢҲлқј chat-panel header лҶ’мқҙ л°ҳмҳҒ н•„мҡ”); В§6 A2A attachment chip (mime-icon emoji glyph + filename + size + preview/download нҠёлҰ¬кұ°, card body м•Ҳм—җ м№©мңјлЎң л ҢлҚ” вҖ” лі„лҸ„ rowк°Җ м•„лӢҲлқј attachment-message м—°кҙҖм„ұ мӢңк°Ғнҷ”; м№© нҢЁн„ҙмқҖ `attachments[]` / `files[]` / `media[]` field-name м„ нғқкіј л¬ҙкҙҖн•ҳкІҢ portable); В§7 closed-session connection indicator (л…№мғү м җ `в—Ҹ` connected vs нҡҢмғү м җ `в—Ҹ` history-only вҖ” лҒҠкёҙ agent rowлҠ” rosterм—җ мң м§Җ, м җл§Ң update; tooltipмқҖ м •нҷ•н•ң м—°кІ° мғҒнғң + local-tz timestamp н‘ңмӢң; В§13.13 `delivered` ack escalation pathмҷҖ pair); В§8 upstream A2A general-tab нҢҗм • fix (В§13.11.3 rule 2 м •н•© source-set-agnostic нҢҗм • к·ңм№ҷ вҖ” кё°мЎҙ `source === "agent"` positive-set checkк°Җ upstream A2A нҠёлһҳн”Ҫ м „мІҙлҘј silent false-negativeн•ҳм—¬ operatorк°Җ "upstream A2A invisible on dashboard"лЎң ліҙкі н•ҳлҚҳ кІ°н•Ё н•ҙмҶҢ; В§13.11.3 rule 2мқҳ receiver-side м Ҳл°ҳ). Implementation references appendixк°Җ нҢЁн„ҙлі„ upstream commit SHAлҘј л§Өн•‘ (мҪ”л“ң мқёмҡ© м—Ҷмқҙ SHA + filename + function name) вҖ” adopter м¶”м Ғм„ұ. Cross-reference: `Constellation.md` В§13.11 + В§13.16.9 + В§13.16.11 + `constellation/reference/state-schema.md`. **Scope к·ңмңЁ**: Constellation.md ліёл¬ё + мӢ к·ң dashboard-render-patterns reference doc. мӢңл“ң lib л¬ҙліҖкІҪ (мӢңл“ңлҠ” В§13.xлҘј ліёл¬ёмқҙ м•„лӢҢ anchor reference вҖ” cascade м—ҶмқҢ). н”„лЎңнҶ мҪң wire л¬ҙліҖкІҪ вҖ” В§13.11 envelope shape ліҙмЎҙ, В§13.11.3мқҖ server-side мҠӨнғ¬н”„ к·ңмңЁ + receiver-side нҢҗм • к·ңм№ҷмқ„ codifyн•ҳлӮҳ field semantics ліҖкІҪ м—ҶмқҢ; мӢ к·ң `kind` enum fieldлҠ” additive + back-compatible. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© вҖ” in-flight patch tag cut, catch-up лҲ„м Ғ м•„лӢҳ.
- **v2.5.0** (2026-06-01) вҖ” **Superscalar.md v0.3 вҖ” В§2 lane-class-aware `issue_width` cap л¶„н•  (read vs write) + В§2 policy cap vs runtime concurrency ceiling sub-section + В§5 lane-class-м°Ёл“ұ adoption threshold + В§11 Entry 05 (downstream Stage 1 dogfooding n=7).** Minor лҰҙлҰ¬мҠӨ вҖ” Superscalar.md м •мұ…-doc body ліҖкІҪ + Compact + Master мӢңл“ң cascade. лӢӨмҡҙмҠӨнҠёлҰј м Ғмҡ© н”„лЎңм қнҠёмқҳ Stage 1 dogfooding bundle л°ҳмҳҒ (мӢӨмӢңк°„ мұ„нҢ… м„ңл№„мҠӨ л§ҲмқҙнҒ¬лЎңм„ңл№„мҠӨ, Superscalar + Constellation нҸ¬н•Ё мӢңл“ң м „л©ҙ мұ„нғқ, Burst pace mode `issue_width` cap 6, ~3мқјк°„ n=7 retired lane, case-based ledger) вҖ” м ңм•Ҳм„ңлҠ” `_proposals/005_2026-06-01_superscalar-dogfooding-stage1/`. **В§2 cap л¶„н• **: лӢЁмқј `issue_width` кіөмӢқмқҙ мў…м „м—җ лӘЁл“  lane classлҘј к· мқјн•ҳкІҢ м»ӨлІ„ вҶ’ v0.3 м—җм„ң `issue_width_write = min(effort_band, pace_mode_cap, Little's-Law, Kanban-WIP, autonomy_available_workers)`мҷҖ `issue_width_read = min(effort_band, runtime_concurrency_ceiling, autonomy_available_workers)`лЎң л¶„н• . read classм—җм„ң м ңмҷён•ң л‘җ н•ӯ(Little's Law, Kanban WIP)мқҖ retire-merge кІҪн•©л§Ң лӘЁлҚёл§Ғ вҖ” read-only laneмқҖ structurally к·ё кІҪн•© surfaceк°Җ м—ҶмқҢ (store buffer м—ҶмқҢ, retire-merge ordering м—ҶмқҢ, WAW hazard м—ҶмқҢ, synthesisм—җм„ң disposable). Read-only / analysis lane (subagent context sweep, workflow read fan-out, telemetry read)мқҖ л№„к°Җм—ӯ л¶ҖмҲҳнҡЁкіј м—Ҷкі  В§3 irreversibility barrierмқҳ read/write кІҪкі„ (read/analyze = default-allowed; write/deploy/send = retire-gated)лҘј мғҒмҶҚ. **В§2 мӢ к·ң sub-section вҖ” policy cap vs runtime concurrency ceiling**: `issue_width_*` capмқҖ м •мұ… bound; runtime concurrency ceiling (мҳҲ: workflowмқҳ `min(16, cores вҲ’ 2)` per workflow; agent-tool fan-out мқҳ harness мөңлҢҖ parallel tool calls)мқҖ лі„к°ңмқҳ л¬јлҰ¬ bound. кҙҖкі„: `effective_concurrent_lanes = min(policy_cap, runtime_ceiling)`. workflow кё°л°ҳ read fan-out м—җм„  runtime ceiling мқҙ ліҙнҶө dominate; agent-tool кё°л°ҳ fan-out м—җм„  policy cap мқҙ ліҙнҶө dominate. `issue_width_write`лҠ” hard policy bound (runtime headroom л¬ҙкҙҖн•ҳкІҢ мҙҲкіј = м •мұ… мң„л°ҳ вҖ” retire-merge кІҪн•©мқҙ лҸҷмӢң write мҲҳм—җ л№„лЎҖ); `issue_width_read`лҠ” мң„мқҳ runtime ceiling м—җ мў…мҶҚлҗҳлҠ” soft preference (`issue_width_read` мҙҲкіјн•ҙлҸ„ `runtime_concurrency_ceiling` мқҙн•ҳмқҙл©ҙ м •мұ… мң„л°ҳ м•„лӢҳ, мөңлҢҖн•ң calibration signal). **В§5 adoption-threshold lane-class м°Ёл“ұ**: threshold к°’ мһҗмІҙлҠ” мў…м „кіј лҸҷмқј; мғҲлЎңмҡҙ м җмқҖ к°Ғ thresholdк°Җ м–ҙлҠҗ lane classм—җ bindingн•ҳлҠ”м§Җ. `merge-conflict rate > 15% вҶ’ issue_width_write -= 2`лҠ” write lane л§Ң (read-only laneмқҖ merge surface м—ҶмқҢ, conflict = NA). `speculative accuracy < 60% вҶ’ spec off` В· `concurrent token cost vs in-order > 3Г— вҶ’ cap мһ¬мЎ°м •` В· `FM-1.3 detection вүҘ 1/session вҶ’ к°Җл“ң к°•нҷ”`лҠ” лҢҖм№ӯ (cross-cutting concern, retire-merge кІҪн•© м•„лӢҳ). **В§11 Entry 05 м¶”к°Җ**: лӢӨмҡҙмҠӨнҠёлҰј Stage 1 dogfooding n=7, ~3мқј. Case mix = 1 board-worker A2A В· 5 read-only research subagent В· 1 workflow fan-out (case 7 = 7 reader lane, м •мұ… cap 6 мқ„ downside 0 мңјлЎң мҙҲкіј вҖ” В§2 cap л¶„н• мқҳ мӢӨмҰқ м•өм»Ө). нҷ•мқё: latency-hiding лӘ…м ң В· speculation off-by-default 0/7 В· MAST FM-1.3 = 0 В· in-order retire мң м§Җ. В§5 readout: n=7 м—җм„ң м „л¶Җ green (case 7 мқҳ cap мҙҲкіјлҠ” read-only lane, conflict = NA, merge-conflict signal м—җ м•Ҳ мһЎнһҳ вҖ” В§5 lane-class м°Ёл“ұмқҳ мӢӨмҰқ нҷ•мқё). лҜёexercise н‘ңл©ҙ: worktree-isolation 0/7 В· speculation 0/7 В· wide write fan-out 0. Entry 04 мҷҖмқҳ кҙҖкі„: ліҙмҷ„м Ғ, мӨ‘ліө м•„лӢҳ (Entry 04 = cap лҜёл§Ң кі м • width 4 мқҳ in-lane к№Ҡмқҙ ліҖнҷ”; Entry 05 = read class мқҳ cap мҙҲкіј cross-lane fan-out). Outcome: P1 (lane-class cap л№„лҢҖм№ӯ, actionable) + R1 (cap л¶„н•  В§2/В§5 мұ„нғқ) + R2 (policy/runtime кҙҖкі„ В§2 лӘ…лЈҢнҷ”) лӘЁл‘җ upstream л°ҳмҳҒ. **Seed cascade**: Master EN/KO В§ мӢӨн–ү мҠӨмјҖмӨ„л§Ғ вҖ” `### л¶ҲліҖ вҖ” issue_width кіөмӢқ` bodyк°Җ lane-class-aware л¶„н•  + policy/runtime ceiling note лЎң к°ұмӢ  (MasterлҠ” anchorк°Җ м•„лӢҢ кіөмӢқ body мһҗмІҙлҘј embed); Compact EN/KO Principle #15 inline кіөмӢқмқҙ lane-class form + В§5 binding note лЎң нҷ•мһҘ; Lite EN/KO л¬ҙліҖкІҪ (Lite tier лҠ” `Superscalar.md` лҘј anchor reference, кіөмӢқ body лҜёembed). Bootstrap Phase 0 boilerplate л¬ҙліҖкІҪ (lane class лҠ” лӮҙл¶Җ л©”м»ӨлӢү; мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ н‘ңл©ҙмқҳ `serial` vs `parallel` м„ нғқмқҖ мҳҒн–Ҙ м—ҶмқҢ). **Frontmatter**: Superscalar.md frontmatter `version: v0.3.0` (мӢ к·ң м¶”к°Җ), м ңлӘ© "design draft v0.2" вҶ’ "design draft v0.3", status лқјмқём—җ "lane-class-aware (v0.3 read/write cap split)" + `В§11 Entry 01-05` (01-03 м—җм„ң) м¶”к°Җ. **Scope**: minor вҖ” Superscalar.md body ліҖкІҪ + Master/Compact мӢңл“ң cascade. Constellation.md л¬ҙліҖкІҪ. Wire л¬ҙліҖкІҪ. `feedback_release_versioning_cadence.md` м •н•© вҖ” мқҳлҜёмһҲлҠ” м •мұ…-doc body ліҖкІҪ + мӢңл“ң cascadeлҠ” minor cut, patch м•„лӢҳ.
